# CHANGELOG

> Archive: detailed historical entries from 2026-06-05 and earlier moved to `docs/CHANGELOG.archive-2026-06-05-details-and-earlier.md`; entries from 2026-05-19 and earlier remain in `docs/CHANGELOG.archive-2026-05-19-and-earlier.md`.
> Keep this file short: current entries plus concise recent summaries only.

## 2026-07-17

- **ADR (ADR-152 opened; documentation only).** Founder approved the bounded
  Browser Script SDK and Durable Job Wait/Notify architecture on clean baseline
  `8fd0159593112b9679fa782b53ea525d786da6a3`. Scope is narrow
  profile-backed Script `snapshot`/`act` through the existing local browser
  bridge and universal model-visible `await` (`wait`/durable `notify`) for
  canonical media/document jobs. It explicitly excludes a general-purpose SDK,
  Document SDK, headless fallback, durable Script-execution restart, and managed
  credential scope. This entry records no implementation, migration, deploy,
  or live-validation claim.

- **ADR (ADR-156 founder-approved global mode-aware tool observation
  windows).** Added a concise follow-through ADR without reopening closed
  ADR-143. `tool-observation-policy.ts` now assigns all tools by mode with no
  name/type exceptions: in-turn newest 3 full / next 3 compact; cross-turn
  unchanged newest 1 full / next 4 compact; older masked; errors never
  bare-mask. Projection metrics count effective tiers. Removed the abandoned
  `41fa0a69` Script-specific compact reducer, 2,000-character cap, truncated-JSON
  representation, and obsolete tests; Script now follows the same global
  windows and ordinary generic reducers as every tool. Seven-exchange boundary
  tests prove in-turn `masked, compact×3, full×3`, cross-turn
  `masked×2, compact×4, full`, and error upgrade. The live-shaped
  `script → todo_write → skill` list is naturally all full in-turn and remains
  `compact/compact/full` cross-turn without special casing. Existing compactors,
  canonical non-mutation, the earlier `job` + `paths` discriminator, and
  cross-turn policy remain unchanged. Dynamic/token-threshold compaction is out
  of scope. Updated real turn-execution fixtures for six-exchange and parallel
  three-tool in-turn windows. Focused tests, full runtime suite, complete repo
  typecheck, repo/runtime lint, format, and diff checks passed; independent
  allowed-model audit returned CLEAN with no P0/P1/P2 findings. Commit
  `43f653b4` passed CI/image publish and deployed 2/2 on exact runtime image;
  strict live `skill → todo_write → script → todo_write → skill` reproduced all
  four exact Script output fields while logs ended at
  `fullCount=3 compactCount=2 maskedCount=0`. Approved-account Admin Scripts UI
  acceptance also passed. ADR-151 and ADR-156 closed 2026-07-17.

- **ADR (ADR-151 live P1 repair: Script result file-extraction
  discriminator).** Fixed the post-tool receipt seam where
  `TurnExecutionService.isSandboxToolPayload` treated every
  `executionMode: "sandbox"` payload as a produced-file
  `RuntimeSandboxToolResult`. A completed `script.execute` result intentionally
  carries exact structured `output` and a `jobId`, not a `job`; the old
  discriminator therefore returned `undefined` from `resolveProducedFileJob`
  and crashed on `job.files` during receipt construction. The produced-file
  discriminator now requires the sandbox result's structural `job` + `paths`
  fields, leaving ordinary `exec`/`shell` sandbox job file projection unchanged.
  Focused runtime coverage exercises
  the actual post-tool `extractProducedFileHandles` seam for both a completed
  Script result (no throw/no handles) and an ordinary shell job (its file
  handle remains); it is included in the existing real isolated runtime
  package gate. Focused test, full runtime suite, runtime typecheck/lint,
  repo-wide format check, and `git diff --check` passed; independent
  allowed-model runtime audit returned CLEAN with no P0/P1/P2 findings.
  ADR-151 remains Accepted/Open pending redeploy and founder live acceptance.

- **ADR (ADR-151 P1 repair: runtime scriptRef materialization fail-closed
  gap; independently audited CLEAN locally).** Fixed
  `skill-scenario-runtime-normalization.ts`'s hand-rolled `scriptRef`
  normalizer, which silently canonicalized a malformed persisted non-null
  `scriptRef` (or a malformed nested `inputMapping`/source entry) to
  `null`/dropped-entry before `script-ref-materialization.ts` saw it, letting
  bundle materialization succeed as if the reference were explicitly absent.
  The runtime normalization pass now carries the raw persisted value through
  unparsed; `script-ref-materialization.ts` is the canonical materialization
  boundary and parses every non-null `scriptRef` with the exact same
  exported `parseScriptRef` the Admin authoring path uses (no duplicated
  parsing logic), throwing the existing typed `ScriptRefMaterializationError`
  (same `script_ref_materialization_unresolvable` code, now with an optional
  `detail` message) for any malformed shape before any database round-trip.
  Explicit null/absent `scriptRef` is unchanged. Added 5 new focused tests to
  `script-ref-materialization.test.ts` covering malformed top-level refs,
  non-object refs, malformed nested mapping sources/shapes, and explicit
  null/absent success, all through the production
  `normalizeSkillScenarioSteps` → `materializeScenarioStepScriptRefs` path.
  Targeted re-audit and affected post-repair gates passed; the final local
  ADR-151 audit/repository gate is satisfied.

- **ADR (ADR-151 Admin UI + MCP authoring implemented and independently
  audited CLEAN locally; accepted/open, deploy pending).** Added a Roles-style Admin Scripts
  page (`apps/web/app/admin/scripts/page.tsx`) with localized metadata
  create/edit, draft/published/archived status, draft ScriptVersion authoring
  (code/manifest/schemas/limits) with save/validate/publish, immutable
  published-version history, typed conflict/error surfacing for every
  documented Admin API error code, and a Skill-bindings section that
  full-replaces one Skill's ordered Script list via the existing
  `GET`/`PUT /admin/skills/{skillId}/scripts` routes (no invented
  runtime-smoke route). Added a Scripts entry to the Admin navigation. Added
  nine thin typed MCP tools to `@persai/admin-mcp`
  (`script_list`/`script_get`/`script_upsert`/`script_version_upsert`/
  `script_version_validate`/`script_publish`/`script_archive`/
  `skill_scripts_list`/`skill_scripts_replace`), all resolving immutable
  `scriptKey` like the existing `role_*` tools and auto-resolving draft
  `versionId`/`expectedRevision`; extended the existing `skill_scenario_upsert`
  step schema with an optional `scriptRef` field mirroring the API's discriminated
  input-source union exactly. No contracts regenerated (no source contract
  changed). A parent-audit repair makes Validate and Publish first PATCH the
  exact visible editor payload, then validate/publish the returned version
  identity (Publish uses the returned revision), preserving typed conflict
  reload behavior. The first independent Admin/MCP audit returned DIRTY; its
  follow-up corrections add Ajv Draft-2020-12/size/depth parity plus exact
  manifest and Scenario mapping bounds to MCP and local UI validation, and
  generation guards that ignore stale Script-version and Skill-binding
  responses. A second independent audit found remaining mutation ownership,
  explicit version-loading, trim normalization, and Script metadata validation
  gaps. The final correction pass guards every Script/version/binding mutation
  by selection generation + identity, prevents stale requests from owning
  loading/saving flags, hides version authoring until the current load settles,
  mirrors all canonical metadata bounds, and forwards MCP-normalized strings
  exactly (while preserving untrimmed code/entry-command fields). The final P2
  repair disables the complete checkbox/reorder/save binding control group for
  the whole full-replace request and applies the server-returned order before
  re-enabling it. 18 web tests and 22 MCP tests are green; touched-package
  typecheck/lint and formatting are green. The final targeted allowed-model
  re-audit returned CLEAN; authenticated Admin UI, real Cursor MCP, and
  model-driven warm-session chat smoke remain deploy/live acceptance gates.

- **ADR (ADR-151 Scenario + Runtime implementation independently audited
  CLEAN locally).** Made authored Script refs
  fail materialization closed; removed optional runtime `scriptRef`
  compatibility; added sandbox admission/execution reauthorization, canonical
  executable hash and input/output schema enforcement, preflight winner
  exclusion, trap plus proven control-plane cleanup/pod retirement, safe Script
  cwd, per-invocation bounded result framing, exact `LimitedCollector` retention,
  reserved-name/prototype/extra-field rejection, and local-ref/allOf dynamic
  schema projection. The final runtime audit repair adds production
  `SCRIPT_TOOL_CODE` dispatch coverage for live todo/Skill reauthorization,
  proves `refreshVolatilePrefix` adds/removes `script`, requires sandbox-enabled
  dynamic projection, wires the ADR-149 abort suite into the real runtime gate,
  and pins ordinary-stdout redirection plus precise direct-stdout overflow
  diagnostics. Wired ADR-151 runtime and sandbox tests into real package gates;
  focused and actual API/runtime/sandbox suites are green. The final
  allowed-model runtime/security re-audit returned CLEAN; Kubernetes policy/
  cleanup, true concurrent PostgreSQL admission, and a deployed model-driven
  warm-session Script turn remain live-only acceptance probes.

## 2026-07-16

- **ADR (ADR-151 Scenario + Runtime block implemented locally; accepted/open,
  audit pending).** On top of the audited Domain + Admin API checkpoint
  (`cbeaccb4`): async Scenario-step `scriptRef` materialization pins the
  exact `{scriptId, scriptVersionId, versionNumber, contentHash}` through the
  owning Skill's live `SkillScript` link (one lookup per distinct
  `scriptKey`; admitted bundles keep their old pin after a republish;
  the 2026-07-17 repair makes archived/unlinked authored refs fail closed);
  a new internal `apps/api` read
  boundary re-authorizes that exact pin live (Script status, SkillScript
  link, hash/key match) without ever returning code; the provider-facing
  `script` tool (`{action:"execute", input:object}`,
  `SandboxJob.toolCode`/internal operation exactly `script.execute`) is
  dynamically projected only when the active Scenario step carries a
  materialized `scriptRef` and is re-resolved (not just re-projected)
  immediately before dispatch via one shared current-step resolver; runtime
  input mapping supports `literal` / `current_user_message` / `tool_input`
  sources validated against the published input/output JSON Schemas with
  strict Ajv 8.18 Draft 2020-12, plus a server-derived
  `scriptInvocationKey`. `SandboxService.submitJob` admits `script.execute`
  atomically by `(assistantId, scriptInvocationKey)` before ordinary
  preflight/backlog consumption, resolving `P2002` races to a
  winner/loser replay and a version/input mismatch to a stable
  `idempotency_conflict`; execution runs through the exact existing warm
  session sandbox with code/input/output staged transiently under `/tmp`
  (never persisted to workspace GCS/Files/snapshots) and reserved
  `PERSAI_SCRIPT_*` env vars. Also repaired a pre-existing `LimitedCollector`
  unbounded-retention bug in `ExecPodBridgeService` (shared correctness, not
  new policy). Focused tests added across apps/api, apps/runtime, and
  apps/sandbox; full local test suites, lint, typecheck, and format:check are
  green. No Helm/image change. Runtime/security audit, Admin UI, MCP,
  deployment, and live acceptance remain pending — do not claim them.
- **ADR (ADR-151 reusable Scripts core; accepted/open).** Founder-approved
  documentation checkpoint on clean baseline `36947f75`: platform-global
  Script + immutable published ScriptVersion; ordered full-replace Skill links;
  bounded active-Scenario-step `scriptRef` and synchronous `script.execute`
  using the existing warm session sandbox; existing `SandboxJob` idempotent
  admission/replay instead of `ScriptRun`; Admin/MCP authoring only. ADR-147
  Role-only effective Skills and ADR-150 warm-pod-only install layer remain
  unchanged. Tool SDK/browser/async and managed secrets are ADR-152/153 scope.
  **Domain + Admin API implemented locally:** Prisma models/migration and DB
  immutability/current-version guards; strict manifest/JSON Schema validation;
  canonical publish hash and optimistic draft revisions; ordered Skill links
  with assistant invalidation; bounded Scenario refs; explicit Admin auth,
  OpenAPI/Orval contracts, and focused tests. Parent-audit corrections add
  publisher `RESTRICT`, authenticated ordered-binding `GET` parity, stable-409
  Scenario reference protection on link removal, strict persisted-ref
  corruption handling, and DB-side JSONB reference existence checks.
  Independent audit proved the full 189-migration history and Script constraints
  on isolated PostgreSQL 16 with zero target-schema drift; generated-index and
  Ajv dependency tails are closed. Runtime execution, Admin UI, MCP, deployment,
  and live acceptance remain pending.
- **Fix (context-meter opaque gray + scissors flush-right; pushed `3367c9e8`).** Expanded meter `color-mix` with `--border` (alpha) let the title bleed through → solid `bg-surface-hover`. Scissors/hover sat left of the right end-cap because a capped text slot left slack on the right; text is uncapped `flex-1` so the scissors button stays flush on the right circle.
- **UX (narrow-chat mode/plan circles + context-meter polish; pushed `43c8b672`).** Mode and plan collapsed chips switch circle↔pill by chat column `@container` at 500px (not viewport `md`). Context meter: ring reveal spins once after collapse; busy ring immediate while compacting; site-pages publish test drains async before teardown.
- **Fix (desktop bridge drops mid-work; local).** `ERR_CONNECTION_RESET` on `browser-bridge/ws` during active use: dial-failure budget no longer counts post-OPEN flaps; API device-token TTL 15m → 4h with matching client safe-age; maintainer renews live credentials after 3h. Rebuild/reload Chrome extension after api+web deploy.
- **UX (context meter expands in-place to pill; local).** Clicking the title-pill context circle no longer opens a dropdown modal. The gray disk expands right over the chat title (title stays put), keeps `%` centered in the left cap, shows «Контекст чата» + link «Сжать сейчас», and a right-cap scissors control with plan-trash hover. Compact collapses back to the circle with a spinner until compaction finishes.
- **Closure (ADR-149 + ADR-150; founder-accepted).** ADR-149 durable Stop / turn deadlines / live activity / orphans closed — do not reopen. ADR-150 ephemeral session install layer closed after push `314ee37a` — session `.local` / `.npm-global` / `node_modules` remain warm-pod only; do not reopen.
- **Change (ADR-150 + meter; pushed `314ee37a`, handoff `25a910eb`).** Session install-layer cutover (session-anchored pull/push excludes, path-aware purge, Files/grep/glob/mirror/hydrate/upsert/`files.write` gates, curated `httpx`). Context meter / compaction pressure uses first `main_turn` `inputTokens`; meter stroke 2px.

## 2026-07-15

- **Fix (ADR-150 session-scoped mount exclude/purge; local).** Pull/push no longer basename-exclude/purge install trees across the whole `/workspace` mount (that wrongly hit assistant `shared/.../node_modules`). Mount tar excludes are anchored under `assistants/*/sessions/*/` (or the exact session when known); post-pull purge uses `isSessionInstallLayerPath`. Session-root snapshot basename excludes unchanged; overlay also purges destination leftovers.
- **Fix (ADR-150 audit repair; local).** Closed P0 session-snapshot/`pullWorkspace` persistence bypass (tar excludes + restore/pull purge), nested `node_modules` directory matcher, grep/glob read-filters, `files.write` refuse-before-GCS, and produced-file mirror defense-in-depth. Install-layer remains warm-pod only.
- **Fix (context meter / compaction pressure uses first main_turn inputTokens; local).** Session `currentTokens` no longer takes the final tool-loop `usage.totalTokens` (inflates with every tool result in the in-turn prompt). Prefers `inputTokens` from the first `main_turn` usageAccounting entry so the meter and post-turn auto-compaction enqueue track durable prompt pressure at the start of the user turn. Billing `usageAccounting` totals unchanged.
- **Change (ADR-150 ephemeral session install layer; local).** Session `.local` / `.npm-global` / `node_modules` stay warm-pod-only: not GCS-mirrored, not hydrated, not upserted to manifest, not shown in Files / `files.list` / `files.search`. Shared `isSessionInstallLayerPath` in `@persai/runtime-contract`. ADR-148 warmth/env/quota remain; storage-plane persistence of install trees is superseded. Curated exec image adds `httpx`. Legacy GCS install blobs are read-filtered (no mandatory purge).
- **Fix (DeepSeek stream usage null → context meter stuck on –; local).** Premium/web turns on `deepseek-v4-pro` completed with `usage: null` because DeepSeek `streamText` never requested or captured Chat Completions stream usage (`stream_options.include_usage` missing; completed/tool_calls hard-coded `usage: null`). Session `currentTokens` never refreshed, so the title-pill context meter stayed empty even after turns. Stream now requests include_usage, reads trailing `chunk.usage`, and focused DeepSeek tests pin the path. Context-meter UI: solid gray disk (no empty track ring); progress stroke draws on top; center label is `45%`-style muted text when tokens exist.
- **UX (Cursor-like shell command activity; local).** Shell/exec `tool_started` carries bounded `toolInputPreview`; web shows `Running command — <mono command>` on one line with right fade + color shimmer. Preview persists in turn `currentActivity` for soft-detach status; `tool_progress` heartbeat no longer clobbers it.
- **Fix (ADR-149 Stop crashes owning API pod; local hotfix).** Live `persai-dev`: Stop during shell aborted `api-54b8f755c-pwsxt` with uncaught `AbortError` (`exitCode=1`), left the attempt `running`, and cascaded into stuck «Выполняю команду» + broken follow-on sandbox hydrate. Root cause: `readRuntimeStream` used `void reader.cancel()`; undici body cancel rejects with the deadline AbortError as an unhandled rejection. Fix catches cancel; regression test pins the path.
- **UX (desktop chat-row actions + context meter align; local).** Desktop chat `...` drops the portal dropdown and uses the same left slide-out as mobile: Archive (+ label), rename pencil, trash with two-step «Удалить?». Mobile only swaps order to Rename → Delete. Context-meter popover left edge aligns with the title pill (`left-[-3px]`), mirroring the mode menu’s right alignment.
- **UX (chat title pill context meter; local).** Replaces the name-pill pencil/rename with an inward 3px circular context ring (sage/gray) vs the plan auto-compaction trigger (`reserveTokens − keepRecentTokens`). Weak center %; click opens a mode-menu-style popover with short copy + Compact now (`compactNow`). Rename stays in the chat list only.
- **Change (ADR-149 S4 orphan reconcilers; local, committed `7b14f8df`).** API + runtime schedulers reconcile stale attempts/receipts after 20m grace with active-owner guards.
- **Change (ADR-149 S3 tool_progress activity; local, committed `d7da3e34`).** Bounded tool_progress runtime→SSE→web with rolling shell lines and reattach merge fixes.
- **Change (ADR-149 S2 turn deadline split; local, committed `bc3d6ee8`).** Wall-clock 30m + idle stall 5m; `turn_idle_stall` vs `runtime_timeout`; no 615s video inflation.
- **Change (ADR-149 S1 durable Stop; local, committed `d0382151`).** Redis stop dispatch, honest API, sandbox cancel, lease heartbeat, user_stopped hydration.
- **ADR (ADR-149 durable Stop + turn deadlines + activity + orphans; opened).** Parent-orchestrated program after cluster-log audit: two `runtime_timeout` kills at ~615s on active DeepSeek tool loops (`firstDeltaMs=-1`), no `POST /stop`, sandbox warmth healthy. Scope: durable cross-replica Stop with shell/sandbox/browser cancel, explicit `user_stopped` next-turn truth, split turn wall-clock from `video_generate` worker timeout, progress-only idle stall watchdog (cadence `slow_avg`/`silent` frozen disabled), bounded `tool_progress` for shell/browser UI, conservative orphan reconciler. Slices S0–S5; no legacy in-memory stop registry. S1 landed locally; S2–S5 pending.
- **Closure (ADR-148 sandbox session warmth; founder accepted).** Warm session-pod reuse + fail-closed cleanup (`9e26f145`) and the live cleanup false-positive repair (`2342c2ae`) are closed after founder confirmation that idle TTL holds on deployed `persai-dev` sandbox. ADR-146 remains closed; do not reopen ADR-148 for new scope.
- **UX (title/plan pill end-cap icon geometry; pushed `5741c521`).** Title-pill pencil stays coaxial with the left rounded end (permanent `bg-bg`, 3px inset). Plan-pill trash mirrors that geometry on the right end with hover fill only (no permanent circle fill). Name-pill title/subtitle get a slight vertical gap without changing pill height.
- **UX (Role catalog hides mission prompt, keeps Skills; setup step 2 = modal catalog; pushed `5741c521`).** Change Role modal and create/recreate step 2 no longer show the model mission prompt; Connected Skills remain. Step 2 replaces the card grid with the same list+detail catalog as the modal (mobile: list → detail + back). Shared `AssistantRoleDetailPane`. Chrome extension rebuilt after WS Errors silence. Focused role selector + change-role modal tests PASS; web typecheck PASS.
- **Fix (Chrome extension bridge WS Errors spam; pushed `5741c521`).** Failed `wss://api.persai.dev/.../browser-bridge/ws` dials were flooding `chrome://extensions` Errors (`ERR_ADDRESS_UNREACHABLE` / `ERR_CONNECTION_RESET`) even though the bridge still worked after reconnect — a Web Store review risk. Dial now requires online + allowlisted URL, wires `onerror`/`onclose` in the same turn as `new WebSocket`, caps consecutive failures at 5 until online/register, and resumes on `online` / fresh registration. Extension lint/typecheck/test/build PASS.
- **Fix (detect-affected sandboxExec indentation fixture; pushed `bdd03007`).** `test:ci-detect-affected` failed because the indentation-trick case hard-coded a stale `sandboxExec.image.tag`; it now derives the live tag from `values-dev.yaml`.
- **UX (pill icon inset + stroke unify + resize dots; pushed `bdd03007`).** Halves the gap between pill contour and circular icon buttons (title pencil, plan trash, composer attach/mic) to ~3px; unifies those Lucide strokes to ~1.15. Left sidebar resize dots shift right off the border (`translate-x-2.5`); right slide-over dots shift left onto the dark overlay (`-translate-x-2.5`) with higher-contrast white dots.
- **Fix (CI ADR-146 cross-layer missing `yaml`; pushed `bdd03007`).** Root `scripts/ci/adr146-cross-layer-contract.mjs` imports `yaml`, but the package was never declared at the workspace root — CI fails with `ERR_MODULE_NOT_FOUND` on Full Verification / `test:adr146-slice5`. Adds root `devDependency` `yaml@^2.8.3` and lockfile entry so the audit resolves under pnpm.
- **UX (Settings status badge on avatar + avatar auto-save + Character label; local).** Moves the live/status green dot from the role text chip onto the avatar bottom-right (Settings hero + sidebar card) so name/role/switch lines align. Selecting a preset or uploading an avatar now auto-patches draft and publishes without needing Personalization Save. Personalization action label `Тюнинг характера` / `Character tuning` → `Характер` / `Character`.
- **Fix (Telegram Settings false disconnect + assistant-create admin notify; local).** Governance Telegram SecretRef `expiresAt` is treated as a TTL/rotation reminder, not bot death: healthy active bindings auto-renew TTL on integration-state resolve (7-day lead), and computed `expired` still counts as connected until revoke/`invalid_token`. Creating an additional workspace assistant now emits `assistant_created` (`User {email} created a new assistant`) instead of false `new_user_registered`; first assistant keeps the registration event. `assistant_created` inherits enablement from policies that already allow `new_user_registered`. Admin Notifications UI lists the new event. ADR-043 / API-BOUNDARY updated.
- **UX (desktop right slide-overs match left sidebar chrome; pushed `321b8c27`).** Settings/Telegram/Knowledge `SlideOver` on `md+`: same `1.375rem` rounding and `p-4` insets as the left sidebar; overlay dimming unchanged; mobile stays full-bleed. Desktop width stays at prior narrow/default lg ceilings (600/680) with a left-edge resize handle clamped to **500–800px** (no persistence). Left and right resize dots sit closer to the panel edge and are ~2× quieter (`opacity-35`, `bg-text-subtle/28`).
- **UX (assistant switcher shows Role; pushed `321b8c27`).** Multi-assistant switcher rows replace the “Specialty coming soon” placeholder with each assistant’s localized Role name. `AssistantListItemState` now requires compact `role: { key, name }` from the directory/bootstrap path; Change-role success reloads app data so the switcher stays fresh. Also in this local wave: personalization action buttons stack full-width on mobile / equal 1/1/1 on desktop; sidebar status/role line is 11px + truncate; change-role list column defaults +15% (253px) and is desktop-resizable ±20% without persistence.
- **UX (Settings Assistant personalization + change-role modals; pushed `af3ce0dc`).** Assistant Settings hero: read-only name, Personalization / Change role CTAs, internet row unchanged; Role accordion removed. Personalization and Change-role use desktop centered dialogs and **mobile fullscreen** sheets; Personalization carries name/behavior/gender/voice/traits/Recreate with in-place Memory swap and Save in-footer; Change-role is list+detail with read-only connected Skills. User Role API adds required `skills[]` display projection (active links only) on catalog/current/PUT; ADR-147/API-BOUNDARY carve-out for presentation-only Skills. AGENTS gate + recursive tests PASS; await api+web pin.
- **Fix (ADR-148 cleanup false-positive `remaining_pids` → per-job retire; pushed `2342c2ae`, later included in sandbox pin `bdd03007+`).** Live `persai-dev` on pin `9e26f145` showed every session job hit `sandbox_job_pod_cleanup_failed error=remaining_pids=<n>` then `sandbox_job_pod_cleanup_retired`, so warm TTL never held. Root cause: cleanup scanned `/proc` via `$(target_pids)` (subshell PID counted as leftover) and parsed tab-separated gVisor `/proc/*/status` with space-only `IFS`. Cleanup now collects targets in-shell, parses status with default IFS, skips threads/zombies/cleanup-shell children, and keeps fail-closed retirement only for real leftovers. Founder later accepted ADR-148 closed after TTL held.

## 2026-07-14

- **Change (ADR-148 sandbox session warmth + fail-closed cleanup; pushed `9e26f145`, pinned `6e631283`).** Restores real 15-minute warm-session semantics for sandbox `shell` / `exec` / `document.*` jobs by stopping unconditional terminal retirement of healthy session pods while keeping sessionless jobs disposable. Session pods now persist after successful/failed/blocked terminal handling only when a control-plane-owned cleanup pass proves the post-job process baseline is clean; otherwise the exact bound UID is retired before lease release. Runtime package paths now live under the canonical session root (`HOME`, `PYTHONUSERBASE`, `NPM_CONFIG_PREFIX`, login-shell PATH), dependency trees get their own bounded contour (`20k` files / `4k` dirs / `512 MiB`) so restored or realistic package installs do not poison later jobs, duplicate same-prefix session rehydrate is removed, expected cold-start marker misses stop logging `stdinless_probe_failed`, and the exec image/pod command now use `tini` for persistent-session child reaping. Focused sandbox service / exec bridge / exec-image tests passed locally (`107/107`). Live follow-up: cleanup false-positive retired pods until the 2026-07-15 repair. ADR-146 remains closed; ADR-148 supersedes only the over-broad per-job retirement behavior.
- **UX (live status line shows Role name; local).** Under the assistant name in the left sidebar and Settings character header: green/`live` shows the current Role name instead of Active/Активен; other lifecycle statuses still show the status label. Focused helper/sidebar/settings tests PASS.
- **Change (Admin MCP `skill_list` bounded repair; local full gate PASS, pushed).** Adds strict-empty-input read-only `skill_list` over the existing bodyless `GET /api/v1/admin/skills` operator route using the shared client/error contour. The canonical payload is returned without local filtering, sorting, pagination, truncation, or projection so agents can discover production Skill UUIDs before `skill_get`, Role composition, or catalog migration. Focused registration/request/passthrough/error/README/existing-tool tests pass (Admin MCP 17/17), as do package lint/typecheck/build, recursive lint, repository format, API/web typechecks, and the vocabulary zero gate. Startup truth reconciliation also updates stale ADR-147 Release C status in architecture/API/data-model docs and removes now-zero historical vocabulary allowances; no API, OpenAPI, schema, Role/Skill behavior, or ADR changes. Package-only: MCP rebuild/reload + new Agent chat required to observe the tool.

- **Fix (ADR-140 Android Lavka pointer activation system; local).** Live logcat proved two independent failures: (1) pre-1.0.34 APK injected CSS coords as view pixels (`pointer_tap x=` without `viewX`); (2) modal overlays blocked taps (`sameNode:false`, hit `modal-text` / «На сайте»). Native tap path now fully enables the hidden WebView (alpha 1, focus), sends DOWN→MOVE→UP finger MotionEvents with consumption logging, and stops immediately re-adding the ownership overlay after each tap. Page runner retargets occluded clicks to the interactive hit element, keeps the ownership overlay disabled through settle, and dispatches a DOM pointer fallback after native tap. - **Feature (ADR-141 native browser activity thumbnail; local).** Capacitor now exposes a quiet, image-only companion for assistant-owned authenticated browser work. - **Fix (ADR-140 Chrome bridge lifecycle + non-destructive configured-session recovery; local).** Assistant-triggered browser turns no longer trust a freshly cached `connected:false` status: web re-probes the live current surface before starting the turn and carries its exact extension device id. The extension keeps a relay socket desired for the lifetime of a fresh registration rather than tying it to one content-script port, and safely drops late replies after a tab/port disconnect. An active Settings profile that cannot open now stays saved and shows a quiet inline connection error; it no longer enters the login modal or exposes a Cancel path that deletes the profile. The actual login modal's disconnected-extension block is one centered text stack with the retry button on its own row; Capacitor does not render it. Model-owned `request_user_action` now creates its chat handoff banner even when the bridge is temporarily disconnected, because no dispatch is required until the user presses Open.
- **Fix + UX (ADR-140 quiet configured-session cards + Android active-work display; local).** Configured browser-profile cards keep their full click target but no longer render the redundant `Open browser window` / reconnect action label. While Android executes an assistant-owned profile `snapshot` or `act`, the native coordinator holds `FLAG_KEEP_SCREEN_ON`; a global active-command count releases it on the final result/error so normal display timeout resumes immediately afterward. Android `1.0.23` / `versionCode 25` passed bridge/unit/debug/release checks and was exported to the PersAI download surface.

## 2026-07-10

- **Fix + UX (ADR-140 quiet login handoff; local).** Desktop/mobile login now presents one centered Open pill plus concise completion copy rather than persistent instruction/status cards; a connected bridge is a quiet inline indicator, help is on-demand, and only an unavailable desktop extension renders a compact install/retry warning. Mobile waits for explicit Open before revealing the native browser and keeps the established Back → Done/Cancel flow. Footer actions match the product’s pill controls. Assistant-triggered extension windows now restore to normal state and apply canonical 70%/16:9 bounds in a second Chrome update, preventing Chrome from retaining its small minimized/popup dimensions.
- **Fix (ADR-131/ADR-137 file/session execution path; local).** Restored canonical chat-ID flow for real web/Telegram turns: web sync/stream now send canonical `assistant_chat.id` in both runtime context positions; runtime resolves that ID before safe real-chat fallback; chat-scoped manifest lists fail closed without issuing a non-UUID Prisma filter; and `document.render` passes the resolved origin into storage-plane output allocation. GCS + manifest remain canonical; the session pod remains an execution cache, now creates its cwd on every command, avoids marking zero-object hydrates successful, and rehydrates session/shared bytes so a storage-plane write becomes visible to subsequent `shell`. Focused API/runtime/sandbox regression suites and the mandatory lint/format/API+web checks pass. Deploy and live acceptance remain pending.
- **Fix (ADR-140 shared DOM-stability gate; local).** Replaced the desktop/mobile page runners' 40-character / two-control readiness shortcut with one universal bounded gate: document at least `interactive`, body present, then 750 ms of DOM quiet under `MutationObserver`, with the existing 10-second cap. Timeout captures current state as `loadStatus: "partial"`; stable reads return `"stable"`. The fact propagates through local-bridge/native/runtime results. No second wait, site-specific heuristic, spinner parser, `load`, or network-idle dependency was added. Android 1.0.22 (`versionCode 24`) was built, exported, and installed.
- **Fix (ADR-140 Capacitor strict-CSP runner injection; local).** Live `ya.ru` profile evidence isolated a page-runner failure before any navigation/action: the Android/iOS wrappers used indirect `eval` for PersAI's packaged runner, and strict site CSP correctly rejected it as `unsafe-eval`. Native wrappers now embed that trusted runner directly in the privileged WebView/WKWebView injection wrapper. Android `1.0.17` / `versionCode 19` passed bridge tests plus Android unit/release compilation, was exported to the download surface, and installed to the connected test device; live `ya.ru` acceptance remains pending.
- **Fix + UX (ADR-140 model-owned browser handoff and cancellation lifecycle; local).** Removed every browser page-text/selector/value heuristic that could emit `needs_user_action`, interrupt commands, or reveal a desktop/mobile browser surface. The model now uses explicit `browser.request_user_action` with a saved profile and exact `userActionPrompt`; PersAI renders a handoff card first, Open reveals the current surface only after the user's click, and Done hides it and starts the continuation turn. CAPTCHA, OTP/verification, payment, and irreversible actions remain a prompt-level safety wall rather than client parsing. Fixed both desktop Cancel races: `close_view` no longer creates a missing extension profile window; Cancel clears UI immediately and aborts unsettled `open-live`; profile deletion can close the caller's current bridge before DB binding exists; extension priority view commands execute in arrival order so a prior Open cannot finish after Close. Android `1.0.16` / `versionCode 18` passed release assembly and was exported to PersAI's download surface.
- **Fix (ADR-140 Capacitor canonical main-frame redirect completion; local).** Live Lavka basket work exposed two exact 30.4-second failures. Persisted tool exchanges proved both requested `https://lavka.yandex.ru/search`; Yandex canonicalized the route to `/`, but the native gate rejected that first main-frame redirect because its path differed from the request and waited for the full 30-second navigation deadline. A valid main-frame navigation action observed while the command is pending now starts the current redirect chain on Android/iOS, while unrelated stale page commit callbacks remain blocked. Android `1.0.15` / `versionCode 17` was built, exported, and installed.
- **Fix (ADR-140 Capacitor null navigation decoding; local).** Live Mail.ru acceptance passed on 1.0.13, but a fresh Lavka profile exposed a fast failure limited to ordinary non-anchor `act`: runtime dispatched valid `https://lavka.yandex.ru/`, while Android rejected `"null"` as a target URL. The anchor-handoff runner serialized absent navigation as JSON null and Android `JSONObject.optString` surfaced it as the literal string `"null"`. Runners now omit absent `navigationUrl`; Android also maps JSON null defensively. Android `1.0.14` / `versionCode 16` was built, exported, and installed.
- **Fix (ADR-140 Capacitor cross-origin/click navigation completion; local).** Post-affinity live evidence successively isolated stale page commits, cross-origin completion replacement, URL canonicalization, and stale pre-goto navigation. Live 1.0.12 then exposed the decisive 109.8-second hang: clicking an ordinary `<a href>` destroyed the ephemeral page-runner JavaScript context before it could call native, so the bridge waited to its execution deadline and never reached the following goto. The shared runner now returns HTTP(S) anchor navigation declaratively before clicking; Android/iOS activate destination cookies and navigate after receiving the callback, then continue remaining segments without reloading an equivalent explicit goto. Existing profiles/cookies remain valid. Android `1.0.13` / `versionCode 15` was built, exported, and installed; matching PersAI web runner deploy is required.
- **Fix (ADR-140 strict current-surface turn affinity; local).** Mobile logcat proved a founder-triggered browser turn never reached Android: ordinary chat turns carried no current bridge identity, so runtime used `mail-ru`'s persisted Chrome ref. Every interactive web/app turn now declares its extension/Capacitor surface and connected device ID through both stream and sync runtime paths. Current-turn dispatch requires that exact installation and cannot fall back to another live device; a disconnected current surface fails honestly before dispatch. Successful profile commands and `open_live` persist relay-authenticated ref + kind together, allowing one logical profile to switch between separately logged-in device-local sessions without phone commands running in Chrome or desktop commands running on the phone. No APK change.
- **Fix (ADR-140 current-surface browser profile affinity; local).** Mobile acceptance unexpectedly returned Chrome-only `Host permission was denied`, and live DB truth showed the `mail-ru` profile remained bound to `bridgeClientKind: extension` plus a Chrome device ref. Settings knew it was running in Capacitor but omitted the current bridge device ID from `open-live`, so API dispatched to the stored extension; chat assist Open had the same gap. Settings and chat now target the current connected surface explicitly. Relay dispatch reports its authenticated `deviceKind`, and successful open atomically persists both device ref and kind, preventing later assistant turns and Back ownership from switching back to a different installation.
- **Fix (ADR-140 mobile priority view lifecycle and bounded navigation; local).** Live Mail.ru login navigation proved a page command could occupy the Capacitor command queue for 120 seconds while a settings `open-live` waited behind it for `98.65s`; once the timed-out result arrived late, the queued view opened after Back had already cleared its handler, explaining both the spontaneous browser reveal and subsequent app exit. Capacitor `open_view` / `close_view` / `check_view` now bypass `snapshot` / `act` serialization. Android treats `onPageCommitVisible` as sufficient to run the DOM-ready reader, caps navigation wait at 30 seconds, and reserves transport time inside the outer command deadline so results cannot lose a same-deadline race. Android release becomes `1.0.9` / `versionCode 11`.
- **Fix (ADR-140 mobile generated runner compile failure; local).** Live Android snapshot dispatch remained pending for exactly 120 seconds and returned `bridge_command_timeout`. Evaluating the deployed `PAGE_RUNNER_SOURCE` reproduced `SyntaxError: await is only valid in async functions`: the generated function lost its `async` modifier while still containing top-level `await`. Restored async generation in PersAI and the mobile package, added tests that compile the final source string and assert `AsyncFunction`, and wrapped Android/iOS runner eval/setup in synchronous error reporting so malformed source returns its real error immediately instead of timing out. Android release becomes `1.0.8` / `versionCode 10`.
- **Fix (ADR-140 retained-session latency, mobile Back ownership, and settings-card stability; local).** Connected-phone and cluster logs proved the reported mobile hang was not `bridge_connection_closed`: the dispatched snapshot remained pending for 31 seconds and then completed successfully because the native bridge redundantly navigated to the profile's already-open URL before running the page reader. Android, iOS, and the desktop extension now compare normalized scheme/host/port/path/query and skip navigation when the requested document is already loaded. Native browser Back handlers now outrank settings/navigation handlers so the first system Back hides the overlay, and configured-session reconciliation runs without replacing the visible card list with a loading state. Android `1.0.7` / `versionCode 9` was built, exported, and installed on the connected phone.
- **Fix + UX (ADR-140 browser ownership and explicit user checkpoint handoff; local).** The local bridge no longer equates a visible browser surface with user ownership. During ordinary profile-backed `snapshot`/`act`, a visible desktop/mobile page is observer-only: user input is blocked and localized `Работает ассистент!` / `Assistant is working!` appears on hover/tap, while assistant operations continue underneath; mobile Back only hides the retained session. Replaced the broad page-text heuristic that classified generic `payment` / `оплат` / `карта` cart copy as `needs_user_action` with strong CAPTCHA/anti-bot/OTP contours plus preflight checks on genuinely sensitive payment/verification controls. A real checkpoint now carries an assist-state profile through API/runtime/SSE and renders a compact PersAI action banner; Open re-shows the same view, and Done hides it and emits the semantic continuation turn so the assistant resumes. Runtime guidance now states that visibility does not block automation and forbids `open_live`/retry loops after a checkpoint. Android/iOS native ownership parity landed, and the mobile TS command contract now includes the already-native `check_view` verb. Android 1.0.6 (`versionCode 8`) built and was exported into PersAI's mobile download surface.
- **Fix (ADR-140 live Mail.ru follow-up: deterministic desktop window bounds, explicit MV3 browser grant, Android hidden runner; local).** Founder live acceptance showed three distinct defects. An assistant-opened profile window stayed at the legacy tiny popup size whenever extension storage already marked it visible, because the existing-window path skipped bounds normalization; every visible open now reapplies the canonical centered 70%/16:9 bounds. Desktop snapshot/act correctly found the bridge but repeatedly returned `Host permission was denied` because a WebSocket-dispatched MV3 service worker has no user gesture; the extension now opens a focused, non-technical PersAI browser-access window, waits for the user's legal click, then resumes the original command automatically. Live PNG acceptance exposed Chrome's separate rule: `captureVisibleTab` rejects an origin grant and requires `activeTab` on the exact target tab or `<all_urls>`. Requiring a manual tab click before every autonomous screenshot is not viable, so `<all_urls>` is declared as an optional-only permission and requested once from that explicit user-gesture window; it is not granted at install time or needed for login/open-view. On mobile, cluster logs showed healthy dispatch/result polling while connected-phone logcat ended with `Timed out waiting for page execution`: the native coordinator hid the retained WebView with `INVISIBLE/GONE` before evaluation, allowing Mail.ru's page-runner Promise/timers to suspend. Background execution now keeps that renderer attached and technically visible but transparent until completion, with a custom overlay host that returns every touch to the underlying PersAI WebView, then restores the hidden state. Installed Android 1.0.5 (`versionCode 7`) debug over the connected phone and directly exercised a hidden Capacitor snapshot of `https://mail.ru/`; it returned Mail.ru title/content in ~11 seconds instead of timing out. An instrumented 10-second hidden command plus real Android tap focused the underlying PersAI `TEXTAREA`, proving the app remains interactive during execution.
- **Fix (ADR-140 bridge connection durability, stable device affinity, direct configured-session UX, desktop permission grant; pushed with this entry).** Live cluster and connected-phone evidence showed a healthy mobile bridge at 21:32Z becoming an immediate `bridge_unavailable` 409 by 21:39Z while the Android process remained alive. The public WebSocket had no protocol keepalive, the Capacitor client never reconnected after a close, and every authenticated re-registration minted a different `bridgeDeviceId`; profiles therefore retained dead device affinity, especially when two Chrome installations were live. The API WebSocket now sends 20s ping frames, Capacitor retries transient disconnects while its token is valid, authenticated registration renews the same per-installation device id (persisted by extension/mobile), and an app-shell maintainer reconnects/renews bridges outside the login modal on app load, foreground, network recovery, and a 30s health interval. Clicking an already configured session card now opens its desktop extension window or mobile native browser directly; the web modal is reserved for login/reconnect or an open error, and mobile Back hides the direct native view and returns to the app. Desktop windows are re-centered/resized on every open from the largest normal Chrome window, so an existing popup can no longer shrink subsequent sessions. Desktop DOM automation now has a real MV3 user-gesture path: the extension popup shows the current profile origin and a `Grant access` button that calls `chrome.permissions.request` directly from the click handler. Browser delivery copy is surface-neutral and regression-locked against `Telegram`. Android release `1.0.4` (`versionCode 6`) was built, exported to PersAI's `/mobile/persai-android-release.apk`, installed on the connected phone, and startup-smoked.
- **Fix (ADR-140 mobile safe area + bounded login completion; local).** Founder live acceptance confirmed the native browser site finally opened, then exposed two mobile defects: the overlay extended behind Android's status/navigation bars, and pressing Done spun until `Failed to fetch`. Live `adb logcat` proved the completion command entered the native page runner and failed with `Timed out waiting for page execution`; cluster logs showed repeated `complete-login` 409s after 8–83 seconds. The Android overlay now applies system-bar/display-cutout insets, and iOS constrains the overlay to the root safe area. Native Android/iOS now implement `check_view` as a lightweight liveness + cookie-flush command without page execution, while API login completion uses `check_view` for both extension and Capacitor clients. Installed the rebuilt debug APK over the connected phone; live native `check_view` returned immediately for `https://mail.ru/`, and cluster `complete-login` completed 200 in 548 ms. Verified mobile bridge tests (6), Android plugin unit/compile, full debug APK assembly/install/startup smoke, API browser-profile tests (13), and API typecheck.

## 2026-07-09

- **Fix (ADR-140 live triage: mobile native-plugin thenable hang, cross-tab register storm, stale bridgeDeviceId hard-fail; local → pushed with this entry).** Live-tested on a connected phone (`adb logcat`) plus live cluster/Redis inspection after the founder reported the mobile modal never once loaded the site and desktop stopped opening the window entirely. Three defects. (1) `browser-bridge-client.ts`'s `getNativeBrowserBridgePlugin()` returned Capacitor's plugin proxy as an async function's resolved value; Capacitor's proxy answers every property access — including `then` — with a native wrapper, so promise resolution treated it as a thenable and called `proxy.then()`, which throws `"PersaiBrowserBridge.then()" is not implemented on android` (confirmed verbatim in live logcat) and left every native command awaiting forever until the server-side dispatch timed out. Fixed by caching the plugin proxy in a module-level variable instead of ever letting it flow through a promise resolution. (2) The 15s device-registration throttle lived in a React ref scoped to one tab; with multiple PersAI tabs/windows open (confirmed live: `browser-bridge/devices` 201s every 5-40s), each tab's independent throttle let combined registrations churn far faster than 15s, and each registration forces the extension to drop and reconnect its socket — killing in-flight commands with `bridge_connection_closed` (confirmed live, `open-live` latencies of 20-120s). Moved the throttle into `registerExtensionBridgeDevice` itself, backed by `localStorage` so it is shared across every open tab. (3) The relay's connection selector treated a caller-supplied (often stale, DB-stored) `bridgeDeviceId` as a hard requirement — a mismatch failed dispatch immediately with `bridge_device_not_connected`/`bridge_unavailable` even when exactly one live connection existed and would have worked. This directly explained a live assistant `browser.open_live` tool call failing with `bridge_unavailable` on an `active` profile. A stale/unmatched id now falls through to the same auto-selection used when no id is given (single connection succeeds; zero stays unavailable; multiple still asks to disambiguate). Verified `@persai/api` browser-bridge relay/cross-pod/assistant-browser-profile tests (24, incl. 2 new), api typecheck/lint, `@persai/web` full suite (563) + typecheck/lint, `format:check`.

- **Fix (web channel truth + assist-modal style + honest extension permission denial; local → pushed with this entry).** Three founder-reported defects. (1) Runtime developer instructions only named the channel for Telegram turns; web turns carried no surface truth, so assistants regularly assumed they were in Telegram and invented wrong limitations. `buildChannelContextDeveloperSection` now emits an explicit `Channel: PersAI web app chat … NOT Telegram` section for web turns (Telegram section unchanged); regression assertions added to the turn-execution suite. (2) Clicking a browser-session card in assistant settings opened the extension window with the old full-screen modal behind it — the compact desktop modal style was gated to `completionMode === "login"`; assist/live view is now compact too (mobile stays full-screen). (3) The extension's `ensureOriginPermission` leaked the raw `This function must be called during a user gesture` error as `browser_failed` when the runtime dispatched `snapshot`/`act` to an origin without a host grant; it now catches the gesture error and returns the structured `permission_denied` result. Verified runtime typecheck/lint + turn-execution suite, extension lint/typecheck/test(16)/build, web modal tests (9) + lint/typecheck, `format:check`.

- **Fix (ADR-140 live-acceptance follow-up: expired-token re-registration, native request storm; local → pushed with this entry).** Cluster logs after the `0c8ca8fd` deploy showed two remaining functional defects. (1) The login modal skipped re-registration whenever the extension already knew the current assistant scope, but bridge device tokens expire after 15 minutes — the extension then redialed the relay forever with the dead token (continuous `Device token has expired` rejections in `api` logs) and could never reconnect. The modal now falls through to (throttled) re-registration when the scope matches but the socket is down, and the extension stops dialing entirely once its stored registration is older than 14 minutes, waiting for a fresh one instead. (2) The mobile modal's 3s poll stacked register + `open-live` calls while the previous ones were still pending server-side (15–26s dispatch timeouts), flooding the relay into its dispatch rate limit (409/429 storm in logs). Added an in-flight guard on the native refresh path and a singleton connect promise in the native bridge client so device identity cannot churn from overlapping registrations. Verified extension lint/typecheck/test(16)/build, web modal tests (9), web lint/typecheck, `format:check`.

- **Fix (ADR-140 login completion truth: `check_view` verification, explicit device targeting, register throttle, mobile overlay escape; local, not pushed).** Desktop `Готово` always failed because `complete-login` verified via `snapshot`, which needs `chrome.permissions.request` host grants that a service-worker command can never obtain without a user gesture → permanent `permission_denied` 409. Extension-kind verification now dispatches a new permission-free `check_view` action (window/tab liveness + last known URL, no DOM access); capacitor keeps `snapshot`. Second failure class was device ambiguity/staleness: with mobile + desktop both registered, `open-live`/`complete-login` dispatched to `bridgeSessionRef` of whichever device registered last or failed on `bridge_device_ambiguous`. The web modal now sends its own connected `bridgeDeviceId` in both request bodies and the API prefers it over the stored ref. Third class was register churn: the 3s status poll re-registered a fresh device id each tick, orphaning the extension's live socket; registration is now throttled (15s/scope) and the extension force-reconnects its socket when a newer device id supersedes the authenticated one. After successful `complete-login` the API fire-and-forgets `close_view` so the surface hides itself. Desktop `open_view` popup now sizes to ~70% of the screen at 16:9 instead of a small fixed window. Mobile: hardware Back now locally hides the native overlay (no server round-trip) so the user can reach `Готово`, with a "показать сайт снова" action and return hint in the modal; overlay auto-open on connect unchanged. Verified extension lint/typecheck/test(16)/build, API typecheck + focused browser-profile/relay/cross-pod suites (20), web typecheck + modal tests (9), runtime/provider/sandbox/contract typechecks, repo lint, `format:check`.

- **Fix + UX (ADR-140 desktop extension `open_view` unblock + compact login modal; local, not pushed).** Desktop login never completed because the extension's `open_view` path gated on `ensureCommandPermissions` (which calls `chrome.permissions.request` — illegal without a user gesture from a WebSocket-dispatched command, so it returned permission-denied → fast 409) and then blocked on `waitForTabLoad` (login redirects hang until timeout → slow 409). `open_view` now skips the host-permission gate entirely (opening/navigating a window you own needs no host permission — only DOM access does) and no longer waits for full page load; it kicks navigation and returns `{ ok: true, finalUrl }` promptly so `open-live` resolves success. `close_view` and the snapshot/act/assist paths keep their host-permission + page-runner behavior unchanged. The web login UI is now a compact PersAI-styled modal instead of a full-screen dialog: it shows site/instructions/extension state, no longer auto-opens the desktop Chrome window from polling/registration, and provides an explicit `Открыть <site>` button plus `Готово`/`Отмена` in the modal. The Chrome popup window is only the browser surface for signing in; no third-party-page overlay is attempted because MV3 cannot reliably draw/control it without host permission. Mobile/native behavior is unchanged. Verified `@persai/browser-extension` lint/typecheck/test (16)/build, focused web `browser-login-modal` (9), `@persai/web` typecheck, and repo `format:check`.

- **Fix (ADR-140 browser bridge cross-pod relay; local, not pushed).** The local browser-bridge relay kept its connection registry and command lifecycle in per-pod memory while `api` runs with ≥2 replicas, so a device WebSocket owned by one pod was invisible to `open-live` / `complete-login` / browser-tool `dispatch`+`result` HTTP that the GCLB round-robins to another pod — surfacing as a permanent `bridge_unavailable` / 409 for both desktop and mobile even after a successful socket connect. Live probing confirmed `api.persai.dev` health, TLS, and the WebSocket upgrade (`101 Switching Protocols` via the GCE LB) were all healthy, isolating the fault to the relay rather than ingress or the client. Introduced a Redis-backed coordinator (`BROWSER_BRIDGE_REDIS_URL`, reusing the runtime Redis) that shares the connection registry + command state across replicas and forwards each dispatch to the pod owning the socket via pub/sub, so `getCommandResult` resolves from any pod; sockets and local timeouts still live on the owning pod. Relay degrades to the previous in-memory single-process behavior when the env is unset (local dev). Verified api typecheck/lint, `@persai/config` typecheck, web typecheck, `format:check`, focused relay + new cross-pod suites, and `helm lint`/`template`.

- **Fix (ADR-140 browser bridge websocket host under same-origin web proxy; local, not pushed).** Device registration for the local browser bridge was returning `wss://persai.dev/api/v1/assistant/browser-bridge/ws` when the request arrived through the web app's same-origin `/api/v1` proxy. That host cannot carry the websocket upgrade path used by the extension/mobile bridge, so both desktop and mobile stayed on the instruction screen after successful registration. The API registration controller now returns the public API websocket host instead (`api.persai.dev` when the request came through `persai.dev`), with a focused regression test covering the proxied web-origin case. Verified focused API controller test and API typecheck.

- **Fix (web chat attachments layout; local, not pushed).** Mixed attachment messages now render previewable media before ordinary files instead of letting image cards and file pills share one flex row. File pills moved to their own lane so they no longer stretch into oversized bubbles beside tall images, duplicate previewable file pills are suppressed when the same image/video asset is already shown, and image cards now use portrait/square/landscape crop-first frames so long screenshots stay readable in the chat feed. Verified focused `chat-message` tests plus API/web typechecks.

- **Fix (ADR-140 browser login modal help-toggle UX; local, not pushed).** The web login modal no longer shows the full instruction block by default in the happy path. It now keeps compact copy plus retry controls, adds an `i` help toggle beside reload, and auto-expands the instructions only as a fallback when bridge-driven `/open-live` cannot open the site. Verified focused modal tests, `@persai/web` typecheck, and repo `format:check`.

- **Fix (ADR-140 desktop/mobile bridge login wiring; pushed `4805aa5f`).** The web login modal now registers the Chrome extension bridge device instead of only checking `persai.bridge.status`, and it also owns a Capacitor bridge client for mobile: register native device, hold the relay WebSocket, and forward commands into `PersaiBrowserBridge.executeCommand`. After bridge connection the modal calls `/open-live`, so the visible browser view receives the target login URL instead of leaving the user on the instruction screen. `PendingBrowserLoginState` now carries `workspaceId` through contract/API/runtime/web parsers because registration needs assistant + workspace identity. Desktop content script catches invalidated extension contexts after extension reload, and Chrome extension icon assets now use the supplied PersAI mobile `P`. Verified extension build/typecheck, focused web bridge tests, and API/runtime/web typechecks.
