## 2026-07-07

- **Fix (ADR-139 D13 addendum — found and fixed the actual root cause behind the recurring "gateway 502"/"type crashes" reports: plain Browserless `429 Too many requests` queue pressure; local, not pushed).** Immediately after D12's logging fix deployed, the parent agent drove the same live PersAI chat session directly to get first-hand evidence. `snapshot` and `click` worked cleanly (60 elements, D11's fix confirmed live). `type` failed — the model's own real-time diagnosis ("Browserless backend crashes on `page.type()`") was wrong; `kubectl logs` on the D12-instrumented pod showed the real cause immediately: `[persistent-bql] transport failure status=429: Too many requests`. Per Browserless's own enterprise docs, `429` specifically means the plan's concurrency queue is full — not a crash, not fingerprinting, not session death — and is very plausibly the true explanation behind the entire live-test arc's "gateway 502" symptoms. Fixed by adding `fetchJsonWithRateLimitRetry` in `ProviderBrowserService`: a bounded retry (2 retries, 600ms then 1500ms backoff) for `429` responses, wired into both the persistent BQL and ephemeral `/function` paths, absorbing transient queue pressure per Browserless's own guidance instead of surfacing every `429` as a hard tool failure. Exhausting the retry budget still raises a normal `BadGatewayException`. If `429`s persist, the account's Browserless plan concurrency limit needs raising — flagged as a residual, not evaluated here. New unit test covers both the successful-after-retry and retry-exhausted paths. `@persai/provider-gateway` typecheck, lint, and full test suite pass.

- **Fix (ADR-139 D12 addendum — closed the real observability gap: browser tool failures were completely silent in both runtime and provider-gateway logs; local, not pushed).** A live borscht-shopping test on the already-deployed D11 image reported 3 straight `act` failures plus a "gateway 502" symptom, but `kubectl logs` across both `runtime` and `provider-gateway` pods showed nothing for the entire test window. Three real defects: **(1)** `RuntimeBrowserToolService.executeToolCall`'s top-level catch (and `executeListProfiles`'s catch) swallowed every browser failure into a structured `browser_failed` tool result with zero logging — the real reason lived only in the model-facing `warning` string. Fixed by adding `this.logger.warn(...)` with action/url/profile-presence and the real error message, plus a `this.logger.log(...)` request-trace line before the outbound call. **(2)** D10's own logging fix used `debug`, which this cluster's actual `LOG_LEVEL=info` filters out entirely — confirmed by grepping full pod log dumps and finding only route-registration output. Fixed by changing to `this.logger.log(...)`. **(3)** D10 only logged BQL-level `errors[]` on a 200 response; the `!response.ok` HTTP-transport branch (a real non-2xx from Browserless) and the ephemeral path's script-level fatal-error branch threw with no logging at all — very plausibly the actual "gateway 502" reported. Fixed by adding `warn` logs with status/message before both throws. On the catalog "+" button itself: D11's visibility filter + 60-cap was already live for this test and the button still never appeared after three scroll+act attempts, shifting the leading (not yet proven) hypothesis to a hover-only-render UI pattern rather than a cap/visibility problem — none of our operation kinds dispatch a hover event, so this needs a live recheck with the new logging before deciding on a follow-up. `@persai/runtime` and `@persai/provider-gateway` typecheck and focused suites pass.

- **Fix (ADR-139 D11 addendum — element-extraction visibility ranking + act chaining guidance, from model-observed friction on the live Lavka session; local, not pushed).** Two follow-up friction points from the D10 test, both verified against code before deciding what to fix. **Real defect:** the 25-element interactive-elements cap (`BROWSERLESS_INTERACTIVE_ELEMENTS_EVALUATE_SCRIPT` and `BROWSERLESS_FUNCTION_CODE`) ran `querySelectorAll` in plain document order with zero visibility filtering, so on an ordinary e-commerce page the first 25 elements were header/nav/logo/cart-icon chrome, not catalog/product content — live-confirmed on Lavka search results, where product controls never made the unfiltered top-25 despite being visibly rendered. Fixed by filtering to currently-visible elements (`getClientRects().length > 0` + non-hidden computed style) _before_ the top-N cap, and raising `MAX_RUNTIME_BROWSER_INTERACTIVE_ELEMENTS` from 25 to 60 in `packages/runtime-contract` as a safety margin; also fixed a parity bug where the ephemeral `/function` path hardcoded a literal `25` instead of reading the shared constant. **Not a code defect:** the model believed `act` needed one operation per call and asked for a way to chain `[click, type, press, click]`; the `operations` array (already up to 6 steps, with an existing `wait_for_selector` kind) already runs every step in one call on both execution paths — the gap was that the schema description never told the model this was safe, so it defaulted to one-op-per-call plus defensive snapshots. Fixed by rewriting the `operations` description (`native-tool-projection.ts`, `tool-catalog-data.ts`) to explicitly teach chaining a full interaction in one call, using `wait_for_selector` as the bridge after any step that opens new content. `@persai/provider-gateway`, `@persai/runtime`, and `@persai/api` focused suites, lint, and typecheck all pass.

- **Change (ADR-139 D10 addendum — post-D9-deploy live acceptance: `act`/UA fixes confirmed live, residential proxy confirmed still inert; server-side BQL logging added).** Re-tested against the deployed D9 image (`provider-gateway:8b36fd09...`, confirmed via `kubectl describe pod`) on the same persistent Lavka profile. **Confirmed fixed:** `act` (`click`/`type`) now completes a full real flow — login, search, click product, add to cart — with no 502s; UA masking confirmed via browserleaks/JA4 (desktop Chrome, not `HeadlessChrome`). **Confirmed still broken:** egress IP unchanged (DigitalOcean datacenter) on two separate post-deploy checks. Root-caused: since the full BQL call succeeded end-to-end, `proxy(...)` did not throw a GraphQL error (a fatal, non-`op_`-prefixed error would have failed the whole call per the existing audit-era `splitBqlErrors` classification) — it is executing without error and simply not changing the egress path, which Browserless's `proxy` mutation response (`{ time }` only) has no field to disprove either way. Most likely cause: this Browserless token's plan/fleet has no residential-proxy entitlement provisioned and silently no-ops an unprovisioned `network: residential` request rather than erroring — an account/billing-plane question outside what provider-gateway's request/response can settle, not a remaining code defect. Also closed a pre-existing observability gap: `ProviderBrowserService` had zero logging, so `kubectl logs` showed nothing but pod-startup route registration for the entire test window. Added a debug-level line per persistent BQL call (profile id, proxy/stealth presence, operation count) and an unconditional warn-level dump of every `errors[]` entry (`path` + `message`) before fatal/warning classification. Documented as ADR-139 D10, including a correction to D7's already-superseded proxy-effectiveness claim and to D9's now-open "not yet live-verified" risk note. Practical outcome: the tested Lavka add-to-cart flow succeeded end-to-end on the datacenter IP, further disproving the "hard-blocks without residential/RU IP" theory. `@persai/provider-gateway` full suite, lint, and typecheck pass.

- **Fix (ADR-139 D9 addendum — `act` opaque 502, and proxy/stealth were never actually engaging on any live session; local, not pushed).** Post-deploy live acceptance surfaced three real defects, found by reading Browserless's own BQL schema/docs against the executed code, and corrects a wrong D7 claim. **Correction:** D7's "residential proxy already resolves to a usable Russian IP" was inferred from a saved delivery address rendering on Lavka's pages — that is account data, not IP evidence; a direct browserleaks check on the same profile/session shows a DigitalOcean datacenter IP on every call, proxy or not. **Fix 1 (`act` 502):** the ephemeral `/function` script's single outer `try/catch` wrapped every operation, so an ordinary "selector not found" miss (the most common `act` outcome while the model is still guessing selectors) discarded the already-successful navigation and surfaced as an opaque `BadGatewayException`, identical to a true platform failure; live-reproduced on a clean `example.com` page with a bogus selector. Each operation is now wrapped in its own `try/catch`, collecting failures into `result.operationWarning` (folded into the success `warning` field, mirroring the BQL path's existing `op_*` classification) instead of throwing, while the page already reached is still returned. **Fix 2 (proxy no-op):** Browserless's `proxy()` mutation is a request-matching filter — its own docs state only matching requests are proxied, "the rest are sent from the instance's own IP address" — and every official example, including the one for proxying _all_ requests, passes an explicit `url: ["*"]`; `buildBrowserlessCapabilityPolicyMutations` never included any filter, so the mutation executed without error on every call and matched zero requests, meaning 100% of traffic kept flowing over the datacenter IP for the life of every persistent session. Fixed by adding `url: ["*"]`. **Fix 3 (UA leak):** live inspection showed the literal string `Chrome/149.0.0.0 (headless)` in the User-Agent on a `stealth: true` session; Browserless documents "User Agent Masking" as distinct from what stealth mode itself covers (CDP-detection, canvas/WebGL noise, automation flags) and requires an explicit `userAgent(userAgent: String!)` mutation. `buildBrowserlessCapabilityPolicyMutations` now also emits a desktop-Chrome `userAgent(...)` mutation whenever `capabilityPolicy.stealth` is true. Both fixes are per-BQL-call (per D8), so neither requires re-creating or re-logging-in any existing persistent profile. Documented as ADR-139 D9; proxy/stealth effectiveness is explicitly **not yet live-verified** — only a post-deploy browserleaks-equivalent check counts, not a successful page load. `@persai/provider-gateway` full suite and typecheck pass.

- **Change (ADR-139 D8 addendum — proxy re-assertion confirmed correct + v0 domain-based RU proxy-country test heuristic; local, not pushed).** Answered two live-validation follow-ups by reading Browserless's own docs/schema instead of guessing. First: re-sending `proxy(network: residential, sticky: true)` on every persistent BrowserQL call is correct, not wasteful — BQL traffic-interception mutations only apply "when the query is executing," and each `.../session/bql/{id}` POST is a discrete query against the same persisted browser, so a call that omitted it would leak that call's traffic off-proxy; re-asserting unchanged parameters does not rotate the sticky IP (`sticky` binds for the connection's lifetime; only _changing_ proxy params mid-session is the bot-detection signal Browserless warns against), matching the D7 live evidence of a consistent Russian-appearing address across calls. Second: confirmed via code read (not assumption) that no PersAI code captures end-user IP/geolocation anywhere and that persistent browser profiles are `(assistantId, profileKey)`-scoped (assistant-owned, not per-end-user, and Telegram never exposes end-user IPs at all) — so real prod `proxyCountry` sourcing (platform/assistant-owned setting vs. existing `AppUser.countryCode` vs. new IP-geolocation infra) is a genuinely open design decision, not something already "laid down." As an explicit test-only stand-in (not the prod answer), `buildBrowserlessCapabilityPolicyMutations` now resolves `country: RU` from the goto/login target hostname (`.ru` / punycode `.рф`) on both the persistent `browserAction` and `startLogin` mutation builders, leaving all other hostnames unchanged. Documented as ADR-139 D8. `@persai/provider-gateway` full suite, lint, format, and typecheck all pass.

- **Fix (ADR-139 D7 addendum — goto reliability + scroll operation, found via live Lavka debugging; local, not pushed).** Live testing on a real persistent profile (Yandex Lavka) showed home/search navigations hard-timing out at 120s while category/product pages loaded fine over the _same_ proxy/session and rendered a real Russian delivery address — proving the sticky residential proxy already works and ruling out a geo/country-IP cause. Root-caused instead of guessed: both browser execution paths defaulted `goto`'s wait condition to `networkidle2`/`networkIdle` ("no more than ~2 connections for 500ms"), which Browserless itself flags "use with caution" and which real SPAs with persistent background traffic (live-tracking sockets, polling, analytics) can never satisfy, turning navigation into a hard failure at the full timeout budget. Fixed by always navigating on `domContentLoaded` plus one bounded 3s settle step (skipped when `optimizeForSpeed` is set) instead of gambling the whole request on network silence, in both the ephemeral `/function` and persistent BrowserQL execution paths. Also added a missing `scroll` operation kind (`{kind:"scroll", selector: string | null}`, selector-into-view or one-viewport-down) since the catalog page's empty/placeholder render was a second, separate gap: virtualized product grids only populate once scrolled into view, and the `act` operation set had no way to scroll. Prompt-owner guidance (`native-tool-projection.ts`, `tool-catalog-data.ts`) now tells the model to use `scroll` when a catalog/feed shows an empty or placeholder list. Documented as ADR-139 D7. Focused tests pass for `@persai/provider-gateway`, `@persai/runtime`, and `@persai/api` browser suites; `@persai/provider-gateway` and `@persai/runtime` typecheck clean.

- **Fix (browser contract root-cause cleanup for persistent-profile `act`; local, not pushed).** Live Lavka verification showed a real contradiction in the PersAI-owned browser contract: the model-facing browser schema/guidance still taught `act` as "CSS selector or keyboard input" and exposed `press`/`Enter` as a normal follow-up move, while the persistent-profile Browserless execution path explicitly rejects `press` with `400 BadRequestException` (`Persistent Browserless sessions do not support press operations reliably`). That mismatch was causing the assistant to choose an operation shape the platform itself disallowed. Fixed the root cause in the model-facing contract instead of adding more post-failure narration: `native-tool-projection.ts` now tells the model to keep saved-profile `act` flows selector-based and explicitly forbids `kind="press"` when `profile` is set; browser catalog guidance now carries the same rule. Focused tests for browser projection and browser catalog guidance pass.

- **Fix (ADR-139 post-implementation audit sweep — provider failure honesty, stale pending reauth reopen, prompt-owner/test tails; local, not pushed).** Independent audit after the main ADR-139 slice found several real follow-through issues and cleaned them before commit: provider-gateway now treats only `op_*` BrowserQL errors as per-operation warnings and fails honestly on capability/setup/extraction errors like `proxy(...)`; persistent-profile `press` is no longer faked via DOM `KeyboardEvent` shims and now rejects explicitly on the Browserless persistent path; API pending-login resolution now verifies the existing live session before narrating `browser_profile_pending_login`, and stale/cold pending rows reopen into same-row `browser_profile_needs_user_reauth` instead of dead-ending on an old `liveUrl`; `completeLogin` now refreshes the pending session when verify fails instead of leaving the stale live URL in place, while infra failures can bubble once refresh also fails; provider delete now treats non-OK cleanup as a real client error instead of silent success; runtime `list_profiles` failures now return structured `browser_failed` results instead of raw exceptions. Prompt/docs/tests were tightened too: browser prompt-owner text now pins "use login only when structured runtime/tool state points there", `API-BOUNDARY.md` and `TEST-PLAN.md` no longer blur product re-auth with legacy Browserless `/reconnect`, and handoff bookkeeping now includes its own updated docs. Full verification after the audit sweep passed: `@persai/api` full suite, `@persai/runtime` full suite, `@persai/provider-gateway` full suite, `@persai/web` full suite, workspace lint, format, and typechecks (`api`, `runtime`, `provider-gateway`, `web`).

- **Change (ADR-139 — Browserless capability policy, persistent `page.elements`, and recovery-owned reauth; local, not pushed).** Opened `ADR-139` and executed the planned local slices on top of ADR-138 without reviving any legacy browser path. Added platform-owned `PersistentBrowserCapabilityPolicy` threading from API to runtime/provider-gateway; persistent profiles now derive `stealth: true` plus sticky residential proxy intent from stable `(assistantId, profileKey)` identity. Provider-gateway now carries that policy into persistent BrowserQL flows, injects the Browserless built-in sticky residential proxy mutation for persistent sessions, fails explicitly on unsupported external proxy policy, and restores normalized interactive `page.elements` for persistent text `snapshot` / `act` while keeping PDF/image outputs honest with `elements: []`. Runtime/catalog prompt owners now teach selector reuse from `page.elements`, forbid invented proxy knobs, forbid ordinary web-chat Browserless live-URL narration, and warn the model not to infer expiry from transient BQL/reconnect failures. Recovery is now product-owned: `assistant-browser-profile.service` reuses the same profile row for re-auth on pending/expired/TTL-elapsed profiles when possible, adds structured reason `browser_profile_needs_user_reauth`, and threads `pendingBrowserLogin` through runtime/browser results so web keeps using the modal/banner path instead of assistant-visible Browserless URLs; Telegram fallback copy now directs the user to PersAI web login rather than raw Browserless live URLs. Full focused browser matrix + API/runtime/provider/web typechecks + workspace lint + format check all passed. Deploy + live acceptance pending.

- **Fix (ADR-138 correction #4 — honest partial-data on BQL per-op errors; kills active-profile `act` 502; local, not pushed).** Live retry after correction #3 (`7f378cc1`) still returned 502 on every `act` with a profile even though `snapshot` worked. Root cause: `runPersistentBrowserActionViaBql` threw `BadGatewayException` whenever the BQL response contained ANY `errors[]`, even when the same 200 response also carried fully-resolved `data` (title/url/text/screenshot). Browserless BQL returns `200 { data: {...partial}, errors: [{path: ["op_N"], message}] }` for per-op runtime failures (e.g. `click`/`type` selector timeout on a SPA that doesn't render the guessed selector) — the legacy `/function` path used try/catch-per-op and returned partial state with a warning; the BQL port broke that contract. Fixed: `data === null` still throws (schema/session failure), but `data !== null && errors.length > 0` now builds a normalized result from data and appends a formatted operation-warning line to the untrusted-content warning. New helper `formatBqlOperationErrors` joins `{ path, message }` entries as `"op_0: Timeout of Nms reached ...; op_1: ..."` prefixed by `Browserless BQL operation warnings: `. Test locks the contract: persistent-profile `act` with mock `{ data: {...populated}, op_0: null, errors: [{ path: ["op_0"], ... }] }` returns successful result with title/finalUrl set and `warning` containing both `Browser-rendered page content is untrusted` and `Browserless BQL operation warnings: op_0: Timeout of 5000ms`. Live BQL probe confirmed pre-fix shape (`200 { data:{...full page state}, errors:[{path:["op_0"],...},{path:["op_1"],...}] }`) — my old handler discarded all the data. AGENTS gate PASS (provider-gateway tests, lint, format:check, provider-gateway typecheck).

- **Fix (ADR-138 correction #3 — real 502 root cause on active profile; BQL schema mismatches + dead-code cutover; pushed `7f378cc1`).** Live retry after correction #2 (`404bea24`) still returned `502` on every `browser` call with `profile: "persai-admin-v4"`. A live BQL probe against the real profile from the api pod uncovered three schema errors inside my `runPersistentBrowserActionViaBql` that provider-gateway was wrapping as 502: (1) `goto(waitUntil: networkAlmostIdle)` — `WaitUntilGoto` has no `networkAlmostIdle` value, only `networkIdle` (`networkAlmostIdle` is a Playwright/Puppeteer JS-API value copied over from the `/function` path); (2) `screenshot(type: PNG|JPEG|WEBP)` — `ScreenshotType` is lower-case; (3) `select(value: String!)` — `select.value` is `StringOrArray!`, not `String!`. Fixed all three plus retired the `/reconnect/{id}` legacy branch that correction #2 had preserved: `startLogin` has never stored `/reconnect/{id}` in prod (every profile row is `/e/{cloud}/session/{id}` or the legacy fixture `/session/{id}`), so the `/function` fallback was dead code and dead tests, and any hand-mutated non-persisting `profileSessionId` now throws `BadRequestException` up-front instead of silently hitting a `/function` path that would 404. Removed `BROWSERLESS_DELETE_SESSION_CODE`, `resolveBrowserlessProfileFunctionEndpoint`, `normalizeProviderSessionPath`. `browserAction` conditional simplified: `profileSessionId !== null` → BQL, else ephemeral `/function`; `deleteSession` early-returns for non-persisting shapes. Tests updated (removed two `/reconnect/session-abc123` `/function` blocks, added `assert.rejects(BadRequestException)`, renumbered `requests[N]` 6..10 without gaps; runtime fixtures `/reconnect/session-1` → `/session/session-1`). Live probe evidence: pre-fix `mutation … networkAlmostIdle …` → 200 with `errors: [{message:"Value \"networkAlmostIdle\" does not exist in \"WaitUntilGoto\" enum. Did you mean \"networkIdle\"?"}]`; post-fix `mutation … networkIdle …` → 200 with full authenticated `pageText` from the real chat session, plus `screenshot(type: png|jpeg|webp)` and `pdf(printBackground: true)` returning valid base64 payloads. AGENTS gate PASS (provider-gateway + runtime tests, lint, format:check, provider-gateway/runtime typecheck).

- **Fix (ADR-138 correction #2 — persistent-session `browser-action` via BQL; kills active-profile 502; local, not pushed).** Live probe on deployed dev cluster after `89c2e1fc` proved that while `verifySession` was fixed, `browser-action` for a persistent profile still routed through `POST .../session/connect/{id}/function`, and Browserless returned `502 Bad Gateway { message: "Not Found: Please verify the endpoint URL, ..." }` because persistent connect-sessions have no `/function` REST endpoint at all — only BrowserQL on `.../session/bql/{id}`. Provider-gateway now sends `browser-action` for persistent profiles through a dynamically-built BQL mutation: `reject` (when `optimizeForSpeed`) → `goto(url, waitUntil, timeout)` → operations chain (`click`, pre-cleared `type` via `evaluate`, `select`, `waitForSelector`, `waitForTimeout`, `press` via synthesized `KeyboardEvent`) → `title/url` metadata → format-branch extractor (`text/screenshot/pdf`). Result coerced back into the same `ProviderGatewayBrowserActionResult` shape as the `/function` path (`elements: []` on the persistent path — interactive-elements probe can be added later). Ephemeral sessions and legacy `/reconnect/{id}` profiles still use `/function`. Test flipped from `/function` fixture to BQL fixture for `/session/session-login`; asserts URL `.../session/bql/session-login`, BQL query contains `goto` + `pageText: text { text }`, variables carry the URL, and result carries the mocked title/finalUrl/content. Live BQL probe against `persai-admin` session (which was 502-ing) confirmed the session is authenticated (`title=PersAI`, real chat text visible) and BQL end-to-end works (screenshot ~7.6KB, PDF ~1.1KB). AGENTS gate PASS (lint, format:check, provider-gateway/api/web typecheck, provider-browser test).

- **Fix (ADR-138 correction — Browserless persistent-session verify via BQL + preserve `/e/{cloudEndpointId}/` prefix; local, not pushed).** Live dev cluster proved two Composer-era ADR-138 seam bugs. First, `POST /session` on multi-cloud Browserless plans returns `stop = https://host/e/{cloudEndpointId}/session/{id}`, but `startLogin` stored only `/session/{id}` and dropped the cloudEndpointId; every downstream BQL / connect / stop derivation then hit a host that could not route the persistent session. Second, `verifySession` used the Browserless `/function` REST endpoint, which returns **404 Not Found** for persistent connect-sessions — the durable liveness probe for a persistent session is a BrowserQL schema query on the per-session `session.browserQL` endpoint. Provider-gateway now parses `session.stop` into a canonical pathname (`/e/{cloud}/session/{id}` when present, legacy `/session/{id}` otherwise), stores it as `providerSessionId`, and derives stop/BQL paths off a shared `persistingSessionPath` helper. `verifySession` targets `.../session/bql/{id}` with `POST { query: "query { __typename }" }`, treats `data.__typename === "Query"` as live, and surfaces the first BQL error message on non-2xx. Removed dead `BROWSERLESS_VERIFY_SESSION_CODE` sandbox script and dead `extractProviderSessionId` helper. Test rewritten to assert stored path + BQL probe URL + `__typename` body. AGENTS gate PASS (repo lint, format:check, provider-gateway/api/web typecheck, focused provider-browser + ADR-138 api tests 14/14).

## 2026-07-06

- **Fix (browser login modal — stable Browserless `index.html` proxy entry path).** Final live root cause: the modal iframe could navigate to `/api/browser-login-live/{assistantId}/{profileId}?i=...` without a trailing slash, while Browserless `client.js` computes the WS URL as `url.pathname + id`. That produced `/profileId{i}` instead of `/profileId/{i}`, so the live client exhausted reconnects and rendered the black `Connection lost` screen. Web modal URLs now use `/api/browser-login-live/{assistantId}/{profileId}/index.html?...`, which Browserless client normalizes into the correct WS path. Live manual check on the deployed proxy with the corrected entry path produced `wsState=1`, `reconnectAttempts=0`, and a non-black canvas. Focused 18 browser-login tests + repo lint/format + API/web typecheck PASS.

- **Fix (browser login modal — strip app auth headers from Browserless WS upstream).** Follow-up live check after `d2f03e93`: direct Browserless live links work when the user's local browser uses VPN, confirming Browserless is healthy and the PersAI proxy remains required for non-VPN/Russia access. The proxied path can return a valid `101 Switching Protocols` through GCLB to HTTP/1.1 clients, while the in-browser modal still closed as `1006`; the remaining browser-only difference is the PersAI/Clerk cookie-bearing WS upgrade. `apps/web/server.mjs` now keeps cookies for the internal liveUrl resolve, then strips `cookie` and `authorization` before forwarding the raw WS upgrade to Browserless. `node --check` + 18 focused browser-login web tests PASS.

- **Fix (browser login modal — live WS proxy reconnect loop / black modal; pushed `d2f03e93`).** Pod-proven diagnosis: server-side `proxy.ws` → Browserless is reliable (101 on a fresh session regardless of cookie/`permessage-deflate`/xfwd/500ms delay); prior 400s were session-TTL expiry. Real failure was end-to-end: `server.mjs` had **no `proxy.on('error')`** listener (upstream failures became a silent 1006) and re-resolved the upstream live URL on **every** reconnect (internal fetch + Clerk `getToken` ~1.5s), so the live client's reconnects kept losing the handshake race → permanent black modal. Hardened `apps/web/server.mjs`: `proxy.on('error')` (log + 502 + close), client upgrade-socket error handler, 30s TTL upstream-URL cache with invalidate-on-error + ws error callback, `proxyTimeout: 20000`. `node --check` + 18 browser-login web tests + web typecheck/lint/prettier PASS. Deploy + live acceptance pending.

- **Fix (browser login modal — `0.0.0.0` origin; pushed `679d78f4`).** Pod-proven: trailing-slash redirect used `requestUrl.toString()` inside web pod → `https://0.0.0.0:3000/api/browser-login-live/...`; `buildProxyPublicBase` lacked `Host`/`PERSAI_WEB_BASE_URL` fallback. Removed BFF trailing-slash redirect; added `resolveProxyPublicOrigin` + client URL normalize; `PERSAI_WEB_BASE_URL` on web helm env. Full gate PASS.

- **Fix (files vision re-view + model instructions; pushed `679d78f4`).** `files.preview` on image/PDF uses plan visual byte limit (ignores model `maxBytes:4096`). Catalog/bootstrap/native projection/Working Files teach current-message vision vs `files.preview` for earlier chat/workspace paths.

- **Fix (ADR-138 — Browserless Session API login + REST artifact routing).** `startLogin` uses `POST /session` + BQL `liveURL` (not CDP in `/function`). Ephemeral `snapshot` pdf/png/jpeg/webp (no `snapshotSelector`) use REST `/pdf` or `/screenshot`; profile/`snapshotSelector` keep session `/function`. Legacy `/reconnect/{id}` still supported. Profile reuse via `/session/connect/{id}/function` remains **unverified against Browserless public docs** — live smoke pending.

- **Change (ADR-138 Wave 2 — audit A+B + image screenshots S7; pushed `d3bdd6f9`).** Chat-scoped stale `pending_login` cleanup; mid-stream login modal gated on `toolRequestedAction === "login"`; browser `snapshot` supports `format: png|jpeg|webp` with `snapshotSelector`/`fullPage` through provider-gateway screenshot + shared outbound artifact pipeline. S8 download / S9 upload planned as ADR-138 continuation.

Media-job recovery runs use a fresh idempotency key when `acceptedProviderTask` is present (no replay of the first failed receipt). ## 2026-07-04

- **Cleanup (Working Files):** removed the `last delivered result` row marker; `last delivered` remains the single chat-delivery anchor. Future source-input marking deferred.
- **Cleanup (ADR-134 hygiene):** removed dead attachment-metadata semantic-summary helpers, dropped orphan `upload_micro_description` scheduler lease key, aligned `API-BOUNDARY.md` to path-keyed `workspace_file_micro_description_jobs`, extended register-path summary invalidation, and extended `xlsx` to `current source` mime coverage.
- **Fix (ADR-134 follow-up — WF cleanup + micro-description invalidation + version markers).** Runtime Working Files now renders only the session file list plus footer guidance; legacy `DOC_*` / `LAST_DELIVERED_FILE` blocks removed in favor of row markers (`last delivered`, `current source`, `v{N}`). Manifest upsert clears stale `shortDescription` on `replace` or `contentHash` change and force-re-enqueues the micro-description job. Internal `short-descriptions` batch lookup also returns `documentVersionNumber` for registered pdf/docx/xlsx paths. Golden prompt snapshot + register-attachment test mocks updated for CI.
- **Fix (shell document delivery integrity — content-hash diff, one v+1 per turn).** Sandbox shell diff now scans only the current session root, treats changed outputs as new path or byte/hash delta (mtime ignored), and emits `contentHash` on `producedFiles`. API metadata registration skips `revise_document` when `contentHash` is unchanged and collapses multiple shell revises in the same user turn into one in-place version update. Runtime passes `contentHash` through shell sync and auto-attaches only shell registrations with `contentChanged: true`. Prompt owners clarify simple XLSX via `document`, complex XLSX/office edits via one `shell` script per turn, and `files.attach` only for this turn's target outputs.
- **Change (ADR-134 — path-based workspace file micro-descriptions; S1–S7 landed locally, not pushed).** Restored the semantic index under ADR-128/133 path identity: the sole durable field is `workspace_file_metadata.shortDescription` (no `AssistantFile` revival, no `attachment.metadata` mirror). New leased queue `workspace_file_micro_description_jobs` keyed by `(workspaceId, path)` replaces the retired `assistant_upload_micro_description_jobs` table. One three-layer write pipeline: deterministic STT/text_extract → sync upsert; `buildGeneratedFileSemanticSummary` → sync upsert with source `generation_request` when informative; otherwise background cheap-LLM job via `WorkspaceFileMicroDescriptionService`. Enqueue wired at web upload/stage, inbound channel media, runtime metadata upsert, outbound delivery, and attach registration; project-mode uploads always enqueue; ordinary/B2C uploads respect `routerPolicy.analyzeUploadsOnB2cUpload`; model-generated paths bypass the B2C gate. Working Files batch-joins manifest descriptions into `semanticSummaryHint`. Restored model-facing `files.search` as the seventh `files` action with API `POST /api/v1/internal/runtime/files/search` tokenized match over path, basename, and `shortDescription`. Migration `20260704140000_adr134_workspace_file_micro_description_jobs`. Focused verification: lint + api/web/runtime typecheck green; focused micro-description + search tests 5/5; `format:check` red on 11 touched files pending prettier. Deploy + live acceptance pending.
- **Fix (document inspect Slice 2 — shell overwrite → version bump + honest auto-attach).** Session `shell` now snapshots visible `pdf`/`docx`/`xlsx` before/after pod exec and emits changed paths as sandbox `producedFiles` with `/workspace/...` storage paths. Runtime sandbox sync upserts those outputs through the existing metadata registration seam and reads back `{ registered, versionNumber, bumped, isOverwrite }`. End-of-turn auto-attach applies PROD shell rules: overwrite (`v+1`) always attaches; exactly one new `v1` doc auto-attaches; multiple new `v1` docs in the same turn do not (model uses `files.attach(final)`). Non-shell produced outputs keep prior attach-all behavior. Slice 1 (project-tree removal + `inspect.editMethod`) remains in the same uncommitted tree.
- **Fix (document inspect Slice 1 — remove project-tree; add editMethod).** `document.inspect` no longer runs silent `DocumentWorkspaceExtractionService` / `projects/doc-*` allocation. Inspect returns `editMethod` (`shell_native` for uploaded PDF/DOCX/XLSX without sibling `.md`, `render_from_markdown` when that sibling exists), optional sibling `*.extracted.md` for PDF OCR when the text layer is empty, and drops imported-project comparison summaries. Deleted dead extract endpoint/service/runtime client and runtime-contract project-layout helpers. `document.render` now rejects in-place replacement of an existing uploaded office file without sibling Markdown. Bootstrap/tool-catalog prompt owners teach `inspect.editMethod` instead of project-tree mechanics. Verification: repo lint, `format:check`, api/web/runtime typecheck; focused inspection + runtime document tests green. Slice 2 (shell overwrite → v+1 + attach) intentionally deferred.

## 2026-07-03

- **Fix (session pod filesystem — pod + GCS are source of truth; no stale push).** Session `runInPod` no longer pushes the control-plane workspace tree into the pod before `shell` / `exec` / `document.render` / `document.convert` jobs. That push was clobbering files already written by `files.write` (pod + GCS) with stale sandbox-local copies, producing byte-identical PDFs and shell reads of old content. Session jobs now execute directly against the live pod filesystem, pull results afterward for artifact staging only, and write transient job inputs (`.render-input.html`, `.document-code.py`, sources/sidecars) directly into the pod via `stagingFiles`. Ephemeral pods still use push/pull. Focused verification: `@persai/sandbox` `exec-pod-bridge.service.test.ts` + `sandbox.service.test.ts` (48/48), `@persai/sandbox` typecheck. All active visible workspace path builders now use `Assistant.id` (UUID) as the `/workspace/assistants/<segment>/...` segment instead of `Assistant.handle` / display slug. Contract builders renamed `assistantStableKey` → `assistantId`; API upload/delivery/manifest/chat-gallery widen roots, runtime `files`/`document` tools, sandbox default visible root, and `assistant_subtree` GC lease metadata were aligned. `assistantHandle` remains only for bash/exec pod hints, not filesystem paths. Full verification gate passed (`lint`, `format:check`, api/web/runtime/sandbox/runtime-contract typecheck, focused path/GC/manifest/files/document tests). Residual: existing GCS objects under handle-based prefixes are not auto-migrated; live acceptance after deploy must confirm new writes land under `assistants/<uuid>/sessions/<runtimeSessionId>/`.
- **Fix (ADR-133 file creation contract — runtime owns current-session paths).** `files.write` no longer requires the model to construct `/workspace/assistants/<assistantId>/sessions/<sessionId>/...` for new visible files. The model-facing contract now supports `requestedName` or a relative path for current-session writes; `RuntimeFilesToolService` resolves those through the real runtime `assistantId` + `sessionId`, canonicalizes stale `/workspace/assistants/current/sessions/current/...` placeholders back to the real session root, and rejects foreign model-authored session-root writes before sandbox execution. Files prompt owners and native schema now forbid spelling assistant/session IDs for new writes. Focused verification passed: runtime files tests, native tool projection tests, API tool-catalog/runtime-policy/golden prompt tests.
- **Fix (ADR-133 document output contract cutover — model supplies filename only, runtime owns session-root path).** `document.render` and `document.convert` no longer depend on a model-authored absolute `outputPath` under `/workspace/...`. The model-facing contract now uses `requestedName` (filename only) for new outputs; `RuntimeDocumentToolService` resolves the real destination under the current session root with the actual `assistantId` + runtime session id, appends the expected extension when omitted, and rejects nested/absolute names so placeholders like `/workspace/assistants/current/sessions/current/...` cannot become live document paths.
- **Fix (ADR-133 document pipeline cleanup — single-owner registration seam, no legacy direct register).** `document.render` / `document.convert` no longer run the old runtime-side inspect + `registerDocumentVersion()` enrichment path after persisting bytes. Instead, `RuntimeDocumentToolService` now threads `sourceUserMessageText` / `sourceUserMessageCreatedAt` into the existing metadata upsert seam so visible `pdf` / `xlsx` / `docx` writes register exactly once at the API-owned overwrite seam. `RuntimeSandboxToolService` now mirrors shell-produced document outputs only when the path is an active hierarchical descendant (`session` / `assistant shared` / `workspace shared`), so retired flat-root paths like `/workspace/report.pdf` or non-descendant assistant roots no longer re-enter document registration through sandbox output sync. `DocumentWorkspaceVersionRegistrationService` now rejects retired flat-root and other non-active paths for `outputPath`, `workspaceProjectPath`, `sourceManifestPath`, and `inspectionPath` using the ADR-133 active-path helpers instead of the broader legacy normalizers. Focused verification passed: runtime document tests, new runtime sandbox-path test, API document version-registration tests, `@persai/runtime` typecheck, `@persai/api` typecheck, and targeted prettier check/write on touched files.
- **Fix (API CrashLoop hotfix).** Removed two unused optional constructor parameters from `RegisterChatAttachmentService` that emitted `Function`/`Object` Nest DI metadata in the production build and caused the new `api:6c9505eb...` pod to crash at startup with `UnknownDependenciesException` on dependency index `[4]`. Verification: `@persai/api` typecheck, targeted attachment registration tests, `@persai/api` build, compiled `design:paramtypes` inspection, `@persai/api` lint, plus repo `format:check`.
- **Fix (ADR-133 final audit tail cleanup).** Removed the last active model-facing `files.list` scope tail from runtime: `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/runtime-files-tool.service.ts` no longer parses or validates a hidden `scope` argument, `FilesListRequest` no longer carries user-supplied scope, and manifest list scope is derived only from the chosen path plus the current assistant/session roots. `packages/runtime-contract/src/index.ts` comments around `RuntimeTelegramChannelContext`, `RuntimeChannelContext`, `PERSAI_RUNTIME_FILES_TOOL_ACTIONS`, and `RuntimeFilesToolItem` now describe the active session-first path truth instead of future migration or scope-aware behavior. Focused verification passed: `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/runtime exec tsx test/runtime-files-tool.service.test.ts`, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/runtime-contract run typecheck`, and `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/runtime run typecheck`.
- **Fix (ADR-133 final audit cleanup landed locally; pushed).** Independent audit follow-up cleaned active flat-root teaching from product-visible API/web/sandbox fixtures and comments, so positive examples now stay on hierarchical session-root paths. The sandbox direct `workspaceFileWrite` control-plane path also now rejects retired root-flat writes such as `/workspace/report.pdf` before quota/pod/GCS work and records the denial audit; full verification passed before push (`lint`, `format:check`, repo `typecheck`, repo `test`, and `test:ci-detect-affected`).
- **Change (ADR-133 Slice 5 web/UI/docs closure landed locally; not pushed).** The assistant-settings Files gallery and its public list route now use `session | assistant | workspace` semantics, default to current-session provenance, and widen by the real hierarchical path roots instead of the older public `chat | workspace` split. `apps/web/app/app/assistant-api-client.ts`, `workspace-files-gallery.tsx`, `assistant-settings.tsx`, and EN/RU messages now agree on `Current session` / `This assistant` / `Workspace` labels, with assistant-wide fallback when no active chat is open; `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/list-chat-workspace-files.service.ts` now scopes rows by session root or assistant root rather than by the retired public split. Active web/API fixtures and docs were cleaned so positive examples no longer teach flat-root `/workspace/*.pdf|txt|csv|docx|xlsx` behavior. Focused verification passed: `@persai/api` `list-chat-workspace-files.service` + `media-attachment.controller` tests, `@persai/web` `assistant-api-client` + `assistant-settings` tests, `@persai/api` typecheck, `@persai/web` typecheck, and repo `format:check`. - **Change (ADR-133 Slice 4 runtime/prompt-owner cutover landed locally; not pushed).** Runtime `files` / `document` tools, the Working Files developer block, native tool projection, bootstrap/tool-catalog prompt owners, and golden/prompt guard tests now teach the hierarchical session-first filesystem truth: default current-session root `/workspace/assistants/<assistantStableKey>/sessions/<sessionId>/...`, assistant/workspace widening by ordinary path choice, and no active `workspace_shared` / `crossScope:true` / flat `/workspace/<path>` fallback. Positive runtime fixtures were rewritten to hierarchical session-root or explicit widen paths, active runtime `files.write` compatibility for legacy `mode:"overwrite"` was removed, the earlier ADR-133 sandbox lint blocker in `apps/sandbox/src/sandbox.service.ts` was fixed, and focused verification passed across runtime tool tests, API prompt-owner tests, repo lint, `format:check`, and runtime/api/web typechecks.
- **Change (ADR-133 Slice 3 landed locally; not pushed).** API-owned manifest/upload/delivery/document behavior now follows the hierarchical session-first workspace model end-to-end for this slice: uploads/staged/inbound media, visible delivery paths, metadata upserts, manifest listing, and visible document registration all resolve or validate against `/workspace/assistants/<assistantStableKey>/sessions/<sessionId>/...`, while retired flat root ingress such as `/workspace/report.pdf` is rejected. Active API file-list scope vocabulary now uses `chat | assistant | workspace`, chat gallery filtering no longer depends on `/workspace/chats/...`, document default project allocation no longer falls back to a global `/workspace/projects` root for active sources, and Prisma/API/sandbox GC lease vocabulary is synchronized on `session_subtree | assistant_subtree | workspace_subtree` via migration `20260703132500_adr133_slice3_gc_lease_kind_rename`. Focused verification passed across API, runtime-contract, and sandbox seams: targeted `@persai/api` `tsx` suites for manifest, chat file listing, registration, extraction, inspection, version registration, delivery, and GC producers; `@persai/api` typecheck; `@persai/runtime-contract` tests + typecheck; sandbox GC test + typecheck; `prisma validate`; `prisma generate`; and repo `format:check`. - **Change (ADR-133 Slice 2 sandbox + GCS cutover landed locally; not pushed).** Sandbox execution now defaults to the hierarchical ADR-133 session root instead of the old flat `/workspace/` behavior. `shell` / `exec` cwd, `grep` / `glob` default paths, basename-only sandbox writes, and hot control-plane writes now resolve through `/workspace/assistants/<assistantStableKey>/sessions/<sessionId>/...` when a runtime session exists, with assistant-shared fallback only for sessionless control-plane cases. Sandbox persisted workspace object keys now mirror visible hierarchical paths in GCS, local/pod workspace materialization preserves the full tree, and sandbox GC/audit semantics now report session/assistant/workspace subtree cleanup instead of stale `chat_scratch` / `assistant_outbound` / `workspace_shared` wording. Flat explicit root writes such as `/workspace/flat.txt` are now rejected at the sandbox control-plane boundary. Focused verification passed: `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/sandbox exec tsx --test test/workspace-file-bridge.service.test.ts test/workspace-gc.service.test.ts test/sandbox.service.test.ts`, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/sandbox run typecheck`, and `corepack pnpm run format:check`. API manifest/upload/delivery/document-path migration and model-facing runtime/web prompt rewrites remain for later ADR-133 slices.

- **Change (ADR-133 Slice 1 shared path contract landed locally; no behavior migration, not pushed).** `packages/runtime-contract/src/index.ts` now owns the first shared session-first workspace path contract: canonical constants for `/workspace`, `/workspace/assistants/<assistantStableKey>`, `/workspace/assistants/<assistantStableKey>/sessions/<sessionId>`, assistant/workspace shared roots, path-safe segment validation/sanitization, and pure visible-path classification helpers that mark `/workspace/report.pdf` as `rootFlatFile` and `/workspace/chats/...` / `/workspace/projects/...` as stale invalid paths for the active ADR-133 model. Added focused pure coverage in `packages/runtime-contract/test/workspace-path-contract.test.ts`, updated `docs/ADR/133-session-first-hierarchical-workspace-filesystem.md` and `docs/TEST-PLAN.md`, and corrected stale shared-contract/runtime-bundle comments so flat/outbound/project wording is historical-only. This slice does **not** migrate sandbox, API, runtime, or web default-path behavior yet.

- **Docs (ADR-133 opened — session-first hierarchical workspace filesystem; orchestrated program, no code yet).** Opened `docs/ADR/133-session-first-hierarchical-workspace-filesystem.md` as the founder-directed clean filesystem program. The active target is no longer the flat ADR-128 `/workspace/<file>` model: new working files default to `/workspace/assistants/<assistantStableKey>/sessions/<sessionId>/...`, assistants widen to their assistant root and then to `/workspace/` by ordinary paths, and implementation must remove stale model-facing filesystem vocabulary (`/workspace/chats`, `/workspace/projects`, `/workspace/input`, `/workspace/outbound`, `workspace_shared`, `crossScope:true`, and flat `/workspace/<path>` teaching) rather than preserving compatibility shims. The ADR records the parent-orchestrator execution model, GPT-5.4/Sonnet implementation-subagent slices, read-only Slice 0 ledger, sandbox/API/runtime/web/doc/test blast radius, and acceptance gates. `AGENTS.md` now points to ADR-133 as an additional active orchestration program. No runtime/API/web code changed in this docs-only opening step.

- **Fix (document versioning + chat file binding; overwrite is the only version bump trigger).** Reworked the visible document workflow so version changes now happen only on real writes to an occupied `pdf` / `xlsx` / `docx` workspace path, regardless of whether the bytes came from `document.render`, `document.convert`, `files.write(replace=true)`, or shell-produced artifacts observed after sandbox completion. `files.attach` no longer registers document versions and now only links the current registered document identity for that path; `document.inspect` no longer gates version registration. The internal workspace metadata upsert path now carries chat/user context and becomes the single registration seam for visible document outputs, while shell/exec mirrors produced workspace document files into that same seam. On the web side, the Assistant settings `Этот чат` gallery is now bound to the active chat/thread instead of the assistant's latest chat, and document-card download URLs are `versionId`-aware so stale cards no longer silently open the current file bytes. Verification: root `lint`, root `format:check`, root `typecheck`, Helm lint/template, focused API/runtime/web tests for document registration/delivery/chat binding, plus full runtime files/document/turn-execution suites and root `build` all passed. Residual full-workflow blockers remain external to this slice: local `prisma:migrate:check` fails because the local database already contains failed migration `20260501120000_adr079_knowledge_skills_foundation`, and the existing full `@persai/web` vitest suite remains red on unrelated timeout-heavy tests under `pnpm run test` / `pnpm run test:step2`.

- **Docs (ADR-130 closure sweep landed locally; not pushed).** `docs/ADR/130-prompt-layering-cache-discipline-and-lazy-context-lookup.md` now marks ADR-130 **Closed locally 2026-07-03**, records the landed follow-through slices (7, 8, 10), notes the founder-directed skip of Slice 9 under the post-ADR-132 tool surface, and updates the next step to rollout/live regression. `docs/ARCHITECTURE.md` now states ADR-130 as closed locally and captures the final prompt-owner truth: compact `<enabled_skills>`, explicit `memory_protocol` / `response_contract`, current-step-only `<persai_active_scenario>`, single-owner `<tool_usage_policy>`, and a truthful admin Prompt Constructor. `docs/API-BOUNDARY.md` now pins `knowledge_search` / `knowledge_fetch` / `quota_status` as the canonical model-facing names and clarifies that `memory_search` / `memory_get` / `persai_tool_quota_status` are hidden alias/remap rows, not competing prompt owners. `docs/DATA-MODEL.md` now records the same hidden-row vs canonical-owner split next to the `assistant_chat_messages.tool_exchanges` ADR-130 truth.

## 2026-07-02

- **Fix (ADR-132 render hotfix — explicit output path in generated document programs; landed locally, not pushed).** Fixed the live `document.render` failure `NameError: name 'PERSAI_OUTPUT_PATH' is not defined`. The ADR-132 runtime-generated PDF/DOCX/XLSX/convert Python programs now embed the normalized `outputPath` directly as `OUTPUT_PATH = Path("/workspace/...")` instead of depending on a nonexistent sandbox global/env variable. Focused runtime document tests assert that generated programs no longer contain `PERSAI_OUTPUT_PATH` and that PDF, XLSX, and convert paths use the requested workspace output path.

- **Fix (ADR-132 repair — document delivery decoupled from metadata enrichment; landed locally, not pushed).** Corrected the live PDF regression where `/workspace/test.pdf` existed in the workspace but did not appear in chat because `files.attach` for doc-extension files still synchronously depended on inspect/register/documentLink enrichment. `RegisterChatAttachmentService` now creates the chat attachment row first after normal file/chat preflight, then runs inspect → version registration → documentLink update as best-effort enrichment; enrichment failure logs a warning but does not drop delivery. `DocumentWorkspaceVersionRegistrationService` now treats `workspaceProjectPath`, `projectManifestPath`, and source-manifest facts as nullable metadata rather than required project-layout truth; root-level `/workspace/*.pdf|docx|xlsx` outputs register when inspection metadata exists and otherwise still deliver as attachments. Runtime `document.render` / `document.convert` no longer materialize active `project.json` files for authored/convert outputs and no longer pass parent directories as delivery gates; active runtime/API guidance no longer teaches `document.extract` / `document.register_version` / active document project workflow. Focused tests now cover doc-extension `files.attach` delivering despite metadata-enrichment failure, root-level registration without `project.json`, sibling-MD Case A revision, and stale-verb rejection. Verification green: focused API/runtime document tests, API/runtime typechecks, repo lint, format check, API typecheck, and web typecheck. No push.

- **Change (ADR-130 Slice 6b — D8 replay path landed locally; not committed, not pushed).** Added bounded cross-turn tool-history replay on the runtime/provider path using the already-landed server-only `assistant_chat_messages.tool_exchanges` JSONB seam. `ProviderGatewayTextMessage` now carries optional `priorToolExchanges`, the runtime hydrator now selects/parses persisted `tool_exchanges`, caps replay to the last 3 prior assistant turns under a deterministic ~2000-token total budget, truncates each replayed `tool_result` to a top-marked tail-preserving 2000-char window, replaces binary results with `[binary content omitted]`, caps serialized `tool_use` arguments to 600 chars, and never attaches replay to the current inbound user message. Provider-gateway clients for Anthropic/OpenAI/DeepSeek now reuse their existing native exchange renderers for both replayed historical exchanges and the live in-turn `toolHistory` loop, emitting the replay immediately before the owning assistant turn's final text. Focused/runtime cache guards were extended to prove deterministic replay, correct per-provider ordering, current-turn `toolHistory` preservation, and stable-prefix isolation. Full local verification passed: `@persai/provider-gateway` typecheck/test, `@persai/runtime` typecheck/test, `@persai/api` typecheck, `@persai/web` typecheck, repo lint, and `format:check`. `@persai/runtime-contract` has no `build` script, so there was no package build step to run.

API internal relay (`assistant-runtime.facade.ts`, sync/stream/Telegram runtime clients, `persistAssistantMessage`, and the chat repository) now threads and writes `toolExchanges` directly to the dedicated column when non-empty, while keeping `metadata` limited to the existing client-safe fields (`workingNotes`, `toolInvocations`, discovered file paths, partial/truncated status). - **Change (ADR-132 Slice 3 — Case A/B editing paths locked; server-side document identity resolution; legacy-verb rejection tests; landed locally `3462e521` + fix `54e5049d`, push=deploy pending founder go).** Slice 3 delivers the two mechanically-distinct edit paths from ADR-132 D3 without any `edit` verb and locks their contract. **Case A guidance** added to `native-tool-projection.ts`, `tool-catalog-data.ts`, and `bootstrap-preset-data.ts` — a four-step recipe the model follows to revise an authored document: `files.read(<siblingMarkdownPath>)`, edit the Markdown, `files.write(<siblingMarkdownPath>, newContent, replace: true)`, `document.render({ contentPath: <siblingMarkdownPath>, format: <same>, outputPath: <same as before> })`. **Case B guidance** was already present ("`shell` + `openpyxl` / `python-docx` / `weasyprint` + `files.attach(path)`"); Slice 3 does not rewrite it. **Rejection tests** added for the removed legacy verbs `edit` and `register_version` at parser time (symmetric to the existing `extract` rejection from Slice 1) — the tool now hard-rejects all three at the parser and cannot silently alias them to a working verb. **Case A property test** at the runtime level asserts that repeat renders at the same `outputPath` bump to `v+1` and that the edited Markdown content flows into the render program's `contentPath` on the second call. **Case B property test** (extending `register-chat-attachment.service.test.ts`) asserts that `files.attach` at an existing document path auto-registers a new version with `descriptorMode: "revise_document"` against the same `docId`. **ADR-119 golden prompt snapshot regenerated** for the added Case A guidance line. **Correction (`54e5049d`) — server-side document identity resolution:** the initial Slice 3 mechanical fix used an in-memory `Map` on `RuntimeDocumentToolService` keyed on `(workspaceId, outputPath)` to remember the docId across renders. This was architecturally fragile — did not survive pod restarts and was not shared across instances, so repeat renders hitting a different runtime pod would still mint a fresh document. Corrected by resolving document identity **server-side** in `DocumentWorkspaceVersionRegistrationService`: when the runtime calls the internal register endpoint with `docId=null`, the API now looks up an existing `assistantDocument` whose current version metadata carries the same `outputPath` and, if found, treats the call as `revise_document` against that docId. This is the same query pattern already used by `RegisterChatAttachmentService` for the `files.attach` path (kept co-located in each service to preserve wiring); historical version bytes remain immutable in GCS keyed on `(path, version)`. Runtime is stateless again: it always sends `{docId: null, descriptorMode: null}` from `finalizeDocumentDelivery`. Added an API-side test `resolves existing docId from outputPath when caller passes docId=null (Case A / render revision)` that exercises the new lookup end-to-end. Files touched (Slice 3 + correction): `apps/api/prisma/{bootstrap-preset-data.ts, tool-catalog-data.ts}`, `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/document-workspace-version-registration.service.ts` (+`resolveExistingDocIdByOutputPath`), `apps/api/test/{document-workspace-version-registration.service.test.ts, register-chat-attachment.service.test.ts}`, `apps/api/test/fixtures/adr119-golden-prompt-snapshot.expected.txt` (regenerated), `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/{native-tool-projection.ts, runtime-document-tool.service.ts}`, `apps/runtime/test/runtime-document-tool.service.test.ts`. Full AGENTS gate green + full `@persai/api` + `@persai/runtime` suites green (13 runtime document tests including the 4 new Slice 3 tests; 5 API version-registration tests including the new lookup test).

- **Change (ADR-132 Slice 2 — document identity registry + honest delivery, document-scoped walls removed; landed locally `0bc56ca2`, push=deploy pending founder go).** The API-side of ADR-132 lands the two D4 registry triggers and removes the document-scoped delivery walls, without touching the general workspace/session file guards. **Trigger 1 — `document.render` / `document.convert`:** on successful persist the runtime auto-registers the output path as a new version of the same document identity (repeat renders/converts at the same `outputPath` increment `v+1`, historical bytes preserved in GCS keyed on `(path, version)`, latest workspace bytes serve the latest version); if the subsequent inspect or register step fails, the tool result now stays `rendered` / `converted` with a `warning` (`auto_register_skipped:<code>` / `inspect_skipped:<code>`) instead of collapsing to `skipped` — the file was written and delivered, so we surface that honestly rather than lie about the outcome. **Trigger 2 — `files.attach(path)` on a document-extension file (pdf/docx/xlsx):** `RegisterChatAttachmentService` now auto-runs the same server-side inspect → `register_version` chain (via `revise_document` when a prior docId exists) instead of hard-rejecting on the previously "blocked" outcome, then re-resolves the ready chat link and delivers exactly once. **Removed document-scoped walls** (scope strictly document-owned code paths per ADR-132 D6, ADR-131 workspace-scope guards untouched): the `blocked` outcome and the entire `validateVisibleWorkspaceDocumentDeliverable` gate (`unsupported_output_format` / `project_path_required` / `project_output_mismatch` / `project_manifest_missing` / `provenance_missing` / `inspect_missing` / `inspect_output_mismatch` / `inspect_format_mismatch`) are deleted from `document-workspace-deliverable-gating.ts`; the manual `document.register_version` nudge is replaced with `InternalServerErrorException` on genuine failure paths so we never pretend the model can rescue an internal server error by re-calling a verb that no longer exists; a `fallbackWorkspaceProjectPath` (parent directory of the storage path) is used when the workspace-facts lookup returns null so a project-owned output is still auto-registered; `assistant-document-job.service.ts` loses 27 lines of blocked-status classifier logic that no longer has a caller. **New runtime seam** (`turn-delivery-facts.ts` + `turn-execution.service.ts`): document-render/convert deliveries record delivery facts so the exactly-once dedup keeps working across the new auto-register path. **Tests** rewritten around: repeat versioning (v1 → v2 same outputPath), attach-triggered auto-registration on a naked doc-extension file, honest-warning semantics on inspect/register failure, no-wall delivery on legacy project outputs that lack the older provenance shape, and preservation of ADR-131 cross-chat protection. Explicitly out of scope in this slice: sandbox scope guards, `files.list`/`files.read`/`files.preview`/`files.attach`/`files.delete` cross-scope semantics, `hardDeleteChat` orphaning, and any schema changes — all reserved to ADR-131 addendum territory. Files touched: `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/{assistant-document-job.service.ts, document-workspace-deliverable-gating.ts, document-workspace-version-registration.service.ts, register-chat-attachment.service.ts}`, matching tests in `apps/api/test`, `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/{runtime-document-tool.service.ts, turn-delivery-facts.ts, turn-execution.service.ts}`, `apps/runtime/test/runtime-document-tool.service.test.ts` (+304 lines of new coverage). Full AGENTS gate green + full `@persai/api` + `@persai/runtime` suites green.

- **Change (ADR-132 Slice 1 — atomic cutover of the document surface to inspect / render / convert; landed locally `2ce5ab88`, push=deploy pending founder go and ADR-130 completion).** Under the newly opened ADR-132 (`d086c530` + Slice 0 ledger `99e58c67`), the model-facing `document` verbs are now exactly three: `inspect(path)`, `render({content|contentPath, format, style?, template?, outputPath})`, `convert({source, targetFormat, outputPath?})`. **Deleted verbs (no aliases, no compat shims):** `extract`, `edit`, `register_version` — removed from the parser/dispatcher and all their private implementations (`executeExtractToolCall`, `executeEditToolCall` + edit helpers, `executeRegisterVersionToolCall`, `readDocumentEditOps`, `DocumentEditOp`/`EditableDocumentContentSource` types, and the corresponding contract members `"extract"|"edit"|"register_version"` in `requestedAction`, `"extracted"|"edited"|"registered"` in `action`, `extraction?:`/`edit?:` payload fields, and the interfaces `RuntimeDocumentEditOpResult` / `RuntimeDocumentEditSummary` / `RuntimeDocumentExtractionSummary` / `RuntimeDocumentSuggestedNextAction`). **Rewritten:** `inspect` now calls the new API-side `inspectDocumentInWorkspace` and returns a structured `RuntimeDocumentInspectionSummary` (source path, inspect sidecar, format, counts, warnings, suggested read paths, optional comparison). `render` now supports authored XLSX from Markdown tables in addition to PDF/DOCX and always persists a sibling Markdown source next to the output (D5 collocation — collision-safe write, `render/content.md` convention replaced). **Added:** `convert({source, targetFormat, outputPath?})` performs pure format conversion via the runtime-managed LibreOffice program; `outputPath` auto-derives from `source` when omitted; new `RuntimeDocumentConvertSummary` in the contract. **Purged legacy guidance:** `native-tool-projection.ts`, `tool-catalog-data.ts`, `bootstrap-preset-data.ts` no longer mention `extract`/`edit`/`register_version`, `render/build.py`, `export_pdf.py`, or visible-script metadata pointers. **Retired dead runtime code:** the legacy `.py` entrypoint fallback, the extracted-project activation seam (`turnState.activeDocumentProjectPath` setter on `"extracted"`), unused `validateDocumentProjectRenderPaths` import, `DocumentProjectManifestFacts` type + all its helper methods (`resolveRenderEntrypoint`, `renderEntrypointMissingWarning`, `resolvePdfHtmlSourceForRender`, `readDocumentProjectManifestFactsOptional`, `resolveImportedNativeRenderWarning`, `resolveImportedOfficePdfExportEntrypoint`, `normalizeRenderOutputPath`, `deriveRenderOutputBasename`, `sanitizeOutputStem`, `isGenericOutputStem`, `readDocumentProjectSourcePath`, `buildRenderProgramSource`, `buildPythonRenderProgramSource`). **Delivery-wall removal (blocked-doc BadRequest, manual `register_version` nudge, provenance walls) remains scope for Slice 2.** ADR-119 golden prompt snapshot regenerated to reflect the new document guidance; new positive tests cover inspect/render/convert + rejection of removed `extract`. Full AGENTS gate green locally: `pnpm -r --if-present lint`, `pnpm format:check`, `pnpm --filter @persai/api|runtime|web typecheck`, plus full `@persai/runtime` and `@persai/api` test runners. - **Change (ADR-130 prompt-layering — Slices 1/2/4 + D6 landed locally, push=deploy batched at session finish).** Prompt-architecture cleanup, slice-by-slice, parent-as-orchestrator with each slice independently verified against the FULL api+runtime suites (not just focused runs). **Slice 1** (`9c284cd4`): `<enabled_skills>` compacted to `key + name` scenario rows with a global cap + compact tail, new lazy read-only `skill.list` / `skill.describe` actions, shared `@persai/runtime-contract` prompt-budget constants, and a real cross-turn cache-guard test (drives `createTurn` twice with different volatile inputs and asserts a byte-identical stable prefix + cache key). **Slice 2** (`88873897`): single-owner system prefix — `memory_protocol` matches ADR-120 reality (no pushed `<persai_memory>`), `response_contract` is its own `{{response_contract_block}}` template, duplicate identity/user/locale/timezone plain lines dropped, `files` mechanics owned only by the catalog entry (runtime-policy + native-projection shadow copies removed); ADR-119 golden regenerated; two stale tests the prior focused runs missed were fixed (`seed-tool-catalog` case-insensitive `engage`; within-cap `files` projection assertions). **Slice 4** (`d61e2cc3`): `<persai_active_scenario>` renders only the current step + exit condition instead of every step body every turn — the current step is derived from the model-owned chat plan (`resolveCurrentStepIndex`: in_progress row position, else completed-row count, else step 1, clamped to range), with the ordered list still owned by `<persai_chat_plan>` and the lean scenario tick reminder kept. **Slice 5 / D6** (this entry): `character_notes` precedence codified as a system-owned `<precedence>` clause inside the `<voice>` envelope (character_notes stays verbatim; it never overrides safety, honest result/tool contracts, or hard invariants; defaults yield to both), documented in `ARCHITECTURE.md`, golden regenerated.
