- **Change (turn/stream/provider timeout ceiling 90s → 300s; landed locally, push=deploy pending founder go).** Founder-directed after the doc live-green: the web streaming turn cap was the hardcoded 90s default of `PERSAI_RUNTIME_STREAM_TIMEOUT_MS` (via `resolveNativeRuntimeTurnTimeoutMs` fallback), and the surrounding chain (`PERSAI_RUNTIME_TURN_TIMEOUT_MS`, `RUNTIME_PROVIDER_GATEWAY_TIMEOUT_MS`, `RUNTIME_PROVIDER_GATEWAY_STREAM_TIMEOUT_MS`, `PROVIDER_GATEWAY_REQUEST_TIMEOUT_MS`, `PROVIDER_GATEWAY_STREAM_TIMEOUT_MS`) was also 90s. Since these are cascading (smallest layer cuts first), the whole chain was raised to 300s: zod defaults in `packages/config/{api-config,runtime-config,provider-gateway-config}.ts` and the two helm-set overrides (`PERSAI_RUNTIME_TURN_TIMEOUT_MS`, `RUNTIME_PROVIDER_GATEWAY_TIMEOUT_MS`) in `infra/helm/values.yaml` + `values-dev.yaml`. `provider-gateway-config.test.ts` default assertions updated to 300000. No ingress/proxy read-timeout override exists in the repo, so the app-level chain is the effective ceiling. Gate green: repo lint, format:check, api/web/runtime/provider-gateway typechecks, provider-gateway test suite, `helm lint` + `helm template` (rendered env = `"300000"`).

- **Validation (ADR-131 Wave 2 — live PROD regression GREEN).** Re-ran the exact prior failure on a fresh chat with the same real founder DOCX (`Карнаух_Федор_Отчет (1).docx`, «переделай это в pdf»). Confirmed by runtime/api/sandbox logs (thread `web-1782990014494`, req `f956cd86`): the model went through `document.render` (narrative «прямой рендер», no shell/`soffice`, no seeded-script execution) in 10 steps (was 26); a single project `doc-3533d8e8` (no `-2`/`-3` proliferation, idempotent extract held); `report.pdf` materialized at `output/report.pdf` (198772 B, exit_code=0), delivered once with version badge `v1`; both the metadata lookup and the real user download of the delivered link returned HTTP 200 (the exact call that 404'd before); turn finished in ~72s (`totalRuntimeMs=71598`), under the 90s cap. The Wave 2 structural fix (commit `a2a6ee88`) is deployed and live-validated.

- **Change (ADR-131 Wave 2 structural correction — runtime-internal builders/exporters, no visible runnable project scripts; deployed `a2a6ee88`, live-validated).** Closed the structural trap found in live re-test: imported DOCX/XLSX extraction no longer seeds visible runnable `render/build.py` / `render/export_pdf.py`, authored `document.render(content/template)` no longer persists a visible `render/build.py`, and runtime default render flows no longer scan the manifest for those scripts or read their bodies from workspace files. `packages/runtime-contract/src/index.ts` now owns the imported Office same-format builder and LibreOffice PDF exporter scaffold bodies as shared functions, `DocumentWorkspaceExtractionService` keeps only visible data artifacts (`project.json`, `source/<copy>`, `extract/*`, and `render/report.html` for PDF/text-like previews), and `RuntimeDocumentToolService` generates imported/authored Python `programSource` in memory before executing the existing ephemeral sandbox `execute_document_code` path. Explicit manual `entrypoint` fallback remains supported for advanced cases, but imported DOCX/XLSX same-format revision, imported DOCX/XLSX -> PDF, and authored `content`/`template` render no longer depend on visible runnable project files. Tests now prove imported Office PDF render works with no visible exporter file, imported DOCX/XLSX extract omits runnable scripts, and authored render keeps only visible editable content (`render/content.md`) while the builder stays runtime-internal. The ADR-119 golden prompt snapshot was intentionally regenerated because document guidance now teaches runtime-internal builders instead of visible `render/*.py` scaffolds.

- **Change (ADR-131 Addendum 2026-07-02 — delivery-safety correction: the attach wall was the bug; landed locally, push=deploy pending founder go).** Live PROD validation on a real founder DOCX proved two prior closure claims wrong: the Wave 13B `files.attach` gate that rejected project-owned outputs without a current registered version was itself the top user-facing failure (broken chat link + orphan + false "готово"), and Problem F was not closed by prompt reinforcement (the model-visible `export_pdf.py` guidance actively taught the shell bypass). Five mechanics-only fixes landed: **(1)** `RegisterChatAttachmentService` no longer hard-rejects — on a real project-owned PDF/DOCX/XLSX output with no current version it runs inspect → register_version server-side (reusing the existing document services, incl. the previously `blocked` path via `revise_document`), re-resolves the ready link, and delivers exactly once; honest failure only when the file truly does not exist. This supersedes the 2026-06-30 Wave 13B attach-refusal behavior. **(2)** `document.extract` is idempotent per source identity (`project.json` `sourcePath` or `contentHash` match) — repeats reuse the existing project instead of allocating `-2`/`-3`, and follow-on edit/render resolve the latest registered canonical version. **(3)** `document.render(format=pdf)` is the single delivery door: `suggestedNextActions` reason and model-facing guidance in `native-tool-projection.ts` / `tool-catalog-data.ts` / `bootstrap-preset-data.ts` no longer name `export_pdf.py` or shell conversion; `shell` is not gated. **(4)** the seeded `export_pdf.py` now reads `PERSAI_OUTPUT_PATH` from `os.environ` with a project-relative default so it never `NameError`s standalone. **(5)** truthful delivery is structural (real attachment row = delivered), not a prose heuristic. Cross-turn tool-memory root cause stays owned by ADR-130 D8; this slice is the idempotency + delivery safety net so documents behave even before D8. Subagent full AGENTS gate green (lint, format:check, api/web/runtime/sandbox typechecks, real api+runtime test runners, ADR-119 golden regenerated); orchestrator independently re-ran the two new reproducing tests green and audited the auto-register determinism + DI wiring. Live regression on the real external DOCX is post-deploy.

## 2026-07-01

- **Change (ADR-129 Addendum II/III — document tool polishing to PROD; landed locally, push=deploy pending founder go).** Reworked the `document` tool around one north-star split: the runtime owns deterministic mechanics (content integrity, render, register, deliver) and the model owns declarative intent (design, authored text, edits). **P-1/P-2:** `document.render` is now the single deliverable door — it normalizes the output path from the requested name, renders, internally inspects → auto-registers a version with honest failure surfacing, and delivers exactly once (turn delivery deduped by `storagePath`); imported Office→PDF is forced through the seeded LibreOffice `export_pdf.py` entrypoint. **P-4:** `document.render` accepts declarative `content` (Markdown string or path) + `template` (title/theme/css/pageSize/running header/footer) and builds both DOCX and PDF through a single seeded Python `markdown` engine in a visible `render/build.py` (PDF via WeasyPrint) — no new npm dependency, imported-source precedence and the single-door register/deliver flow preserved. **P-3:** new additive `document` `action="edit"` applies ordered `replace`/`section` operations server-side over the full canonical content (`render/content.md` for authored, `extract/extracted.md` for imported) with strict all-or-nothing semantics (zero/ambiguous match → honest per-op failure, nothing written) and optional `rerender` that chains back through the single render door. **P-6:** `document.extract` gained a transparent layout→text auto-fallback on layout-extraction timeout and deterministic newest-version source selection (`name (6).docx` over `name (5).docx`). **P-5:** anti-loop is now purely structural (single-door render + `suggestedNextActions` + the existing generic per-turn tool budget); the earlier document-specific hard cap was removed as an arbitrary symptom fix per founder review. **P-7:** exec image now preinstalls `markdown==3.10.2` (python-docx/openpyxl/weasyprint/LibreOffice already present since ADR-123) with build-time self-check — needs an image rebuild at deploy. The uncommitted symptom guard (`blockSmallPdfAfterDocumentStdoutLimit`) was reverted. Full AGENTS gate green: repo lint, format:check, api/web/runtime/sandbox/provider-gateway typechecks, and full runtime (38, incl. 4 new edit tests) / api (golden byte-equal) / sandbox (91) suites. Note: `contracts:generate` produces single-quote churn across 659 committed prettier-formatted generated files (reverted; pre-existing repo hygiene drift, not this slice).

- **Change (ADR-131 local continuation — Slice 2 chat scope, replace projection hardening, Slice 3 residual closeout; final verification passed).** Fixed the GitHub Actions `exactOptionalPropertyTypes` failures from the prior ADR-131 push, then continued locally per founder instruction not to push until all remaining ADR-131 work is batched. `files.list` now defaults to current-chat manifest scope, supports `scope:"assistant"` and `scope:"workspace_shared"` widens, and `files.read` / `files.preview` / `files.attach` / `files.delete` preflight known `/workspace/...` manifest rows before sandbox access; out-of-chat rows require explicit `crossScope:true`. Runtime/API internal workspace file list and metadata lookup surfaces now carry `scope`, `currentChatId`, and `currentAssistantId`, and attachment registration now upserts `originChatId` / `originAssistantId` so uploads remain visible in chat scope. Telegram now threads canonical PersAI `assistant_chat.id` into runtime `channelContext.chatId` / `telegram.chatId`, and runtime uses that unified chat id for Working Files, `files.*`, document origin metadata, and auto-attach; the top-level contract field is channel-agnostic for future MAX runtime adapters. `replace:true` now propagates through manifest upsert; text `files.write` sends a SHA-256 content hash; API refreshes matching attachment rows by path, updates MIME/size, clears stale thumbnail/poster refs, and media file endpoints no longer emit one-hour cache headers for mutable path bytes. Slice 3 closed locally by documenting the already-active fresh document-project allocation and project-output attach gate, plus tightening document guidance: follow `suggestedNextActions`, do not shell-dump large DOCX/XLSX/PDF, do not hand-build imported Office→PDF, and do not attach unrelated/stale project outputs. Final gate passed: full repo lint, format check, API/web/runtime/sandbox typechecks, runtime build, and full API/runtime/sandbox tests.

- **Change (ADR-131 Slice 1 — anti-clobber Variant A landed locally across model-visible and control-plane writes).** Implemented Block 1 of ADR-131: default writes to occupied paths now preserve previous deliveries by allocating macOS/Finder-style sibling names (`report (1).pdf`) on `files.write`, `document.render` `outputPath`, and sandbox control-plane explicit-path writes. Boolean `replace: true` is the explicit exact-overwrite opt-in on those same surfaces; legacy `mode: "overwrite"` is accepted only as compatibility and maps to exact overwrite, while `mode: "create_only"` still fails on exact collision. `document.render` resolves the output path before rendering, persists and auto-registers the resolved path, and returns the resolved path in tool results so later attach/register flows do not use stale requested paths. Production model-facing guidance was aligned across runtime fallback, API catalog/runtime-policy text, prompt fixture, runtime contract, and tests. GPT-5.4 audit found and then re-cleared one blocker (stale API document catalog guidance); focused runtime/sandbox/api tests plus full AGENTS gate passed.

- **Docs (ADR-131 founder-closed — all four decision points confirmed).** Moved `docs/ADR/131-workspace-project-isolation-and-cross-turn-delivery-safety.md` from `Open (problem statement plus candidate directions)` to `Accepted`. All four decision points documented as pending in the broadening push are founder-confirmed: Block 2 default scope tier is `chat` (assistant / workspace-shared are on-demand widens); anti-clobber overwrite-contract shape is boolean `replace: true` on `files.write` / `document.render` / control-plane writes (no enum, no `existingPath` double-confirmation, no removal of `replace`); implementation slice order is Block 1 → Block 2 → Block 3; Problem F is closed by the existing 2026-06-30 seeded-exporter enforcement in `document.render(format=pdf)` on imported DOCX/XLSX plus the 2026-07-01 `suggestedNextActions` addendum on `document.extract` plus a prompt reinforcement ("when `suggestedNextActions` is present in the previous tool result, follow it verbatim"); no runtime heuristic over `shell` (explicitly rejected). Section replaced: `Decisions still required from the founder before implementation` → `Implementation plan (no further decisions required)` with three-slice scope. Block 1 and Block 2 direction headings switched from `Candidate direction (chosen/proposed: ...)` to `Direction (founder-confirmed: ...)`. `AGENTS.md` active-orchestration-programs blurb for ADR-131 updated to reflect closure and implementation ordering. Docs-only; no runtime, contract, or schema touched.

- **Docs (ADR-131 broadened — workspace file identity, isolation, and safe delivery).** Rewrote `docs/ADR/131-workspace-project-isolation-and-cross-turn-delivery-safety.md` from the narrow doc-tool "cross-turn delivery safety" problem statement into a full umbrella problem statement plus candidate directions for the whole `/workspace/` model-facing surface. Three blocks now live inside the same ADR: **Block 1** anti-clobber and stable byte identity (founder-confirmed base: Variant A — macOS-Finder / Google-Drive style ` (N)` collision + explicit `replace: true` applied uniformly on `files.write`, `document.render`, and control-plane writes; content-addressed Variant B documented but deferred to a later dedicated ADR); **Block 2** scope tiers and default visibility (three tiers backed by existing `workspace_file_metadata.originChatId` / `originAssistantId`; chat as default scope is a parent-orchestrator proposal that still needs founder sign-off; assistant on-demand widen and workspace-shared on-demand widen; no physical `/workspace/` migration and ADR-128 flat namespace preserved); **Block 3** cross-turn delivery safety (original Problems E / F / G kept verbatim, now positioned as specialisations of Blocks 1 and 2; ADR-129 addendum `suggestedNextActions` partially mitigates Problem F). Founder-confirmed decisions so far: Variant A as anti-clobber base and ADR-131 stays as a single umbrella (E / F / G do not spin off). Still open for founder decision: default scope tier for Block 2, priority order across blocks, exact widen-scope contract shape, and whether Problem F fix is prompt-only or runtime-enforced. Docs-only; no code, contracts, or schema touched. `AGENTS.md` active-orchestration-programs blurb for ADR-131 updated to the broadened umbrella wording.

- **Change (ADR-129 addendum — auto-register on document.render + extract nextAction hint; ADR-131 opened).** `document.render` now deterministically registers a new document version on success. The render payload carries `versionId`, `docId`, `descriptorMode`, and a `registration` summary for PDF/DOCX/XLSX symmetrically; on failure the render is still valid and a `warning` starting with `auto_register_skipped:<code>` is surfaced so the model can decide to retry or degrade. The model no longer needs to call `document.register_version` for the standard render → attach flow; that action stays available for advanced cases (revising an existing `docId`, non-default `sourceManifestPath` / `inspectionPath`). `document.extract` now returns `suggestedNextActions` for imported DOCX/XLSX with the exact `document.render(format=pdf, projectPath, outputPath)` call to run next via the seeded LibreOffice `export_pdf.py` entrypoint. Model-facing guidance in `native-tool-projection.ts` and the documents-category selector was updated to reflect both. New ADR-131 opened (problem-statement only) for cross-turn workspace pollution → wrong-file attachment, model bypass of `export_pdf.py` when instructions are indirect, and sandbox `shell` `stdout_limit_exceeded` on large document dumps. `AGENTS.md` active-orchestration-programs list now includes ADR-131.

## 2026-06-30

- **Cleanup (ADR-129 audit — neutral visible-workspace naming and presentation-only active-job contract).** Fixed the independent ADR-129 cleanup blockers without reopening Gamma/presentation behavior. Fresh visible `document.register_version` writes now use neutral active-path values (`descriptorMode=create_document`, `documentType=workspace_document`) instead of retired worker-era `create_pdf_document` / `create_data_document` / `pdf_document` / `data_document`. The model-facing `document` tool schema now advertises only `create_document | revise_document` for `register_version`, while compatibility readers still accept historical worker-era values and normalize them back to the new active-path naming. Published active-job contract truth was tightened to match server reality: runtime/openapi `activeDocumentJobs` are presentation-only again (`documentType=presentation`, `descriptorMode=create_presentation | revise_document | export_or_redeliver`). Prisma/client and generated contract artifacts were regenerated with the new visible-workspace enum additions.
- **Change (ADR-129 Wave 13B — inspect/provenance gating for register_version and files.attach).** Visible PDF/DOCX/XLSX document deliverables now share one structural API gate. `document.register_version` rejects outputs whose project/output ownership, source provenance, imported-native `projectSourcePath`, or inspect truth is missing or mismatched. `files.attach` now refuses to silently deliver project-owned document outputs as ordinary files when no valid current registered version points to that output, and it returns clear missing-truth guidance (`document.inspect` / `document.register_version`) instead of attaching a provenance-free final file. Ordinary non-document files remain unaffected.

- **Change (ADR-129 Wave 12C — real imported Office -> PDF export path).** Sandbox exec-image baseline now includes LibreOffice as the real Office conversion engine, with build-time `soffice --version` verification. Imported `DOCX`/`XLSX` document projects now seed a visible `render/export_pdf.py` entrypoint that converts the visible native `projectSourcePath` to PDF and writes exactly to `PERSAI_OUTPUT_PATH`. Runtime `document.render(format=pdf)` now allows imported Office projects only through that visible exporter entrypoint, keeps authored HTML->PDF unchanged, preserves same-format imported Office revision through `render/build.py`, blocks `extract/extracted.md` -> HTML fallback for imported Office -> PDF, and fails honestly when the exporter entrypoint is missing or does not create the declared PDF.

- **Docs (ADR-129 rewrite — clean final PROD target state).** Rewrote `docs/ADR/129-agentic-document-workspace-extraction-render-inspect-and-versioning.md` so the top of the ADR now states the final production document design directly instead of burying it under wave-by-wave implementation history. The rewritten ADR now says plainly what counts as production closure, what paths are forbidden, what the current local state really is, and which remaining gaps still block closure. Follow-up clarification: general UI/UX stage rendering is not owned by ADR-129; instead the document closure now explicitly requires an independent final cleanup audit that removes stale, parallel, and dead document-path code before `push/deploy`.

- **Change (ADR-129 Wave 13A — imported Office inspect comparison against visible source).** API `document.inspect` now detects when an inspected DOCX/XLSX output belongs to an imported same-format document project, reads the visible native `projectSourcePath`, and compares output-vs-source structural counts before writing the inspect sidecar. XLSX sidecars/results now record compact comparison facts such as sheet-count / formula-count / blank-sheet drift plus missing source sheet names; DOCX sidecars/results now record paragraph / heading / table / readable-text drift. Structural degradation is surfaced as explicit inspect warnings and a compact runtime comparison summary, while authored projects, non-project files, and PDF inspect behavior remain unchanged.

- **Change (ADR-129 Wave 12B — imported Office same-format native visible render path).** Imported DOCX/XLSX document projects now seed a visible `render/build.py` scaffold that loads `projectSourcePath` with `python-docx` / `openpyxl` and writes the revised same-format output to `PERSAI_OUTPUT_PATH`. Runtime `document.render` now allows imported Office projects to render only when the requested format exactly matches the imported source format and a visible native entrypoint exists under the project `render/` directory; imported PDF and imported DOCX/XLSX -> PDF still skip honestly with no extracted-text/HTML fallback.

- **Change (ADR-129 Wave 12A — materialize imported native source and block false HTML fallback).** Imported document projects now persist a visible native source copy under the project itself and record that path as `projectSourcePath` in `project.json`, extraction results, visible-workspace version metadata, and attachment `documentLink` readback. Runtime `document.render` now reads project/source facts before rendering: imported `pdf` / `docx` / `xlsx` projects no longer degrade through `extract/extracted.md` -> scaffold HTML -> WeasyPrint, and instead return a structured `native_render_not_implemented` skip until a real source-preserving native engine lands. Authored HTML/Python project renders continue to work unchanged.

- **Change (ADR-129 Wave 11 — document projects are the source of truth for PDF/DOCX/XLSX work).** Document project manifests now carry explicit provenance (`sourceKind`, `sourcePath`, `sourceFormat`, `sourceMimeType`), while extract manifests are marked as sidecar views instead of authoritative source identity. `document.register_version` now requires/resolves a real project, infers `<project>/output/...` ownership when possible, canonicalizes `project.json` for authored projects, and stores consistent project/source/output facts on visible-workspace version metadata plus attachment `documentLink`. Visible Office outputs also keep `xlsx`/`docx` `outputFormat` on readback instead of degrading through the older PDF/PPTX-only parser path.

- **Change (ADR-129 Wave 10b — kill legacy extract from model path + full-text PDF render).** Removed `outputDir` from model-facing `document.extract`; runtime rejects legacy `outputDir` arguments and API returns `legacy_output_dir_rejected`. Every extract now creates `/workspace/projects/<slug>/`. PDF `document.render` on document projects rebuilds HTML from full `extract/extracted.md` server-side before WeasyPrint so partial `files.read` chunks cannot truncate output. Native tool description and Working Files active-project note updated; no `.extract` guidance.

- **Change (ADR-129 Wave 10 — document project binding on extract + render scope).** Default `document.extract` now creates a bounded project under `/workspace/projects/<slug>/` with `project.json`, `extract/` sidecars, a full-text `render/report.html` scaffold, and reserved `output/`. Runtime tracks `activeDocumentProjectPath` per turn and rejects `document.render` when `projectPath`, entrypoint, or output path fall outside that project. Working Files adds a short active-project note.

- **Change (ADR-129 Wave 9b — auto-deliver produced workspace files; remove user-facing honesty notices).** After `document.render` / binary `files.write`, runtime now auto-invokes `files.attach` for any `producedPaths` not yet attached before turn completion — user gets the file instead of a «Поправка» about `files.attach`. Removed user-visible structural correction notices and `expectsMediaArtifact` regex heuristics from API honesty. Working Files developer prompt is chat-scoped only (cap 10); gallery `scope=chat` default and manifest `originChatId` remain.

- **Change (ADR-129 Wave 9 — delivery truth, session-scoped files; superseded by 9b for honesty UX).** Runtime `deliveryFacts`, gallery scope, manifest origin fields.

- **Change (ADR-129 Wave 8 — split model-facing `document` and `presentation` tools).** Models kept choosing deferred `create_presentation` for ordinary PDF document/manual/report requests because one `document` tool still exposed both visible workspace actions and Gamma presentation modes. Runtime projection now emits separate tools: `document` (`extract` / `inspect` / `render` / `register_version` only) and `presentation` (`create_presentation` / `revise_document` / `export_or_redeliver` only). Billing, quota, and plan enablement stay on `document`; `presentation` mirrors `document` activation, reuses the same Gamma enqueue path with `toolCode: "document"`, and is hidden from the plan editor. Catalog/preset guidance, runtime routing, batch reorder (document-family before `files`), and focused API/runtime tests cover the split.

## 2026-06-29

- **Fix (ADR-129 live document loop — keep uploaded DOCX/PDF/XLSX revisions on the visible workspace path).** Re-tested on freshly deployed `f6263cb6` and traced the new turn `e3d1504c-efa2-45f5-8c32-c47f52f75400`. The backend no longer timed out on `document.extract`: API logs showed `document-inspect` `200` in ~9.1s and `document-extract` `200` in ~4.3s, with the sandbox also writing `/workspace/Карнаух_Федор_Отчет (1).inspect.json`. The remaining failure was a mode-selection bug: after successful inspect/extract, the model still called deferred `descriptorMode=revise_document` on `/workspace/Карнаух_Федор_Отчет (1).docx`, but `revise_document` by `storagePath` only resolves PersAI-managed Gamma presentation attachments carrying `documentLink/docId` metadata. Ordinary uploaded DOCX/PDF/XLSX workspace files are not revision targets for that path. API rejection copy now explicitly says not to ask the user to re-upload the same file and instead to continue via the visible workspace workflow (`document.extract` -> edit visible source -> `document.render` -> `document.inspect` -> `files.attach`). Runtime tool projection and schema wording now also say `descriptorMode=revise_document`, `docId`, and `storagePath` are presentation-only and must never be used to revise uploaded DOCX/PDF/XLSX workspace files. Focused API/runtime regressions cover the new steering.

- **ADR (prompt architecture cleanup — compact prefix, single-owner layering, lazy lookup).** Opened ADR-130 as the active prompt-cleanup program for reducing cached-prefix bloat, restoring single-owner prompt/tool layering, moving heavy dynamic descriptor context to lazy action-based lookups, narrowing scenario/chat-plan volatile duplication, and locking explicit `character_notes` precedence. No runtime behavior changed in this slice; the ADR defines the orchestrator-owned slice plan for future implementation.

- **Fix (ADR-129 live document loop — stop treating DOCX builders as PDF renderers).** Re-tested the DOCX-to-PDF workflow on deployed `01dfefca` and inspected `sandbox_jobs` for request `4f3943d1-e699-4763-9368-3fb04239de1a`. The remaining `document` failures were no longer missing upload paths or sidecar sync; `document.render(format=pdf)` auto-selected `/workspace/premium_word_project/build.py`, but that script produced `premium_word_demo.docx`, not `premium_word_demo.pdf`, so the sandbox failed with `Build script did not create the declared output path`. PDF render now only auto-selects HTML/HTM entrypoints; Python PDF rendering remains possible only through an explicit entrypoint that writes the PDF to `PERSAI_OUTPUT_PATH`. Runtime/API guidance and prompt/catalog tests now state that PDF render must not auto-run a DOCX/XLSX Python builder as the PDF renderer.

- **Fix (ADR-129 live document loop — exact workspace paths and render output contract).** Investigated the 38-step DOCX-to-PDF live turn. Runtime/sandbox logs showed the model tried `/workspace/Карнаух_Федор_Отчет.docx` and got `path_not_found`, then extract sidecars hit the earlier hot-pod `write_failed`; after that the model burned shell/exec steps trying to repair paths and produced `/workspace/workspace`-style retries. Root cause: the Working Files developer block exposed alias + displayName but not the authoritative `storagePath`, while files/tool/prompt guidance still taught models that uploads appear at `/workspace/<filename>`. Working Files rows and priority anchors now include `path=/workspace/...`, active files guidance says to use exact listed paths from Working Files / `files.list` / prior tool results and never reconstruct from displayName/filename, and document guidance says Python render entrypoints must write exactly to `PERSAI_OUTPUT_PATH` and must not construct `/workspace/workspace/...` paths. Focused runtime/API prompt/catalog tests cover the new contract.

- **Fix (ADR-129 live document loop — sidecar sync and efficient first-call guidance).** Live browser/K8S validation showed simple PDF creation could start with a failed `document` call before source files existed, and DOCX revision could succeed only after fallback work because extract sidecars were persisted to GCS/DB but failed to hot-push into the running session pod (`workspace_file_writeed ... reason=write_failed`, then `workspace_file_readed ... reason=path_not_found`). Explicit control-plane `path` writes now use the normal required `workspaceFileWrite` path so `/workspace/*.extract/*` and inspect sidecars are visible immediately in the active pod; upload-style basename hot-push remains best-effort/deferred. Runtime `document` guidance now teaches the efficient first call for simple new PDF/DOCX/XLSX: write the visible source entrypoint first (`index.html` for PDF, `build.py` for DOCX/XLSX), then `document.render`, `document.inspect`, and `files.attach`. Focused sandbox/runtime/API document tests cover the fix.

- **Change (ADR-129 — deep cleanup, presentation-only deferred document pipeline).** Followed up on the hard cutover after founder feedback that the cleanup did not go far enough. Deferred `document` jobs are now strictly presentation-only end-to-end: the runtime `document` tool parser, `RuntimeDeferredDocumentJobSummary`, runtime acknowledgement copy, runtime `extractDeferredDocumentJob`, the runtime job worker (`runtime-document-provider-adapter.service.ts`), the runtime jobs controller, the web `AssistantWebChatActiveDocumentJobState` plus chat-input chip label, and the API enqueue/job/scheduler/delivery/read/completion/failure surfaces all narrow `descriptorMode` to `create_presentation | revise_document | export_or_redeliver` and `documentType` to `presentation`. The Prisma `AssistantDocumentRenderProvider` enum was shrunk to `gamma` and `AssistantDocumentOutputFormat` to `pdf | pptx` via `20260629200000_adr129_presentation_only_document_enums`, which also purges historical non-presentation render-job rows and drops the dead PDF-structure columns from `assistant_document_versions`. Retired descriptor modes now fail at parse with `invalid_arguments` instead of dispatching through `buildRetiredDescriptorModeResult`, which was removed. Visible-workspace PDF/XLSX/DOCX work is unchanged: it still goes through `document.extract / document.render / document.inspect / document.register_version / files.attach`, and the `AssistantDocumentType` / `AssistantDocumentDescriptorMode` enums and the chat-attachment `documentLink` metadata stay wide because visible-workspace registration continues to write PDF/XLSX/DOCX visible documents into `AssistantDocument`.

- **Change (ADR-129 — hard cutover for non-presentation document generation).** Tightened the local document-tool cutover after founder cleanup feedback: PDF/DOCX/XLSX document work is now visible-workspace only (`document.extract` / `document.render` / `document.inspect` / optional `document.register_version` / `files.attach`). Runtime/model-facing projection no longer advertises PDF/DOCX/XLSX descriptor generation, stray non-presentation descriptor calls return `descriptor_mode_retired`, and API enqueue rejects `create_pdf_document` / `create_data_document` before creating background jobs. `document.extract` also rejects non-empty output sidecar directories instead of deleting/replacing existing sidecars. Presentation generation is intentionally preserved on the existing presentation worker path.

- **Verification (ADR-129 — local implementation gate passed).** Completed the local ADR-129 implementation program through Wave 6 and passed the final local gate: full repo lint, format check, API/web/runtime/sandbox/provider typechecks, and focused document workflow tests for extraction, inspection, version registration, delivery metadata, attachment registration, enqueue/revise guards, tool catalog/projection wording, runtime tool behavior, and web document metadata rendering. ADR-129 remains deploy/live-validation pending before closure.

- **Docs/cleanup (document tools — visible workflow wording closeout).** Landed ADR-129 Wave 6 locally: the model-facing `document` descriptor, seeded tool catalog guidance, and prompt selection guide now all teach the same visible workspace document loop (`document.extract` when useful -> edit real `/workspace` source -> `document.render` -> `document.inspect` -> optional `document.register_version` -> `files.attach`). Active docs that still contradicted the current path-based file/document truth were tightened, and stale wording about async document providers, PDFMonkey-backed sandbox documents, hidden XLSX/DOCX generation, and retired role-based workspace subpaths was removed from active surfaces.

- **Feature (document tools — PDF revise honors visible workspace source).** Landed ADR-129 Wave 5 locally: `revise_document` now stops the hidden PDF patch/requeue path whenever the current PDF version already carries visible `documentWorkspace.workspaceProjectPath` and `outputPath` facts. Instead of silently enqueueing DB-only revision, API/runtime return an honest structured skip that points the model back to the visible `/workspace` workflow (`document.render` -> `document.inspect` -> `document.register_version` -> `files.attach`) using the existing project/output paths. Older DB-only PDF rows without visible workspace source remain compatible with the prior revise behavior, and focused tests cover both the new guided rejection and the legacy-compatible path.

- **Feature (document tools — retire opaque data-document generation path).** Landed ADR-129 Wave 4 locally: the model-facing `document` projection no longer advertises `create_data_document` or legacy `outputFormat: "xlsx" | "docx"` as the normal XLSX/DOCX path, and ordinary calls that still send those retired shapes now return honest structured skipped results directing the model to the visible `/workspace` workflow (`document.render` -> `document.inspect` -> optional `document.register_version` -> `files.attach`) instead of enqueueing the hidden sandbox worker. Historical compatibility remains for persisted `create_data_document` version/attachment metadata so older data-document rows still read back as `data_document` with `xlsx`/`docx` workspace facts.

- **Feature (document tools — visible version registration).** Landed ADR-129 Wave 3: `document.register_version` now records visible workspace render outputs as `AssistantDocumentVersion` truth without delivering files, preserving source manifest, output path, project path, inspection sidecar, and inspection summary in existing JSON metadata. Document attachment `documentLink` metadata is centralized and widened for PDF/XLSX/DOCX so refresh/replay and `files.attach` surfaces keep descriptor/output/workspace facts without schema migration.

- **Feature (document tools — visible render and inspect).** Landed ADR-129 Wave 2: `document.inspect` now writes visible `/workspace/*.inspect.json` sidecars for PDF/XLSX/DOCX and returns compact counts/warnings, while `document.render` can run visible workspace projects from HTML or Python `build.py` entrypoints and persist PDF/XLSX/DOCX outputs back to canonical workspace state. Focused tests cover XLSX/PDF inspection, invalid inspect paths, source-overwrite prevention, HTML→PDF render, Python build.py XLSX render, unsupported render honesty, output extension validation, and descriptor exposure.

- **Feature (document tools — visible extraction sidecars).** Landed ADR-129 Wave 1: the runtime `document` tool now supports explicit `action: "extract"` for `/workspace/...` sources, calling an API-owned extraction endpoint that reuses existing extraction/OCR policy and persists visible sidecars under `/workspace/<name>.extract/`. Outputs include compact model results plus `manifest.json`, `extracted.md`, and spreadsheet sheet CSVs in canonical GCS + `workspace_file_metadata`, with best-effort hot-pod sync for immediate sandbox visibility. Focused tests cover PDF extraction sidecars, XLSX sheet extraction, generic MIME fallback, outputDir/file collision rejection, runtime result shape, and descriptor exposure.

- **ADR (document tools — agentic workspace workflow).** Opened ADR-129 as the active orchestration program for redesigning `document` from an opaque async generator into a workspace-visible extraction/render/inspect/version workflow. The program keeps `(workspaceId, path)`, `/workspace`, existing extraction/OCR services, sandbox render/build tools, source snapshots, and final `files.attach` delivery as the governing model, and explicitly retires the normal hidden `create_data_document` path before closure.

- **Docs (file ADR closure).** Closed ADR-126 v3, ADR-126 v3 cutover program, ADR-127, and ADR-128 as active filesystem programs. `AGENTS.md` now treats all file/workspace ADRs as closed archive; that closure left no open orchestration program until the later ADR-129 founder priority for document tools.

- **Fix (chat/file delivery — broader text/source artifacts).** Expanded the media validation allowlist for ordinary text/source files so chat uploads and sandbox/tool-generated artifacts such as HTML, CSS, TypeScript/JSX, JSONL, TSV, INI, `.env.example`, Dockerfile, YAML, TOML, XML, SQL, and common language source files can be accepted instead of being rejected by missing MIME/extension coverage. Safe text/source extensions now bypass the old dangerous-extension block for `chat_upload` and `tool_output_persist`, while unknown generic binaries remain blocked. Focused policy tests cover raw `.js`/`.py` chat upload acceptance, HTML delivery, generic-octet TypeScript fallback, and the compound/no-extension formats.

## 2026-06-27

- **Fix (sandbox file delivery — tool-generated source files are deliverable).** Live retry of `files.attach` for `/workspace/parse_v7.py` showed the sandbox publish path was correct (`parse_v7.py` existed in the session pod and in GCS at `4791` bytes), but API delivery rejected the chat attachment with `Files with .py extension are blocked by security policy.` Root cause: `media-security-policy.ts` used a single hardcoded dangerous-extension denylist for both user uploads and sandbox/tool output delivery. Fix: user/chat uploads remain blocked for dangerous extensions, but `tool_output_persist` now allows safe text source extensions (`.py`, `.js`, `.mjs`, `.rb`, `.sh`) to be delivered as normal attachments after MIME/sniffing validation still passes. Focused policy test covers `.py` blocked for `chat_upload` and allowed for `tool_output_persist`.

- **Fix (sandbox hot-pod upload sync — large chat uploads no longer rely on base64 control-plane payloads).** Live validation on workspace `24926096-953e-49b9-af56-f3551ce6f602` showed `LOG006.01.csv` uploads were correctly persisted in DB + GCS (`10006879` bytes each), but the duplicate `/workspace/LOG006.01 (2).csv` missed the already-running session pod because the API-to-sandbox hot-push sent the 10MB file as base64 JSON and the sandbox process timed out after 15s (`workspace_write_control_plane_failed ... Sandbox process exceeded 15000ms`). The current pod was manually unblocked by mirroring the existing CSV to the duplicate path. Code fix: `ManageChatMediaService.stageForWebThread` now sends `storagePath` to the sandbox control-plane endpoint; the sandbox downloads canonical bytes from GCS and writes them into the hot pod through the existing workspace bridge, while retaining `contentBase64` compatibility for older callers. Focused API staging and sandbox service regressions cover the new storage-path path; API/sandbox typechecks are green.

- **Fix (web upload proxy — valid 11–24MB chat attachments no longer hit Next's 10MB proxy body cap).** Live cluster logs for failed 11MB/24MB chat uploads showed the web pod warning `Request body exceeded 10MB for /api/v1/assistant/chat/web/stage-attachment` and the API pod downstream error `Request aborted` from multer. Root cause: the browser uploads to same-origin `/api/v1/...`, which is proxied by the Next app route before reaching the API; Next 16 defaults `proxyClientMaxBodySize` to 10MB, while the API upload contract allows `MAX_MEDIA_FILE_BYTES = 25 * 1024 * 1024`. Fix: `apps/web/next.config.ts` now sets `experimental.proxyClientMaxBodySize` to the same 25MiB API limit, preserving API-side validation while stopping valid uploads from being truncated by the web proxy. UX follow-up: oversized picker/paste/drop files are rejected locally in the composer with localized RU/EN copy (`Файл слишком большой. Максимальный размер — 25 МБ.` / `File is too large. Maximum size is 25 MB.`) instead of failing later with an opaque upload error.

- **Fix (web assistant files — gallery row cap, quiet tiles, real thumbnail previews, and auth spinner guard).** Founder screenshot review of the Assistant Files gallery showed an unbounded tile wall with bright white cards; chat inline images also behaved like thumbnails visually but could still load/open the full original when no derivative path existed, and live browser validation on `/sign-in` showed Clerk JS/proxy resources healthy while the submit button remained in spinner state after Clerk requests had completed. Fix: the Assistant Files gallery now scrolls after roughly three rows and uses the same quiet `bg-background/35` card treatment as the media limit cards; chat/gallery inline image previews now use `/files/preview`; API preview endpoints downscale `image/*` responses to a 256px webp when `sharp` is available while full/download/lightbox URLs keep the original; custom sign-in/sign-up pages use local submit state instead of global Clerk `fetchStatus` so a stale fetching state cannot leave the form permanently disabled. Focused web tests, API media controller test, lint, format, API typecheck, web typecheck, and full API suite are green; a mistakenly broad web suite also ran and only failed an unrelated `app/admin/plans/page.test.tsx` timeout while the changed tests passed.

- **Fix (Telegram media jobs — safety-rejected provider failures are no longer one-shot silent best-effort).** Live Danilov check showed `image_provider_safety_rejected` was not a stuck queue: the media job created a normal assistant-authored failure explanation in DB, but Telegram delivery was a one-shot `bestEffort` after the job had already been closed `failed`, so a transient skip/failure could leave the user with no first visible message. Fix: Telegram terminal media failures now move from the scheduler into durable `completion_pending` delivery with zero artifacts and preserved `lastErrorCode/lastErrorMessage`; the completion-delivery worker sends the persisted failure explanation, marks `deliveredAt` only after the Telegram text notice is actually delivered, and keeps the job retryable if the notice is skipped or fails. Focused API regressions cover scheduler-authored `image_provider_safety_rejected` Telegram delivery and the scheduler no longer doing direct one-shot outbound.

## 2026-06-26

- **Fix (web auth — Clerk proxy pins broken major-only Clerk JS URL).** Founder console output during slow sign-out/sign-in showed the real client failure: `GET /clerk-proxy/npm/@clerk/clerk-js@6/dist/clerk.browser.js` returned cached `404 text/plain`, so the browser refused to execute Clerk JS and Clerk failed with `code="failed_to_load_clerk_js"`. Exact versioned URLs under the same proxy (`@6.22.0`, `@6.4.0`) returned `200 application/javascript`. Fix: the custom Clerk npm proxy now rewrites major-only `@clerk/clerk-js@6/*` requests to pinned `@clerk/clerk-js@6.22.0/*`, and web build/runtime env now sets `NEXT_PUBLIC_CLERK_JS_URL=/clerk-proxy/npm/@clerk/clerk-js@6.22.0/dist/clerk.browser.js` so normal app reloads request a different exact-version URL instead of relying on Ctrl+F5 to clear a locally cached `@6` 404. Focused web proxy regression test covers the failing URL.

- **Fix (web auth — sign-in/sign-up wait for Clerk form resources).** Cluster investigation for intermittent login-form load complaints found healthy pods/ingress and successful `/sign-in` + `/sign-up` probes, with the only server-side error being stale Next Server Action IDs from old tabs after deploy. The custom auth pages are client-only and do not use server actions, but they gated rendering only on `useAuth().isLoaded` while also depending on `useSignIn()` / `useSignUp()` resources. Fix: keep the loading shell until `signIn` / `signUp` exists; regression tests cover unloaded Clerk resources for both pages.

- **Fix (ADR-128 Slice 4 follow-up — `files.read` now honors `maxBytes` before stdout/base64 transfer).** Danilov workspace `2d29a9b3-76f8-436f-a189-d7470ac3ef3b` no longer had current pending sandbox jobs; the later assistant text repeated a stale `sandbox_workspace_backlog_full` claim, while the real new failing sandbox rows were `files.read` calls on an 8.1 MB Betaflight Blackbox log with payload `maxBytes=10000` blocked by `stdout_limit_exceeded`. Root cause: `SandboxService.executeFilesBridgeAction` ignored `args.maxBytes` and called `workspaceFileRead` with no cap, so the bridge defaulted to 16 MiB and pushed base64 through model-visible stdout. Fix: validate and forward optional positive `maxBytes`; regression test covers the Danilov payload shape.

- **Fix (ADR-128 Slice 4 follow-up — sandbox plan memory cap raised for full-size image operations).** Live validation with `3530.jpg` (`3000x4000`) showed `files.attach` delivery working on sandbox image `65082a2e`, but multi-effect Pillow batches killed the session exec pod and the control plane then surfaced `Workspace tar pull failed ... cannot exec in a stopped state`. Root cause was plan-bound, not a stdout issue: active plan `ultima` and all stored dev plan `sandboxPolicy` documents still carried `maxMemoryBytesPerJob=268435456` (`256 MiB`), and exec pods also hardcoded `/workspace` + `/tmp` emptyDir limits to `256Mi` despite `SANDBOX_SHARED_EMPTYDIR_SIZE_MIB=512`. Fix: default sandbox memory is now `1 GiB`, migration `20260626165000_adr128_sandbox_plan_memory_1g` raises stored plan sandbox memory caps to at least `1 GiB` and bumps config generation so existing runtime bundles refresh, and exec pod emptyDir limits now use the configured `SANDBOX_SHARED_EMPTYDIR_SIZE_MIB`.

- **Fix (ADR-128 Slice 4 follow-up — `files.attach` publish path no longer uses model stdout/base64).** The initial exec-created-file delivery fix correctly required `files.attach` to publish pod bytes to GCS before returning `attached`, but it reused `workspaceFileRead`, which transfers bytes through the model-facing stdout/base64 path and therefore hit the normal sandbox `maxStdoutBytes=128 KiB` cap for full-size processed images (`sharp_fix.jpg`, `blur_fix.jpg`). Clean fix: `ExecPodBridgeService.readWorkspaceFileFromSessionPod` now performs a control-plane-only raw file read from the session pod, with an in-pod size precheck against outbound delivery limits before transfer and no `LimitedCollector` stdout policy. `WorkspaceFileBridgeService.workspaceFilePersist` uses that raw byte path for publish-to-GCS. Regression test now covers a 200 KiB exec-created file and asserts the old shell/base64 read path is not used.

- **Fix (ADR-128 Slice 4 follow-up — `files.attach` now publishes exec-created files to GCS before delivery).** Live persai-dev validation on `info@gemeral-fly.com` workspace `24926096-953e-49b9-af56-f3551ce6f602` showed Python/Pillow created `/workspace/thumb.jpg`, `/workspace/sharp.jpg`, and `/workspace/blur_overlay.jpg` successfully and sandbox `files.attach` jobs for all three completed with valid `action:"attached"` payloads, but no chat attachment rows appeared and final-delivery honesty appended `Поправка: изображение или другой медиафайл не был реально доставлен в этот чат.` Root cause: `files.attach` only verified the pod file existed; API delivery later downloaded from canonical GCS, but files created by `exec`/`shell` were never mirrored there. Fix: `WorkspaceFileBridgeService.workspaceFilePersist` reads an existing `/workspace/*` pod file and saves it to the flat workspace GCS key, and `SandboxService` now runs that publish step inside `files.attach` before returning `attached`. Focused sandbox gate PASS: `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/sandbox test -- workspace-file-bridge.service.test.ts sandbox.service.test.ts` (80/80).

- **Fix (ADR-128 Slice 4 follow-up — sandbox bootstrap + stale backlog cleanup).** Two live persai-dev regressions were confirmed from `sandbox_jobs`, not model guesses. First, user `mr.danilov.r.s@gmail.com` workspace `2d29a9b3-76f8-436f-a189-d7470ac3ef3b` had four `running` sandbox jobs stuck since 2026-06-23 with `execPodName=null`; they permanently consumed the per-workspace backlog and caused later `files.read`, `glob`, `grep`, and `shell` calls to be blocked with `sandbox_workspace_backlog_full`. Fix: `resolvePreflightViolation` now sweeps pending `queued/running` jobs through the existing stale-timeout logic before counting backlog. Second, workspace `24926096-953e-49b9-af56-f3551ce6f602` repeatedly failed `files.read`, `glob`, `shell`, `exec`, and runtime `workspace_write` before process spawn with `Failed to create workspace directory for handle=persai.` Root cause: Slice 4 bootstrap attempted `chmod 0755 /workspace` from a non-root exec container even though `/workspace` is the root of an `emptyDir` mount. Fix: bootstrap now verifies `test -d /workspace` and `test -w /workspace` and no longer chmods the mount root; marker writes remain in `/tmp`. `runStdinlessProbe` now captures/logs stdout+stderr on failed probes so future bootstrap errors keep their real cause. Gates: sandbox lint PASS, typecheck PASS, tests PASS (79/79).

- **Fix (ADR-128 Slice 4 follow-up — `computeWorkspaceStats` lstat defense-in-depth).** Live persai-dev session at ~00:20 UTC surfaced a real sandbox crash that the model reported verbatim: `ENOENT: no such file or directory, stat '/tmp/persai-sandbox/assistants/<aid>/<wsid>/workspace/outbound/self'`. Diagnosis traced to `SandboxService.computeWorkspaceStats` (the baseline-stats walk run before every queued sandbox job): `fs.readdir(... { withFileTypes: true })` returned the `outbound/self` symlink as a non-directory `Dirent`, then `fs.stat` was called on it which **follows symlinks**, and on the sandbox-service control-plane filesystem the absolute target `/workspace/outbound/luma` did not exist (it only exists inside the pod). The function threw, the entire job aborted with `violationCode=ENOENT`, and the model received the message as a real sandbox error and stopped trying. The symlink reached the control-plane cache via `pullWorkspace` after the pre-Slice-4 pod bootstrap created `outbound/self → outbound/<handle>`, and was re-applied every turn from the session-snapshot tar cached in GCS. **Primary fix already in Slice 4 (subagent):** the `outbound/self → outbound/<handle>` symlink + the entire `outbound/<handle>` and `input/` mkdir/chmod block is removed from `ensureWorkspaceMountBootstrapped`, so no symlink is ever introduced into either the pod or the control-plane cache going forward. **Defense-in-depth fix added on top:** `computeWorkspaceStats` now uses `fs.lstat` instead of `fs.stat` and skips `isSymbolicLink()` entries from the byte total (still counts them as files). Any future symlink dragged into the workspace cache by any path (snapshot restore, user upload of a tar, manual paste) is now measured by the link itself and cannot crash the baseline walk. Sandbox suite remains 79/79 green.

- **Refactor (ADR-128 Slice 4 — flatten `/workspace/` to a single-namespace, role-free filesystem; landed locally).** Final closure of the dual-namespace migration. After founder feedback that `input/` + `outbound/<handle>/` + `outbound/self` symlink produced confusing semantics (user uploads in `input/`, model outputs in `outbound/`, "editing" a user file silently created a new file in outbound), Slice 4 collapses the entire workspace to a single flat `/workspace/` root — Claude Code-style UX, one user + 1–2 assistants, share-by-default. New pod layout: `/workspace/` (mode `0755`, owner `sandbox`); no `input/`, no `outbound/`, no `outbound/self`, no `outbound/<handle>`, no symlinks. User uploads land at `/workspace/<basename>` with macOS-style numeric collision suffix; the model reads + writes any file under `/workspace/<path>` directly; ephemeral computations use `/tmp/` (tmpfs already in the pod). Cross-assistant isolation defaults to "share by default" — the workspace owns files. GCS layout unchanged at `fs/workspaces/<wsid>/workspace/<rel>`. **Retired symbols (deleted from active codebase):** `WorkspaceMountRole` enum and all variants (`workspace_input`, `workspace_outbound_self`, `workspace_outbound_other`, `workspace_scratch`); `isPersistedWorkspaceRole`; the `outbound/self → outbound/<handle>` symlink + the `input`/`outbound/<handle>` mkdir/chmod block in `ensureWorkspaceMountBootstrapped`; `buildWorkspaceObjectKey`'s role-based special-casing (now strips `/workspace/`); `resolveWorkspaceInputStoragePath` / `resolve-workspace-input-storage-path.ts` (collapsed into `resolveWorkspaceStoragePath`); all model-facing `files.*` tool description text mentioning `input`, `outbound`, `self`, `<handle>`, or role distinctions. **Renamed symbols:** `writeWorkspaceInputControlPlane` → `writeWorkspaceFileControlPlane`; `writeWorkspaceOutboundWithCollision` → `writeWorkspaceFileWithCollision`; `recordWorkspaceInputPublished` → `recordWorkspaceFilePublished` (audit event `audit_event=workspace_file_published`); `pushWorkspaceInboundBytes` → `pushWorkspaceFileBytes` (sandbox-control-plane client); sandbox HTTP endpoints `/api/v1/jobs/workspace-outbound-write` → `/api/v1/jobs/workspace-write` and `/api/v1/jobs/workspace-inbound-write` → `/api/v1/jobs/workspace-write-control-plane`; `SandboxClientService.writeWorkspaceOutbound` → `writeWorkspaceFile`. **Simplified primitives:** `assertAllowedMountPrefix(input)` now normalises → asserts `/workspace` prefix → throws `WorkspacePathError` if not, returning `{ absolutePath, relativePath }` with no `role`. `ensureWorkspaceMountBootstrapped` runs `mkdir /workspace` → `chmod 0755` → GCS hydrate → write marker; once per cold pod. `workspaceFileWrite` rejects only paths outside `/workspace/`, mirrors every write to GCS + upserts `workspace_file_metadata`; no scratch carve-out. `workspaceFileDelete` same shape. GC handler `purgeAssistantOutbound` becomes a marker-only purge (no per-handle subdir exists); `purgeWorkspaceShared` wipes `rm -rf '/workspace'/* '/workspace'/.[!.]*` per warm pod + drops the GCS workspace prefix + removes matching `workspace_file_metadata` rows. **Tool description (production text the model sees):** `Path-driven file operations on the single flat /workspace/ namespace. Read and write any file directly under /workspace/<path>; user uploads land at /workspace/<filename> and stay there. Use /tmp/ for ephemeral scratch that the user should never see.` `document.storagePath` cross-chat example updated from `/workspace/outbound/self/report.pdf` → `/workspace/report.pdf`. **Files touched (high level).** Sandbox: `workspace-path.ts`, `workspace-file-bridge.service.ts`, `workspace-audit.service.ts`, `exec-pod-bridge.service.ts`, `sandbox-object-storage.service.ts`, `sandbox.service.ts`, `sandbox.controller.ts`, `workspace-gc.service.ts`. API: `runtime-tool-policy.ts`, `tool-catalog-data.ts`, `bootstrap-preset-data.ts`, new `resolve-workspace-storage-path.ts`, `manage-chat-media.service.ts`, `inbound-media.service.ts`, `media-delivery.service.ts`, `sandbox-control-plane.client.service.ts`, `upsert-workspace-file-metadata-from-runtime.service.ts`, `list-workspace-files-from-manifest.service.ts`, `media-attachment.controller.ts`, `internal-workspace-files.controller.ts`. Runtime: `native-tool-projection.ts`, `sandbox-client.service.ts`, `write-runtime-outbound-artifact.ts`. Web: assertion paths in `chat-message.test.tsx`, `sidebar.test.tsx`, `use-chat.test.tsx`, `assistant-settings.test.tsx`, `assistant-api-client.test.ts`. Tests: a one-shot bulk-flatten script `scripts/flatten-workspace-test-paths.mjs` rewrote literal-form fixture paths across api + runtime + web tests; targeted hand-edits for tests that asserted on `role`, method names, URL-encoded path strings, or tool description regexes. **Gates green (all four packages):** lint PASS, typecheck PASS, test PASS — sandbox 79/79, web 832/832, runtime suite PASS, api suite PASS; `corepack pnpm run format:check` PASS. Final `rg` retired-symbol grep returns only (a) historical CHANGELOG / SESSION-HANDOFF entries describing the prior state, (b) historical migration SQL, (c) explicit ADR-128 Slice 4 negation assertions across three test files that prove the flat layout creates none of these. **No commit/push yet** per the standing rule; orchestrator commits and pushes. Deploy + live validation pending the next dev rollout. Open a follow-up only if a new structural concern surfaces during live test; do not reopen this slice for scope creep.

- **Refactor (ADR-128 S1+S2 — retire `/shared/<workspaceId>/` pod namespace, single `/workspace/` root).** Two atomic commits land the entire model-facing + sandbox + storage refactor: `4eb68921` (sandbox layer, 15 files, +435/-830) eliminates the `/shared/<wsid>/` mount, all `Shared*` helpers, `injectWorkspaceIdSegmentIfMissing`, the `shared-root` k8s emptyDir, and `WORKSPACE_ID_UUID_RE` (no more wsId in pod paths); `fe4d61f3` (api+runtime+web+Prisma seed, 86 files, +598/-535) rewrites every `storagePath` shape, GCS key, wire-protocol method, and tool description to the single namespace. New pod layout: `/workspace/input/` (mode 0555 — listable, RO uploads), `/workspace/outbound/self → /workspace/outbound/<handle>` symlink (mode 0755 — RW deliveries), `/workspace/<rest>` (ephemeral scratch). GCS prefix unchanged at `fs/workspaces/<wsid>/` but the tail under it changes from `shared/...` to `workspace/...`. Manifest `path` and `AssistantChatMessageAttachment.storagePath` both adopt the new shape. Tool description text in `tool-catalog-data.ts`, `bootstrap-preset-data.ts`, `native-tool-projection.ts`, and ADR-119 golden snapshot rewritten to single-namespace contract. NO translation layer left in code, NO `// legacy` branches, NO transitional dual-prefix readers. Gates: sandbox 80/80 tests, web 832/832 tests, api+runtime tests green, lint+typecheck+format clean, repo-wide `rg "/shared/"` (ex migrations) and `rg` for ~14 retired symbol names both return 0 hits. Deploy + dev wipe (S3) + closure (S4) pending.

- **Open (ADR-128 — single `/workspace/` namespace; retire `/shared/<workspaceId>/`).** New ADR opened after 2026-06-25 founder live test surfaced the structural gap left by ADR-126 v3 / ADR-127 closures: two pod namespaces (`/workspace/` for assistant scratch, `/shared/<wsid>/` for shared user/model files) with different persistence/sync/manifest semantics caused the model to make 6+ fallback tool calls on a fresh xlsx upload (defaulted to `/workspace/X.xlsx` instead of `/shared/input/X.xlsx`). Symlinks fix in commit `d3db1c93` acknowledged as a kludge layered on top of the dual-namespace structure — does not bridge cross-namespace model bias. ADR-128 plans a six-slice cutover: pod bootstrap + path containment, sandbox bridge, API/runtime path generation, DB back-fill, GCS layout + transitional dual-prefix read, closure + docs + legacy GCS wipe runbook section. Single root `/workspace/` with `input/` (0555 read-only, listable), `outbound/self/` (0755 writable), free area for ephemeral scratch. No code change yet; opens the program.

## 2026-06-25

- **Fix (ADR-127 follow-up — pod-side symlinks for model-canonical `/shared/` paths).** Added `ensureSharedMountSymlinks` to `ExecPodBridgeService` (Phase 2b of `ensureSharedMountBootstrapped`): creates `/shared/input → /shared/<workspaceId>/input` and `/shared/outbound → /shared/<workspaceId>/outbound` symlinks on every cold bootstrap so the model's `shell` commands resolve `/shared/input/X.xlsx` without workspaceId injection (was ~7 tool calls; now ~2). Requires a new `shared-root` emptyDir (2Mi) mounted at `/shared` in the exec pod spec — `readOnlyRootFilesystem: true` made the image-layer `/shared` dir unwritable otherwise. WorkspaceId validated against strict UUID regex before shell interpolation. `injectWorkspaceIdSegmentIfMissing` left intact for `files.*` tool defense-in-depth. 4 new unit tests added. Deploy + live validation pending next rollout.

- **Operations (ADR-127 W5 — legacy GCS wipe executed on dev; D10).** `gcloud storage rm -r --quiet gs://persai-dev-workspaces/assistant-media/` removed ~1978 objects in ~25s on the `persai-dev` cluster: legacy v1/v2 fileRef-shaped chat/runtime-output blobs, Gen 2 path-identity attachments under `assistant-media/workspaces/...`, and sandbox session snapshots. `assistant-media/` prefix now absent (verification `gcloud storage ls` returns no-objects error). `fs/` subtree unaffected. Founder approved data loss explicitly (dev is non-commercial). Prod wipe NOT executed — deferred indefinitely. Live validation surfaced a separate model-UX issue: model uses model-canonical `/shared/input/X.xlsx` paths inside `shell` commands, but pod-physical filesystem has `/shared/<workspaceId>/input/X.xlsx` — path translation only applies to `files.*` tool args, not to shell command bodies, causing the model to do ~7 tool calls (files.list → shell → "path not found" → glob → knowledge search) instead of ~2 to read a binary file. Flagged as ADR-127 follow-up (pod-side symlinks); not implemented.

- **Hygiene (ADR-127 follow-up — drop residual `?? "assistant-media"` fallbacks).** Removed the now-dead nullish-coalescing fallback `?? "assistant-media"` from all five sites in `apps/sandbox/src/` (`sandbox-object-storage.service.ts` ×4, `workspace-gc.service.ts` ×1). `PERSAI_MEDIA_OBJECT_PREFIX` is typed `string` (schema guarantees presence), so option A (bare removal) applied at every site. Zero string-literal hits for `"assistant-media"` remain in `apps/sandbox/src/`. Gate: lint/format/typecheck (sandbox, api, runtime) + sandbox test suite (79/79) all green.

- **Change (ADR-127 W4.5 — D9: `PERSAI_MEDIA_OBJECT_PREFIX` default rename).** Default value changed from `"assistant-media"` to `"fs"` in all three config schemas (`api-config.ts`, `runtime-config.ts`, `sandbox-config.ts`) and all six explicit Helm pins in `values.yaml` / `values-dev.yaml`. `ADR-126-V3-GCS-WIPE-RUNBOOK.md` annotated with an ADR-127 D9 note explaining pre-D9 vs post-D9 prefix semantics. No DB changes; no GCS object moves; no logic delta. Wipe runbook (W5 / D10) remains pending.

- **Change (ADR-127 W4 — drop objectKey fallback in isAttachmentRef; D8).** One-shot Prisma migration `20260625000000_adr127_w4_drop_objectkey_fallback_data_migration` rewrites `assistant_media_jobs.request_json.attachments[].objectKey` → `storagePath` (idempotent; rows already carrying `storagePath` are untouched). Both `isAttachmentRef` validators (`EnqueueRuntimeDeferredMediaJobService`, `WorkspaceMediaJobSchedulerService`) now require `storagePath` only; `objectKey` fallback branch removed. Three ADR-127 W4 regression tests added to each test file.

  **Change (ADR-127 W3 — delete-everywhere symmetry; D5 delete-side + D7).** Chat-scoped delete, runtime `files.delete`, and the UI orphan-tile delete path now all converge on the manifest as source of truth: `ManageChatMediaService.deleteChatWorkspaceFile` / new workspace-scoped delete remove GCS bytes, delete `workspace_file_metadata`, mark attachment-backed rows unavailable when applicable, and best-effort evict warm pod copies through the new sandbox control-plane `POST /api/v1/control/workspaces/:workspaceId/shared/rm`; runtime `files.delete` now calls the new internal manifest-delete endpoint `DELETE /api/v1/internal/workspaces/:workspaceId/files/metadata?path=...` for `/shared/...` paths, and `WorkspaceFilesGallery` now uses the new public `DELETE /api/v1/assistant/workspaces/:workspaceId/files?path=...` for orphan tiles (`chatId === null`).

- **Performance (ADR-127 W2 — parallel cold-start shared hydrate; D6).** `apps/sandbox/src/exec-pod-bridge.service.ts` now hydrates `/shared/<workspaceId>/...` with a bounded `Promise.allSettled` worker pool (`SHARED_MOUNT_HYDRATE_CONCURRENCY = 12`) instead of a serial per-object loop, preserving per-file warn semantics while overlapping GCS downloads and pod exec writes; completion now logs `shared_mount_hydrate_done workspace=<id> objects=<n> elapsed_ms=<ms> concurrency=12`, and `exec-pod-bridge.service.test.ts` adds focused empty / bounded-concurrency / download-failure / non-zero-exit coverage.
- **Change (ADR-127 W1 — manifest-as-index, create-side; D1 + D3 + D4 + D5).** `workspace_file_metadata` is now the authoritative file index for the model-facing `files.list` and the UI gallery; pod FS is treated as a cache and the `assistant_chat_message_attachment` table is demoted to a chat-display join. **API.** New application services `ListWorkspaceFilesFromManifestService` (manifest read + one-level dir derivation + role classification by handle ownership) and `UpsertWorkspaceFileMetadataFromRuntimeService` (validates `/shared/`-only, rejects `..` traversal). New controller `InternalWorkspaceFilesController` mounted at `/api/v1/internal/workspaces/:workspaceId/files/{list,metadata}` (internal-token auth). `ListChatWorkspaceFilesService` rewritten — manifest is primary, attachment table joined LEFT by `storagePath` (latest by `createdAt`); manifest entries with no attachment row become orphan tiles with `chatId: null` / `messageId: null` / inferred `attachmentType`; voice-note and external-download filters retained; `ChatWorkspaceFileTile.chatId/messageId` widened to nullable. `MediaDeliveryService` gained `downloadWorkspaceFileByPath` / `previewWorkspaceFileByPath` (manifest lookup + GCS via `buildSharedObjectKey`; 404 if no manifest row, 410 if GCS lost the bytes). `MediaAttachmentController` exposes workspace-scoped `GET /assistant/workspaces/:workspaceId/files?path=&download=0|1` and `/files/preview?path=` (auth re-uses `resolveRequestAssistant` and asserts the workspaceId matches); chat-scoped endpoints kept for backward compatibility. **Runtime.** `RuntimeFilesToolService.executeListAction` now delegates `/shared/...` listings to a new `executeListFromManifest` that calls `PersaiInternalApiClientService.listWorkspaceFilesFromManifest` instead of running a sandbox `find` (so listings reflect manifest truth, not stale pod FS); `/workspace/...` keeps the sandbox path. `executeWriteAction` now upserts the manifest after a successful sandbox write on `/shared/...` via the new `upsertWorkspaceFileMetadata` client method — best-effort, failure logged at warn, write outcome still surfaced to the model. `inferMimeForWrite` derives the manifest MIME from the path extension (with a JSON heuristic and `text/plain` fallback). **Web.** `ChatWorkspaceFileTile.chatId/messageId` widened to `string | null`; new `buildWorkspaceFileUrl` helper mirrors `buildChatFileUrl` against the new workspace-scoped endpoints. `WorkspaceFilesGallery` takes a new `workspaceId: string | null` prop and uses a new `buildTileUrl` helper to pick between chat-scoped and workspace-scoped URLs based on `tile.chatId` everywhere a URL is built (preview src, download url, thumbnail, poster, lightbox, tile menu, "open in new tab"). Orphan-tile delete is short-circuited with a `console.warn` until the workspace-scoped DELETE lands in W3. `AssistantSettings` threads `assistant?.workspaceId ?? null` into the gallery. **Tests.** `list-chat-workspace-files.service.test.ts` rewritten to drive the manifest path with attachment-backed + orphan + voice + external-download + filtered + paginated cases. New `list-workspace-files-from-manifest.service.test.ts` (7 cases — prefix validation, dir derivation, role classification by handle, deep sub-prefix, empty result, input parsing). New `upsert-workspace-file-metadata-from-runtime.service.test.ts` (6 cases — happy path, `shortDescription` propagation, `/workspace/` reject, `..` reject, non-finite/negative sizeBytes reject, non-object body reject). `runtime-files-tool.service.test.ts` gained 5 W1 cases — `/shared/` list reads manifest API and skips sandbox; `/workspace/` list keeps sandbox find; `/shared/` write upserts manifest with correct payload; `/workspace/` write does NOT upsert; manifest upsert failure is swallowed and the write still succeeds. (Three pre-existing `files.attach happy path` failures in the same file are out of W1 scope — confirmed present at baseline `cf8f2963`.) **Out of W1 (later waves):** D6 parallel cold-start hydrate, D7 delete-side symmetry (workspace-scoped DELETE + orphan delete UI), D8 `isAttachmentRef` `objectKey` fallback drop, D9 `PERSAI_MEDIA_OBJECT_PREFIX` rename, D10 GCS wipe runbook execution. **Gate (all green, local).** lint PASS · format:check PASS · api/runtime/web typechecks PASS · `pnpm --filter @persai/api run test` PASS · `pnpm --filter @persai/runtime run test` PASS. **No commit/push yet** per the standing rule.

- **Fix (ADR-126 v3 — `image_edit` deferred enqueue attachment validation).** Live dev: vision saw uploaded JPEGs but `image_edit` failed with `runtime_degraded` / "attachments must contain valid runtime attachment refs". Root cause: ADR-126 v3 renamed `RuntimeAttachmentRef.objectKey` → `storagePath` and `filename` → `displayName`, but `EnqueueRuntimeDeferredMediaJobService.isAttachmentRef` and `WorkspaceMediaJobSchedulerService.isAttachmentRef` still validated the retired fields — every enqueue with a real attachment was rejected at parse. Fix: both validators now accept `storagePath` (with legacy `objectKey` fallback for persisted job payloads). Test: new `image_edit` + `storagePath` parse/enqueue case in `enqueue-runtime-deferred-media-job.service.test.ts`.

- **Fix (ADR-126 v3 amendment — model-canonical /shared/... path translation + hot-pod inbound bytes-push).** Two coupled live-regression fixes from the dev cluster (user-visible: uploaded images showed "0 byte" / "file not found" to the model). (a) `apps/sandbox/src/workspace-path.ts:assertAllowedMountPrefix` now translates the model-facing canonical `/shared/<input|outbound>/<...>` (no workspaceId — the model never sees it) into the pod-physical `/shared/<workspaceId>/<...>` shape before the prefix check. The unknown-handle outbound reject path is preserved. (b) New control-plane endpoint `POST /api/v1/jobs/shared-inbound-write` (sandbox) + `SandboxControlPlaneClientService` (api) wired into `manage-chat-media.stageForWebThread` as a best-effort push: after the GCS upload succeeds the api forwards the bytes through the sandbox bridge into the workspace's already-`Running` session pod via the new `WorkspaceFileBridgeService.writeSharedInputControlPlane` + `ExecPodBridgeService.tryExecShellInExistingSessionPod` (atomic `chmod 0744 input/ && cat > input/<basename> && chmod 0444 input/<basename> && chmod 0444 input/` script that respects the D2 access matrix). If the pod is cold the bridge returns `mode: "deferred"` and the cold-start `hydrateSharedMountFromGcs` is the authoritative recovery path — GCS remains the single canonical store for inbound bytes; no double-write, no quota double-count (`media_storage_quota` on the api side stays the single accounting source). Helm: api env block in `values-dev.yaml` + `values.yaml` now sets `PERSAI_SANDBOX_BASE_URL` + `PERSAI_SANDBOX_TIMEOUT_MS`; `sandbox-ingress-runtime-only` NetworkPolicy extended with `app.kubernetes.io/name: api` as a second pod selector. ADR: top-of-file Amendment 2026-06-25 block. Tests: 6 new path-translation tests + 4 new `writeSharedInputControlPlane` tests (written / deferred / failed / basename-validation) — both suites green. Also fixes the CI failure of the previous push (`apps/runtime/test/runtime-config.test.ts:30` updated to expect `"assistant-media"` instead of `undefined` for `PERSAI_MEDIA_OBJECT_PREFIX`, matching the 2026-06-24 schema default).

- **Fix (ADR-126 v3).** `files.attach` now binds to the assistant message via the artifact pipeline; mid-turn `registerChatAttachment` was removed, and `resolveRuntimeMessageId` no longer falls back to `userMessageId`.
- **Fix (ADR-126 v3 — runtime media-prefix regression).** Every web/telegram chat turn carrying an image attachment failed with `Chat runtime is temporarily unreachable` because `runtime-config` / `sandbox-config` declared `PERSAI_MEDIA_OBJECT_PREFIX` as optional with no default, and the runtime helm env block did not enumerate the variable, so `PersaiMediaObjectStorageService.getObjectPrefix()` threw inside `TurnContextHydrationService.downloadDirectInputAttachmentBytes` and the entire turn rejected. Fix: schema default `"assistant-media"` is now the source of truth in both `packages/config/src/runtime-config.ts` and `packages/config/src/sandbox-config.ts` (matches the existing api-side default), and the helm runtime env block in `values-dev.yaml` + `values.yaml` now lists the variable explicitly for operators. Test fixtures across runtime + sandbox (8 files) were widened to populate the now-required field; runtime + api + sandbox typechecks green.
