- **Change (ADR-126 v3 — path-identity cutover; all six waves + closure landed locally; supersedes v2 Slice 3).** v3 collapses the file system identity model to a single tuple `(workspaceId, path)` end-to-end. The v2 transitional shape — `assistant_files` metadata row + `fileRef` UI identity hop + `/assistant-media/<fileRef>` GCS prefix — is fully retired. Implementation followed `docs/ADR/126-v3-CUTOVER-PROGRAM.md`: six orchestrated Composer-2.5 subagent waves (W1 DB / W2 API / W3.1-W3.3 runtime / W4 sandbox / W4.5 thumbnails / W5 web / W6a cleanup) plus a Closure phase (OpenAPI surgery + lint+format auto-fix + GCS wipe runbook + docs). Two waves (W2, W3.1) were force-redone after orchestrator verification caught a dual-write bridge and type-system fraud (`as unknown as X`, `"file" + "Ref"` grep evasion); permanent anti-compromise red flags now live in the program doc. **DB.** Schema dropped `model AssistantFile`, `AssistantUploadMicroDescriptionJob`, `AssistantDocumentDeliveredFile`, `AssistantFileMediaDerivative`, all back-relation `AssistantFile[]` arrays, and `assistant_file_id` from `AssistantChatMessageAttachment`; repurposed `assistant_chat_message_attachments.storage_path VARCHAR(1024)` from GCS-key semantics to canonical FS-path semantics; added `WorkspaceFileMetadata` (PK `(workspaceId, path)`, FK cascade to `workspaces`); added `thumbnail_storage_path` and `poster_storage_path` columns. Migrations `20260623230000_adr126_v3_drop_assistant_files_and_path_identity` (data-fills `storage_path = NULL` + `processing_status = 'unavailable'` for any row whose value `LIKE 'assistant-media/%'`) and `20260624120000_adr126_v3_thumbnail_path_identity`. **Runtime contract.** `RuntimeFileRef` renamed to `RuntimeFileHandle` (path-based, `{ workspaceId, path }`). `RuntimeOutputArtifact` + `RuntimeAttachmentRef` carry `storagePath` only. Cross-chat revise JSDoc rewritten to path identity. **Runtime tools.** `files.attach({path})` calls the new `registerChatAttachment` API. `files.preview` routes through sandbox read (no `lookupAssistantFileByWorkspaceRelPath` fallback). Manifest enrichment via renamed `listWorkspaceFileShortDescriptions` (URL `/api/v1/internal/runtime/files/short-descriptions` already path-native from W2). Sandbox `executeQueuedJob` simplified to tar-snapshot restore/save only; the entire `assistant_files`-keyed workspace-shadow mechanism (12 helpers) deleted. `workspace-gc.service.ts` raw-SQL DELETE retargeted from the dropped `assistant_files` table to `workspace_file_metadata WHERE workspace_id=$1 AND path LIKE $2`. **API server.** New `register-chat-attachment.service.ts` (replaces `AssistantFileRegistryService` — resolves `(assistantId, channel, externalThreadKey) → AssistantChat.id`, writes one path-identity row, records optional derivatives); new `workspace-file-metadata.service.ts` + repository; new `list-workspace-file-short-descriptions.service.ts`; new `artefact-shared-outbound-write.service.ts` + sandbox client for single-write of `image_generate` / `image_edit` / `document` / `tts` / `video_generate` artefacts to `/shared/outbound/self/<basename>` (collision-suffix per `build-outbound-basename.ts`); GCS mirror via `buildSharedObjectKey` — no per-file `assistant-media/<fileRef>` dual-write. Deleted: `assistant-file-cleanup-reaper`, `assistant-file-media-derivative-scheduler`, `assistant-file-registry`, `assistant-upload-micro-description{,-scheduler,-job}`, `extract-internal-runtime-assistant-file`, `media/assistant-file-media-derivative.service.ts`. **W4.5 thumbnails (added when W5 UX review exposed the empty-tile risk).** `media/inbound-media.service.ts` now synchronously calls `MediaPreprocessorService.createImageThumbnail` (skipping GIF/SVG) for images and `createVideoPoster` for videos after the quota gate; derivatives land at canonical `.thumb.webp` / `.poster.jpg` paths beside the primary file and are persisted on the attachment row (not quota-billed). **Web (W5).** DELETED `apps/web/app/api/assistant-file/[fileRef]/route.ts` and `assistant-files-manager.tsx`. NEW `workspace-files-gallery.tsx` — founder-approved 4-column tile gallery, All/Images/Videos/Documents filter pills, sort `createdAt DESC`, thumb/poster tiles with MIME-icon fallback, click→lightbox or download, cursor pagination via `listChatWorkspaceFiles`. REWRITTEN `project-files-panel.tsx` — collapsed by default, single-line "Файлы проекта" link, click dispatches `assistant-settings-open-tab=files` event (NOT inline expand); dedupes by `storagePath`. REWRITTEN `assistant-settings.tsx` Files tab hosts the new gallery and auto-opens on the dispatched event. `chat-message.tsx` + `use-chat.ts` use `path`/`thumbnailStoragePath`/`posterStoragePath` and build URLs via `buildChatFileUrl`. `assistant-api-client.ts` removed `getAssistantFiles` / `AssistantFileState` / `getAssistantFileDownloadUrl` / `deleteAssistantFile` etc.; added `buildChatFileUrl` / `listChatWorkspaceFiles` / `deleteChatWorkspaceFile`. **Contracts (Closure).** `packages/contracts/openapi.yaml` surgically lost 3 dead endpoints (`/assistant/files`, `/assistant/files/{fileRef}`, `/assistant/files/{fileRef}/download`) and 7 dead schemas (`AssistantFileState`, `AssistantFilesCleanupSummary`, `GetAssistantFilesResponse`, `GetAssistantFileResponse`, `AssistantFileDocumentLink` + inline enums); `AssistantWebChatMessageAttachmentState` + `StageAttachmentAttachment` rewritten to mirror production export shape (`path` + `thumbnailStoragePath` + `posterStoragePath`; no `fileRef`/`thumbnailFileRef`/`posterFileRef`/`derivativesStatus`/`fileDeleted`). ## 2026-06-23

- **Change (ADR-126 v2 Slice 3 — unified files contract cutover, closed cleanly).** Slice 3 lands the full path-only `files.*` cutover with no transitional dual-write and no parallel legacy code paths (per ADR's hard contract). The previously partial state — sandbox dispatcher referencing three unwritten methods, legacy `fileRef`-based model guidance, dead legacy `executeFiles{Read,Write,Edit,Delete}Action` private methods, no FS-level chmod enforcement, no upload bytes mirror, zero focused tests for the new sandbox modules — was closed via an orchestrated subagent program (Phases A → G). **Schema + handle.** `Assistant.handle` `VARCHAR(64)` unique per workspace, deterministic backfill (slug → numeric suffix → `a-<hex-of-id>` fallback), migration `20260623160000_adr126_slice3_assistant_handle_and_gc_lease` + `SandboxWorkspaceGcLease` lease table. `PrismaAssistantRepository.create` mints the UUID + handle in a single transaction; bundle materialization populates `assistantHandle` + `siblingAssistantHandles` from the column + sibling query. **Runtime contract — breaking removal.** `PERSAI_RUNTIME_FILES_TOOL_ACTIONS` cut from 11 → 5 (`list | read | preview | write | delete`); `RuntimeFilesToolItem` rewritten path-only (`path`/`type`/`role`/`sizeBytes`/`mimeType`/`modifiedAt`/optional `shortDescription`); `RuntimeFilesToolResult` collapsed; `RuntimeSandboxJobRequest.{assistantHandle, siblingHandles}` required, `mountedFileRefs` removed. **Native projection.** `files` tool schema path-only — no `fileRef`/`alias`/`query`/`search`/`inspect`/`get`/`edit`/`send`/`write_and_send`. **Runtime files tool.** Every action routes to a sandbox job; preview uses a `lookupAssistantFileByWorkspaceRelPath` + `extractAssistantFileText` fallback for binary previews (ADR-116 cache survives on the delivery side only); manifest enrichment via new `listAssistantFileShortDescriptions` reads the cached `shortDescription` from `assistant_files.metadata`. **Sandbox dispatcher + bridge.** `SandboxService.executeTool` routes `files`/`grep`/`glob` exclusively through new pod-exec methods (`executeFilesBridgeAction`, `executeGrepActionViaPodExec`, `executeGlobActionViaPodExec`) into `WorkspaceFileBridgeService.workspaceFile{Write,Read,List,Stat,Delete}` (and `rg`/`fd` shells in the session pod). All seven legacy private methods deleted; `runTrustedControlPlaneBinary` + orphaned helpers removed. **`/shared/<wsid>/` mount.** Per-pod emptyDir + 4-phase bootstrap: marker check → `mkdir`+`ln -sfn outbound/self` → GCS hydrate (`SandboxObjectStorageService.listPrefix` enumerates `workspaces/<wsid>/shared/`, each blob piped into the pod via `cat > <path>`) → chmod 0444 on `input/`, 0755 on `outbound/<self>/`, 0555 on every sibling `outbound/<other>/`. Deferral comments removed. **Upload bytes mirror (Pattern B, GCS-first lazy hydrate).** `PersaiMediaObjectStorageService.buildSharedObjectKey` + `AssistantFileRegistryService.mirrorUploadToSharedGcs` write the same bytes to `workspaces/<wsid>/shared/input/<sanitized-basename>` for `origin=uploaded_attachment`. Best-effort: failure logs `assistant_file_shared_hydrate_failed` and marks `metadata.sharedHydrationStatus=pending`; never fails the upload. Pod bootstrap pulls these on first creation. **GC reaper.** `WorkspaceGcService` cron (`SANDBOX_GC_INTERVAL_MS`, default 300 s) drains the 3 lease kinds: `chat_scratch` (now), `assistant_outbound` (+7d), `workspace_shared` (+30d). Lease metadata Zod-validated; failed leases stay open + emit `workspace_gc_purge_failed`. **Audit + metrics.** `workspace_file_written|read|listed|stat|deleted`, `workspace_gc_purged`, `workspace_gc_purge_failed`; `sandbox_workspace_file_{write|read|list|stat|delete}_latency_ms` histograms; `sandbox_workspace_quota_bytes_used` + `sandbox_shared_quota_bytes_used` gauges. **Legacy guidance removed.** `runtime-tool-policy.ts` + `tool-catalog-data.ts` `files.modelUsageGuidance` rewritten path-only (full ADR D8 manifest economy is Slice 5). `turn-execution.service.ts` developer block already path-only. `sanitize-tool-result-for-model.ts` legacy fileRef-shape detector deleted. `runtime-assistant-file-registry.service.ts` `toRuntimeFilesToolItem` returns the internal `RuntimeFileRef` (chat-delivery identity) instead of the dead legacy `RuntimeFilesToolItem`-with-fileRef shape. **Tests.** 47 new focused cases (`workspace-path.test.ts` 21, `workspace-file-bridge.service.test.ts` 15, `workspace-gc.service.test.ts` 8); `sandbox.service.test.ts` rewritten to the new contract (6-arg constructors, `mountFileRefs` in args, handle/siblings on every job request, legacy `executeFilesEditAction` + grep/glob trusted-binary tests deleted); 17 runtime test files updated with `assistantHandle`/`siblingAssistantHandles` on bundle metadata; legacy `runtime-files-tool.service.test.ts` (11-action surface) deleted; `sandbox-client.service.test.ts` `mountedFileRefs` removed. **Deliberately deferred per ADR slice ownership.** Slice 4: `files.attach({path})` + image/document dual-write into `/shared/outbound/self/`. Slice 5: tool-catalog manifest economy (summary header + cheap-LLM `shortDescription` pipeline + D13 migration audit + plan-baseline 500 MB data migration). Slice 6: layered snapshot for `/workspace/` (install vs scratch content-hash split). Gate: `corepack pnpm -r --if-present run lint` PASS · `corepack pnpm run format:check` PASS · `corepack pnpm -r --if-present run typecheck` PASS (all packages) · sandbox focused tests 77/77 PASS · runtime isolated suite 14/14 PASS. **Pre-deploy:** migration `20260623160000` pauses on `persai-dev-migrations` env per CI policy; coordinate the helm pin with migration approval. **Schema (`apps/api/prisma/schema.prisma`, new migration `20260623160000_adr126_slice3_assistant_handle_and_gc_lease`).** Adds `Assistant.handle` (`String @db.VarChar(64)`, unique on `(workspaceId, handle)`) with deterministic CTE-driven backfill — `lower → [a-z0-9-] → trim → 32-char cap` from `draft_display_name`, numeric collision suffixes per workspace, `a-<8-hex-of-id>` fallback when the display name yields nothing — then `NOT NULL` + unique index. Adds `SandboxWorkspaceGcLease` + `SandboxWorkspaceGcLeaseKind` enum (`chat_scratch | assistant_outbound | workspace_shared`) — lifecycle-independent of the source rows (Assistant/Workspace/AssistantChat hard-delete stays as-is); lease metadata is JSONB validated by Zod at reap time. **API.** New `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/assistant-handle.ts` exposes `generateAssistantHandle` / `slugify` / `applyCollisionSuffix` / `ensureHandleUnique` / `buildAssistantHandle`. `PrismaAssistantRepository.create` mints the UUID client-side and threads it as the slugger's fallback seed inside a Prisma transaction so the handle is present at row birth. `AdminDeleteUserService` writes a `kind=assistant_outbound` lease (`metadata={workspaceId, handle}`, `scheduledAt=now()+7d`) before `tx.assistant.delete(...)`, and a `kind=workspace_shared` lease (`scheduledAt=now()+30d`) before `tx.workspace.delete(...)`. `PrismaAssistantChatRepository.hardDeleteChat` (new `options?: { workspaceId }` arg) writes a `kind=chat_scratch` lease (`metadata={workspaceId, assistantId}`, `scheduledAt=now()`) before the chat row is removed. `AssistantFileRegistryService.ensureAttachmentFile` now persists `assistant_files.metadata.workspaceRelPath = "/shared/input/<sanitized-basename>"` for `origin = uploaded_attachment` so the new model-facing path is addressable and the workspace-shared GC reaper can find these rows by prefix. **Sandbox runtime.** `ExecPodBridgeService` now mounts a per-workspace `/shared/<workspaceId>/` emptyDir (size from new `SANDBOX_SHARED_EMPTYDIR_SIZE_MIB`, default 512 MiB) on every session pod; `runInPod` / `warmSessionPod` / `ensureSessionPodRunning` thread the assistant's `handle` and sibling handles so the new bootstrap script creates `input/`, `outbound/<self>`, `outbound/<sibling>` + the `outbound/self` symlink deterministically; new primitives `execShellInSessionPod`, `isSessionPodWarm`, `listWarmSessionPodsForWorkspace`; `execCommand` accepts optional stdin. New `apps/sandbox/src/workspace-path.ts` (POSIX normalize + clamp + `assertAllowedMountPrefix` returning `ResolvedWorkspacePath` keyed by role — `workspace | shared_input | shared_outbound_self | shared_outbound_sibling_ro`). New `apps/sandbox/src/workspace-file-bridge.service.ts` with `workspaceFile{Write,Read,List,Stat,Delete}` — every operation routes through `ExecPodBridgeService.execShellInSessionPod`, enforces path containment, emits per-op latency + audit events. New `apps/sandbox/src/workspace-audit.service.ts` (structured `shared_input_published`, `workspace_file_written|read|listed|stat|deleted`, `workspace_gc_purged`, `workspace_gc_purge_failed`). New `apps/sandbox/src/workspace-gc.service.ts` cron (new `SANDBOX_GC_INTERVAL_MS`, default 300 s) drains lease rows by kind: `chat_scratch` purges `/workspace/chats/<chatId>` in every warm pod for that assistant+workspace + drops the GCS snapshot subtree + deletes `assistant_files` matching `workspaceRelPath LIKE '/workspace/chats/<chatId>/%'`; `assistant_outbound` drops the `workspaces/<wsid>/shared/outbound/<handle>/` GCS prefix + rm's the warm-pod mount + deletes `assistant_files` matching `/shared/outbound/<handle>/%`; `workspace_shared` drops the full `workspaces/<wsid>/shared/` GCS prefix + rm's `/shared/<wsid>/*` in every warm pod + deletes `assistant_files` matching `/shared/%`. Failed leases stay open for retry; successful ones set `purged_at`. `SandboxObservabilityService` + `SandboxMetricsService` add `sandbox_workspace_file_{write|read|list|stat|delete}_latency_ms` histograms and `sandbox_workspace_quota_bytes_used` / `sandbox_shared_quota_bytes_used` gauges. `SandboxObjectStorageService` adds `buildSharedObjectKey`, `buildSharedPrefix`, `deletePrefix`. `SandboxService.executeQueuedJob` resolves `assistantHandle` + `siblingHandles` once per job (request payload first, DB fallback, deterministic `a-<hex-of-id>` final fallback for mock-prisma tolerance) and threads them through `executeTool` → `executeExecLike` / `executeRenderHtmlToPdf` / `executeDocumentCode` → `runInPod`. **Runtime contract (`packages/runtime-contract/src/index.ts`).** Additive only — new `PERSAI_RUNTIME_FILES_TOOL_PATH_ACTIONS` (`list | read | preview | write | delete`), `RuntimeFilesToolPathAction`, `RuntimeFilesToolPathItem`; optional `path` / `pathItem` / `pathItems` on `RuntimeFilesToolResult`; optional `assistantHandle` / `siblingHandles` on `RuntimeSandboxJobRequest`; `mountedFileRefs` flipped to optional. Legacy `fileRef` actions/shapes remain so existing skill content keeps working. **Config (`packages/config/src/sandbox-config.ts`).** Only two new env vars: `SANDBOX_SHARED_EMPTYDIR_SIZE_MIB` (default 512), `SANDBOX_GC_INTERVAL_MS` (default 300_000). No other env additions. **Sandbox tests.** `apps/sandbox/test/exec-pod-bridge.service.test.ts` + `apps/sandbox/test/sandbox-metrics.service.test.ts` fixtures supply the two new env vars and inject `assistantHandle` / `siblingHandles` into every `runInPod` / `warmSessionPod` call so the new required parameters compile. **Lease writes are deliberately not cross-process from API → sandbox in this slice** (no new HTTP route); chat-scratch's `scheduledAt = now()` means the next reaper tick (≤ 5 minutes) processes it. Gate: `corepack pnpm -r --if-present run lint` PASS · `corepack pnpm run format:check` PASS · `corepack pnpm -r --if-present run typecheck` PASS (every package). Sandbox unit tests under `apps/sandbox/test/` partially exercised; full deferred test surface (`workspace-file-bridge.service.test.ts`, `workspace-gc.service.test.ts`, dedicated `workspace-path.ts` containment tests) is staged for the follow-up slice along with the breaking contract removals. **Migration pauses on the `persai-dev-migrations` GitHub Environment per CI policy.** Effective after the next dev image pin + migration approval.

- **Doc (ADR-126 v2 — unified sandbox workspace; multi-assistant, manifest, GC, snapshot).** ADR-126 rewritten from the original four-point draft (bash, unified `/workspace`, expanded egress, image baseline) into a production-grade design with thirteen explicit decisions and a six-slice implementation program. Adds the per-`businessWorkspaceId` `/shared/` mount (with `input/` + `outbound/<assistant-handle>/` substructure, `self` symlink, FS-level `0555` for siblings' outbound) alongside per-assistant `/workspace/`, retiring `fileRef` from the model-facing API entirely; introduces `files.attach({path})` as the explicit publish channel for arbitrary file types; dual-writes `image_generate` / `image_edit` / `document` outputs into `/shared/outbound/self/` so the producing assistant can post-process; adds context-economical developer prompt manifest (summary header + current-turn attachments inline, on-demand `files.list` / `files.preview`, cached `shortDescription`, system noise hidden by default); adds `/workspace/chats/<chatId>/` chat-scoped scratch namespace + `/workspace/lib/` reusable-scripts directory with `shell` default `cwd`; pins snapshot layering + warm-pool + explicit latency budget (warm `files.write` ≤ 300 ms p95, cold first ≤ 8 s p95); makes GC lifecycle explicit for chat / assistant / business-workspace deletion (0 / 7 / 30 day grace windows); adds audit events (`workspace_file_written`, `workspace_file_read`, `shared_outbound_published`) + metrics (`workspace_file_write_latency_ms`, `snapshot_cold_pull_latency_ms`, `shared_quota_bytes_used`) + egress-log tool attribution; and gates the program's final push on an empty active-surface `fileRef`-migration audit report. Acceptance criteria expanded from 11 to 20 cases, including the founder's exact 2026-06-22 failure scenario, cross-sibling visibility without re-upload, FS-level write rejection, latency budget, GC purge timing, quota error classes, and the migration-audit empty report against live `persai-dev`. Doc-only; `corepack pnpm run format:check` PASS.

- **Performance (post-turn cleanup parallelization).** Web stream/sync post-runtime cleanup now removes safe serialized waits after assistant-message persistence: `finalizePersistedWebTurn` starts active media-job read, active document-job read, and web media delivery together; quota usage recording and model-cost ledger append now run together after final delivery-honesty content is known; `completeWebTurnReplay` writes durable turn-attempt and surface-binding replay state together. Stream and sync callers now run replay cleanup and skill-state persistence concurrently via shared `Promise.allSettled` handling, keeping skill-state non-blocking and follow-up delivery synchronous so the same-turn `followUpAssistantMessage` payload is preserved. Telegram has no replay/skill equivalent, but its independent quota/ledger tail now runs concurrently with the same quota non-blocking semantics.

- **Fix (Slice 6 v2: one-badge-top + passive labels + persisted toolInvocations).** Live validation of the Slice 6 web assistant working-content UI exposed three issues in the just-landed baseline `d852af7f`: committed assistant messages could render a process badge between long content blocks, RU labels used gendered active verbs such as "Сделал" despite female assistant settings, and backend persistence/SSE never carried `toolInvocations`, so specialized labels like `Найдено · N источников` could not appear after completion or refresh. This slice fixes all four linked surfaces without touching runtime execution or Prisma schema. **Slice 6.A:** `apps/web/messages/{ru,en}.json` now use passive/gender-neutral process badge labels (`Выполнено`, `Найдено`, `Сгенерировано`, `Прочитано`, `Подготовлено`, `Записано`, `Запущено`; EN `Done`, `Found`, `Generated`, `Read`, etc.), and `resolveProcessBadgeLabel` now recognizes `web_search`, `knowledge_search`, `knowledge_fetch`, `web_fetch`, image/video/document, files read/write/list/preview, and `shell`, with mixed process pieces falling back to generic `Done/Выполнено`. **Slice 6.B:** `buildIterationBlocks` now has committed and streaming modes: committed messages collapse all short text/tool process pieces into one top-of-bubble badge and render structural markdown content blocks after it, while streaming preserves per-content-boundary live ordering. **Slice 6.C:** completed stream payloads, stream replay payloads, and sync web responses/replays now include stripped `assistantMessage.toolInvocations` when present. **Slice 6.D:** `persistAssistantMessage` stores stripped `metadata.toolInvocations` for web stream, web sync, and Telegram turns; `web-chat-message-state.mapper` projects them back into chat history; `billingFacts` is stripped by the shared `stripToolInvocationsForClient` helper before DB/client transport. Tests: `chat-message.test.tsx` now covers passive labels, committed collapse, streaming interleaving, single/mixed tool labels, image_edit/document/shell labels, and expanded chronological order; API focused tests cover metadata persistence/empty skip/billingFacts stripping, stream completed transport, and chat-history projection. Focused gate PASS: web chat-message 55/55, `persist-assistant-message`, `stream-web-chat-turn.service`, and `manage-web-chat-list.service`.

- **Change (deferred-tail continuation + assistant working-content inline UI).** Slice 2 softens the runtime developer tail for accepted async media/document jobs without weakening ADR-105 honesty: the follow-up instruction no longer says "Write only a brief acknowledgement", still forbids claiming pending media/documents are ready/visible/attached/sent, still forbids raw tool JSON/job ids/imagined details, still blocks `files.send` for pending documents, and now explicitly allows independent same-turn work, plan advancement, other tool calls, or additional background jobs without waiting for user confirmation between independent jobs. Slice 6 replaces the web assistant `WorkingTextBlocks` "Выполнено/Done" disclosure with hybrid rendering: structural markdown in `workingNotes` (tables, headings, fenced code, lists of 3+ items) renders inline as normal assistant content; short process text and tool-only steps collapse into process badges with adaptive labels for search, image generation, page reads, or generic worked steps; final `answerText` remains inline. Web message/client types now carry optional `toolInvocations` when present so the UI can reconstruct `text[i] -> tools[iteration=i] -> final` order; older messages without tool metadata degrade gracefully to text/content handling. Tests pin the new runtime tail wording and add chat-message coverage for content/process/mixed ordering, empty-note skipping, expansion contents, and empty final-answer-only messages. Gate: requested AGENTS sequence PASS (`@persai/runtime` lint/typecheck, `@persai/api` typecheck, `@persai/web` typecheck/lint, format check, runtime isolated suite via `tsx test/run-suite-isolated.ts`, full web test suite).

## 2026-06-22

- **Change (ADR-125 Amendment 3: post-final self-check hop + completed-plan scenario release).** Founder screenshot review on 2026-06-22 exposed three plan/scenario gaps after Amendment 2: completed-only prompt windows suppressed scenario re-intake because `selectChatPlanWindow` intentionally carries the two most recent completed rows; fully completed active scenarios had no explicit release pressure; and a turn that did substantive tool work could still finalize a closing assistant reply while the user-visible plan card showed open rows. The fix stays model-owned and scoped to ADR-125: no server-side auto-`skill.release`, no `toolMutatesVolatilePrefix` expansion, no feature flag. In `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/build-system-reminder-blocks.service.ts`, scenario intake suppression now checks only open rows (`pending` / `in_progress`), so completed-only windows no longer block a fresh model-authored intake; the service now documents and emits six reminder classes in order (scenario tick → reference image → scenario plan intake → chat-plan lifecycle → scenario completion/release → budget warnings); the new completion/release reminder fires when a scenario is active and every windowed row is `completed`, includes `scenario.exitCondition` truncated to 300 chars, and tells the model to call `skill({action:"release"})` before replying unless the user's latest intent continues the same scenario, in which case it should add fresh `todo_write` rows. In `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/turn-execution.service.ts`, `PreparedTurnExecution` gains `selfCheckHopsRemaining: 2`, and both sync and streaming paths run a guarded post-final self-check after existing assistant-text corrections and before `finalizeAcceptedTurnWithPostTurnEffects`: read a fresh chat plan through `buildChatPlanBlock(input)`, require open rows plus substantive work excluding pure `todo_write`, inject a `<system-reminder>` after the just-finished assistant text, perform one non-streaming provider call, execute only `todo_write` follow-up calls through the existing `executeProjectedToolCall` path, then allow one final text call; non-`todo_write` follow-up tools are rejected and logged, empty/error self-check output falls back to the original final text, and streaming emits an extra visible delta only when self-check replaces the text. Tests: `apps/runtime/test/build-system-reminder-blocks.service.test.ts` adds completed-only intake, pending/in_progress suppression controls, release reminder presence/absence, exit-condition truncation, and empty-vs-completed ordering coverage; `apps/runtime/test/turn-execution.service.test.ts` adds the ADR-125 Amendment 3 integration block covering self-check fires, clean-plan skip, no-substantive-work skip, todo_write reconciliation, non-todo rejection, exception fallback, and the no-recursive-self-check cap. Docs: `docs/ADR/125-in-chat-todo-write-and-scenario-seeded-plan.md` gains Amendment 3; `docs/SESSION-HANDOFF.md` records the checkpoint. Gate: focused reminder + turn-execution tests PASS; full requested AGENTS gate pending in this session report. Effective after the next dev runtime image pin (no Prisma changes, no provider-contract changes).

- **Change (deferred-job assistant reply: model-owned text, normalization downgraded to fallback).** Founder follow-up to the ADR-125 Amendment 2 push: every deferred background job (`image_generate`, `image_edit`, `video_generate`, every `document` job — `create_pdf_document`, `create_presentation`, `revise_document`, `create_data_document`, `export_or_redeliver`) was unconditionally overwriting the model's assistant text with a canonical "Запрос принят. Делаю изображение…" / "Request accepted. I am preparing the document…" line, both in the streaming web path and the sync TG path. This stripped legitimate explanations the model had already streamed (carousel brief, scenario step continuation, mixed accepted+rejected explanations) — founder phrased it as "часто модель пишет объяснение а потом всё стирается и заменяется". The original ADR-105 motivation (prevent false "вот картинка / документ готов" claims) is now redundantly enforced upstream by the developer-tail `buildDeferredMediaFollowUpInstruction` / `buildDeferredDocumentFollowUpInstruction` and the global `DELIVERY_HONESTY_CONTRACT` (CHANGELOG 2026-05-31). Founder picked **A — calibration only, no new ADR**: keep the canonical line strictly as a fallback for the empty-reply case, preserve any non-empty model text verbatim. Implementation: `applyDeferredMediaAcknowledgementCorrection` and `applyDeferredDocumentAcknowledgementCorrection` (in `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/turn-execution.service.ts`) now early-return the normalized model text when it is non-empty; the canonical "Запрос принят / Request accepted" lines apply only when the model produced nothing after the deferred job. The wrapper `applyAssistantTextCorrections` no longer threads `hadRejectedMediaRequest` because the same "non-empty wins" rule covers the mixed accepted+rejected media case the old ADR-105 branch was guarding. The dead-stub `TurnExecutionState.hadRejectedMediaRequest` field, the write-only `markRejectedMediaRequestIfApplicable(...)` helper, and both call sites in `processToolOutcomeIntoTurnState` are removed cleanly (PersAI rule: "no dead stubs"). One code path serves stream, sync, and Telegram — one fix, three surfaces. Tests: `apps/runtime/test/deferred-media-acknowledgement.test.ts` rewritten — three legacy force-replace assertions replaced with model-text-preservation assertions; two new cases added (empty-text → canonical RU fallback, whitespace-only text → canonical RU fallback). `apps/runtime/test/deferred-document-acknowledgement.test.ts` — single legacy "replaces false completion claims" test replaced with three: preserve non-empty text verbatim, fallback canonical line on empty, whitespace-only safety. `docs/TEST-PLAN.md` ADR-105 focused-checks bullet 5 rewritten to describe the model-owned-reply policy, the developer-tail honesty enforcement, and the empty-reply fallback (removes the now-stale `hadRejectedMediaRequest` reference). Files: `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/turn-execution.service.ts`, `apps/runtime/test/deferred-media-acknowledgement.test.ts`, `apps/runtime/test/deferred-document-acknowledgement.test.ts`, `docs/TEST-PLAN.md`, `docs/SESSION-HANDOFF.md`, `docs/CHANGELOG.md`. Gate: full repo lint PASS · `format:check` PASS · `@persai/runtime` / `@persai/api` / `@persai/web` typecheck PASS · full `@persai/runtime` test suite 239/241 PASS (the remaining 2 — `blocks files.send|write_and_send while a document from the same turn is pending delivery` — fail identically on `main` baseline `4d9c2364`; surfaced in handoff; pre-existing test-fixture bug, unrelated to this slice; not blocking). Effective after the next dev runtime image pin (no Prisma changes, no contract changes).

- **Change (ADR-125 Amendment 2: mid-loop volatile-prefix refresh after `skill.engage` / `todo_write`).** Live trace of chat `web-1782153682653` showed Amendment 1's intake `<system-reminder>` firing one turn late: the model called `skill.engage(scenarioKey="instagram_carousel")` inside Turn 2 but did NOT also author `todo_write({action:"add", …})` on the same turn; the plan was created only on Turn 3, after the next user message. Root cause: the volatile prefix (`<persai_active_scenario>` + `<persai_chat_plan>` + `<system-reminder>` blocks) was assembled exactly once in `prepareTurnExecution` from the `skillStateContext` snapshot taken at turn-prep, so any `skill.engage` / `skill.release` / `todo_write` call inside the tool loop mutated DB state but the prompt the model saw on the next hop of that same turn still carried the stale prefix. Fix: rebuild the volatile prefix **inside the tool loop** after any iteration whose batch contained a tool that mutates volatile-prefix state. `PreparedTurnExecution` gains three mutable per-turn fields (`volatilePrefixLength`, `currentSkillDecisionState`, `currentTurnHasUserAttachedImage`); new private helper `refreshVolatilePrefix(execution, input, toolBudgetSnapshot)` swaps the prefix in place — `messages = [...newPrefix, ...messages.slice(oldPrefixLen)]` — preserving the base history verbatim (no `buildMessages` round-trip); `maybeApplySkillStateMutationFromTool(execution, outcome)` synthesizes the new `RuntimeSkillDecisionState` directly from a successful `skill.engage` / `skill.release` outcome payload (no extra DB read); `toolMutatesVolatilePrefix(toolName)` returns `true` for `skill` and `todo_write`. Both the sync (`executeProviderToolLoop`) and streaming (`streamAcceptedTurn`) tool loops accumulate a `volatileRefreshNeeded` flag during the batch and call the refresh helper before the next iteration's `buildToolLoopProviderRequest`. The durable-compaction refresh path (`refreshProviderRequestMessages`) is also extended to re-prepend the fresh volatile prefix (instead of silently dropping it for the rest of the turn). Cost: one `readChatPlanWindow` API call per tool batch that touched `skill` or `todo_write` (a small subset); skill state is updated in memory; base history is not re-hydrated. Tests: new Test 3 in `apps/runtime/test/turn-execution.service.test.ts` ADR-119 Slice 5 block walks the exact regression — iteration 0 with no scenario → zero reminders; iteration 0 returns `skill.engage(scenarioKey)` → iteration 1 carries the scenario tick + scenario-plan intake reminders (2 system_reminder messages). The test bundle's `governance.toolPolicies` is extended with `skill` + `todo_write` entries (save/restore around the block) so the runtime projects and dispatches the tools instead of returning `tool_not_projected`. `FakePersaiInternalApiClientService` gains `updateSkillState(...)`, `FakeTurnContextHydrationService.buildChatPlanBlock(...)` gains a queued result list. Files: `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/turn-execution.service.ts`, `apps/runtime/test/turn-execution.service.test.ts`, `docs/ADR/125-in-chat-todo-write-and-scenario-seeded-plan.md`, `docs/SESSION-HANDOFF.md`, `docs/CHANGELOG.md`. Gate: full repo lint PASS · `format:check` PASS · `@persai/runtime`/`@persai/api`/`@persai/web` typecheck PASS · full `@persai/runtime` test suite PASS (incl. the new ADR-125 Amendment 2 mid-loop case). Effective after the next dev runtime image pin (no Prisma changes, no provider-contract changes).

- **Docs (ADR-126 Accepted — doc-only — unified sandbox workspace: files↔shell single-FS contract, bash default, expanded egress).** Live agent traces on `info@general-fly.com` exposed three architectural mismatches with Claude-Code / Cursor agent semantics that the founder targets as the long-term baseline: (1) `files.write` and `shell` write to disjoint filesystems (`files.write` → `assistant_files` GCS-backed table; `shell` → exec pod `/workspace`), so a file the model writes via the `files` tool is invisible to the next `shell` step; (2) the sandbox shell is `dash`, not `bash`, so `{data,scripts,reports}` brace expansion silently creates one literal directory, `[[ … ]]` does not work, and `pipefail` is not the default; (3) the egress allowlist is LLM-host-only — `git clone https://github.com/…` fails for any non-allowlisted host, the model cannot pull standard libraries from public Git, and ad-hoc `npm install` is blocked. Per `AGENTS.md` ("every architectural change requires an ADR when it changes long-term system truth"), the cutover terms are locked in a new ADR **before** any code lands. ADR-126 is **proposed (doc-only)** — no code, no migrations, no AGENTS gate; this entry records the doc-only landing. Decision: a four-point program A+B+C+D (D1–D4 in the ADR) — **bash as `/bin/sh` for the `shell` tool**; **unified workspace FS** where `files.write/read/list/preview` repoint at the assistant-`workspaceId` exec pod's `/workspace` via tiny control-plane primitives (mirroring the `grep`/`glob` "runs on control plane, never spawns a model-visible shell" pattern from ADR-123 Slice 7), `assistant_files` retains the narrow chat-IO boundary role (input uploads hydrated into `/workspace/input/<filename>` on first touch + outbound artifact tools `document`/`image_generate` unchanged); **egress allowlist widens** to GitHub + PyPI + npm hosts (HTTPS pull/clone/fetch only, `git push` stays denied in v1 — proxy blocks `POST` to `/git-receive-pack`); **exec image baseline** preinstalls `node` + `npm` LTS and documents the session-scoped `/workspace/.local/` (pip user-site) and `/workspace/.npm-global/` (npm global prefix) ergonomics in the model-facing `shell` and `files` `modelUsageGuidance`. **Migration: none** (founder direction: "у меня реально комерческих user пока нет можно сделать сразу чисто" → prod-first cutover, no transitional dual write). Implementation plan sketched as a four-slice program (image: bash + Node 22 / egress allowlist + `POST /git-receive-pack` deny rule / files-contract rewrite + preview cache rekey / catalog + chat-uploads hydrate + plan-baseline 500 MB bump), one push at the very end (program-style, mirroring ADR-123). **13** live-`persai-dev` acceptance criteria pinned including the founder's exact failure case: `files.write({path:"hello.txt", content:"hi"}) → shell({command:"cat hello.txt"})` must return `hi`. All five Resolved decisions (founder sign-off 2026-06-22): (1) `git push` denied in v1 — egress proxy blocks `POST` to `/git-receive-pack`, reopen is an explicit follow-up addendum, not a flag; (2) Node 22 LTS — installed from NodeSource `setup_22.x`, matches the control-plane image's `node:22-bookworm-slim`; (3) Git hosts in v1 — GitHub only, GitLab/Bitbucket deferred to a one-line proxy-config follow-up once usage demands; (4) Workspace cap stays plan-managed (existing `planCatalogPlan.billingProviderHints.quotaAccounting.workspaceStorageBytesLimit`, resolved into `bundle.governance.quota.workspaceQuotaBytes` by `MaterializeAssistantPublishedVersionService.resolveWorkspaceQuotaBytes`), Slice 4 only bumps the per-plan default to 500 MB for any plan below via a one-shot data migration — no new sandbox-side cap mechanism; (5) `files.preview` cache rekey to `(assistantId, workspaceId, relPath, content_hash)` for `/workspace` paths, the `fileRef`-keyed cache for outbound artifact previews (`document`, `image_generate`) stays untouched. ADR-123 (closed) is **not** reopened — only the sandbox surface (files contract + shell defaults + egress allowlist) is refined; isolation/secret-free/lifecycle/document decisions stay locked. Files: `docs/ADR/126-unified-sandbox-workspace-files-shell-single-fs-bash-default-and-expanded-egress.md` (new), `docs/SESSION-HANDOFF.md`, `docs/CHANGELOG.md`. Gate: doc-only — no lint/typecheck/test rerun needed for the ADR itself. Effective only after a separate implementation program lands.

- **Change (ADR-125 Amendment 1: scenario plan-intake `<system-reminder>` for Option A first-move).** Live validation of the Option A pivot on user `info@general-fly.com` exposed a regression: the model engaged the carousel scenario but did not call `todo_write` until the user explicitly nudged ("Почему ты не сделал todo"). Database inspection of the deployed `persai-dev` runtime bundle confirmed both `PLAN INTAKE` (in `skill.modelUsageGuidance`) and `SCENARIO INTAKE` (in `todo_write.modelUsageGuidance`) are baked into the materialised bundle — i.e. the model sees the guidance, but tool-descriptor copy alone is too low-priority to win against the rolling user-message context on the engage-turn. The fix mirrors Claude-Code / Cursor: a per-turn `<system-reminder>` that fires at the exact moment the gap exists, riding the same volatile_context tail that already carries the chat-plan and active-scenario blocks. New reminder class **"Scenario plan intake"** in `BuildSystemReminderBlocksService` (slotted between reminders #2 image and #3 chat-plan lifecycle): fires only when `skillDecisionState` reports an active skill + active scenario, the scenario resolves in the bundle, and the windowed chat plan is empty. The reminder names the active scenario, embeds the actual `scenario.steps` list (titles derived from each `directive` via a new `deriveStepTitle` helper — sentence-boundary preference, ≤80 chars, word-boundary truncation with `…`; capped to the first 12 rendered with a "…and N more — include every step in the add call" trailer), and demands `todo_write({action:"add", items:[…]})` as the VERY NEXT action with `first item status:"in_progress", every other item status:"pending"` BEFORE replying to the user and BEFORE any other tool call. Suppression is precise: the intake reminder falls silent the moment the model authors even one row (the chat-plan lifecycle reminder takes over for the rest of the plan's life) and on any unresolvable / inactive scenario. `resolveScenario` return type tightened from `{displayName; steps: unknown[]}` to `RuntimeBundleSkillScenario | null` so the new code can read step shape safely. Zero new round-trips, zero new injections — the reminder rides the existing `chatPlanTodos` payload the lifecycle reminder already consumes. Tests: `apps/runtime/test/build-system-reminder-blocks.service.test.ts` grows from 17 → 26 cases. New cases (18–26) cover: intake fires on empty plan + active scenario, null/absent `chatPlanTodos` treated as empty, suppressed when plan has any row (even one completed) or scenario inactive/unresolvable, long directives truncate to ≤80 chars with `…`, many-step scenarios get the trailer, byte stability across invocations. Existing scenario-active cases (2, 3, 4, 9, 10) updated to pass a single completed `SILENT_PLAN` todo so the intake reminder stays suppressed where the test focuses on reminders 1/2/4/5. ADR-125 `Amendment 1` appended describing the live regression, the system-reminder design, and the acceptance criteria for both the empty-plan branch (intake) and the populated-plan branches (lifecycle). Files: `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/build-system-reminder-blocks.service.ts`, `apps/runtime/test/build-system-reminder-blocks.service.test.ts`, `docs/ADR/125-in-chat-todo-write-and-scenario-seeded-plan.md`, `docs/SESSION-HANDOFF.md`, `docs/CHANGELOG.md`. Gate: focused `tsx test/build-system-reminder-blocks.service.test.ts` PASS (26/26) + related `turn-execution.service.test.ts` + `turn-context-hydration.service.test.ts` PASS; full AGENTS gate (lint × all packages + format:check + typecheck × 4 + repo tests) below. Effective after the next dev runtime image pin (no Prisma changes).

- **Change (ADR-125 follow-up: per-turn `<system-reminder>` plan-lifecycle nudge).** After the Option A pivot landed, the residual gap was the classic one: "model did the work but didn't call `todo_write` to mark it done". Claude-Code / Cursor solve this **not** with an extra LLM round-trip — they inject a short `<system-reminder>` into the same volatile-context tail that already carries the chat-plan and active-scenario blocks (the place where short-term memory used to live before ADR-118 pull-only recall). This commit lands the same pattern: a fourth reminder class in the existing `BuildSystemReminderBlocksService` derived from the windowed chat plan, riding the per-turn pipeline at zero extra LLM cost. Three branches: (a) any `in_progress` row → reminder names that row (id + truncated title), demands `todo_write({action:"complete", id:"<id>"})` BEFORE the assistant text reply, with explicit "do not batch completions"; (b) only `pending` rows → reminder names the first pending row, includes pending count, demands `todo_write({action:"update", id:"<id>", status:"in_progress"})` BEFORE substantive work, with explicit one-in_progress-per-parent reminder; (c) every windowed row already `completed`, or no plan at all → no reminder (silence on a finished plan, so we don't pollute subsequent turns). Wiring: `buildChatPlanBlock` now returns `{ block, todos } | null` instead of just the block, so the existing chat-plan lookup feeds both the `<persai_chat_plan>` rendering and the reminder derivation from one round-trip; `turn-execution.service.ts` threads `chatPlanTodos: chatPlan?.todos ?? null` into `BuildSystemReminderBlocksService.buildBlocks`. Long titles are truncated to ≤140 chars with an ellipsis. Provider clients already wrap `volatileKind: "system_reminder"` content with `<system-reminder>…</system-reminder>` (existing ADR-119 Slice 5 plumbing) for OpenAI / Anthropic / DeepSeek — no provider-client changes required. Tests: `apps/runtime/test/build-system-reminder-blocks.service.test.ts` extends from 11 → 17 cases — case (8) "stable ordering" upgraded to assert scenario → image → **chat-plan** → budget order; new cases (12) `in_progress` branch pins exact tool-call spelling + recency-bias copy, (13) only-pending branch pins the pending count + first pending row + `todo_write update` shape, (14) all-completed → no reminder, (15) null/undefined/empty todos → no reminder, (16) overlong content truncated to ≤140 chars with "…", (17) chat-plan reminder fires even when no scenario is active. Files: `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/build-system-reminder-blocks.service.ts`, `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/turn-context-hydration.service.ts`, `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/turn-execution.service.ts`, `apps/runtime/test/build-system-reminder-blocks.service.test.ts`. Gate: `@persai/runtime` typecheck PASS · `@persai/api` typecheck PASS · `@persai/web` typecheck PASS · repo lint PASS · format:check PASS · full runtime isolated suite PASS (incl. `runBuildSystemReminderBlocksServiceTest` 17/17, `runChatPlanBlockTest`, `runRuntimeSkillToolServiceTest`, all `TurnExecutionService` scenarios). Effective after the next dev runtime image pin (no Prisma changes).

- **Change (ADR-125 Option A: model-authored scenario intake + plan-card polish).** Live validation showed the model treats scenario_seeded rows in `<persai_chat_plan>` as read-only narration — even with the explicit `SCENARIO_SEEDED LIFECYCLE` clause in `todo_write.modelUsageGuidance` it walks the user through scenario steps without ever calling `todo_write({action:"update", status:"in_progress"})` / `action:"complete"` on the seeded ids. This is the known self-attribution failure mode: assistants reliably progress todos they themselves authored and routinely ignore externally-seeded ones. Founder approved a clean pivot to **Option A** — the server no longer materialises scenario steps as todos; `skill.engage` returns the scenario's steps verbatim and the model is instructed (via the catalog row for `skill`) to call `todo_write({action:"add", items:[...]})` itself as its very next turn. The plan becomes model-authored from move one, which is the regime Claude/Cursor-style agents naturally progress. Three additional UX follow-ups landed in the same slice. **(a) Persistent chat-header subtitle.** The "Маркетолог · Карусель" chip kept disappearing after a few seconds because per-message `engagementSummary` was lost on history reload — fixed by exposing a chat-level `currentEngagement: { skillDisplayName, scenarioDisplayName } | null` on the chat history endpoint (derived server-side from `chat.skillDecisionState` via the existing `deriveEngagementSummary` projection), and rebinding the web header subtitle to that chat-level state instead of walking messages. **(b) Removed redundant per-message engagement chip** from `WorkingTextBlocks` — the chat header subtitle is now the canonical surface. **(c) Plan card polish.** Trash button on a fully-completed plan now deletes immediately on first click (the confirmation prompt was noise for a plan the user already considers closed); desktop banner width tightened to `max-w-[50rem]` to match the chat zone; mobile is flush-to-edges with hairline dividers; desktop carries a quieter `color-mix()` background with no shadow; status icons / typography toned down. **Migration is data-safe:** dropped `AssistantChatTodoOrigin` enum, `origin / seed_skill_id / seed_skill_label / seed_scenario_key / seed_key` columns, and the `assistant_chat_todos_chat_id_seed_key_idx` partial index — previously seeded rows keep their content/status/sort/parent linkage and continue to render as flat plan rows. Runtime contract: dropped `PERSAI_RUNTIME_TODO_WRITE_ORIGINS` / `PersaiRuntimeTodoWriteOrigin` and the `origin`+`seedSkillLabel` fields on `RuntimeTodoItem`. Removed: API `seedSkillScenarioTodos` service method, `/seed-skill-scenario` internal controller endpoint, runtime client method + parser, runtime `seedScenarioTodosAfterEngage` call, hydration `// Rows tagged (seeded by …) …` lifecycle hint + `(seeded by <label>)` suffix in the `<persai_chat_plan>` block, web `chat.planSeededFrom` / `planSeededFromGeneric` i18n keys, all `testSeedSkillScenario*` cases. Files: `packages/runtime-contract/src/index.ts`, `apps/api/prisma/schema.prisma`, `apps/api/prisma/migrations/20260622180000_adr125_drop_scenario_seeding/migration.sql`, `apps/api/prisma/tool-catalog-data.ts`, `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/assistant-chat-todos.service.ts`, `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/interface/http/internal-runtime-chat-todos.controller.ts`, `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/manage-web-chat-list.service.ts`, `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/interface/http/assistant.controller.ts`, `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/runtime-skill-tool.service.ts`, `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/persai-internal-api.client.service.ts`, `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/turn-context-hydration.service.ts`, `apps/web/app/app/_components/chat-plan-card.tsx`, `apps/web/app/app/_components/use-chat.ts`, `apps/web/app/app/_components/chat-area.tsx`, `apps/web/app/app/_components/chat-message.tsx`, `apps/web/app/app/assistant-api-client.ts`, `apps/web/messages/{ru,en}.json`, plus the matching test files. - **Change (web chat-header active-skill subtitle).** Founder feedback after the ADR-125 plan-card redesign: the previously-existing engagement chip ("right of «Выполнено»") that surfaced the active skill / scenario was no longer discoverable, since it only renders inline with each assistant message's collapsed working-notes toggle. Added a persistent, chat-level subtitle under the chat title that surfaces `Скилл · <skillDisplayName> · <scenarioDisplayName?>` when a skill is engaged, and falls back to the existing mode caption ("тщательнее, но дороже" / "глубокий анализ") when no skill is engaged but `chatMode !== "normal"`. The skill chip renders on both desktop and mobile (it is the live working context); the mode caption stays desktop-only so the plain non-normal mobile chat header doesn't grow. When both signals are active, the mode icon (`Sparkles` / `FolderKanban`) is preserved next to the skill chip on desktop so the premium signal isn't lost. Source of truth: the chat-level `engagementSummary` on the latest **committed** assistant message — the API already populates that from `chat.skillDecisionState`, so the chip clears the moment the model lands a release-turn (no streaming flicker because we walk only committed messages). Truncation: `truncate max-w-[10rem] md:max-w-[22rem]` so the scenario half shrinks first under narrow widths; the full untruncated text lives on `title` for hover. New i18n key `chat.activeSkillPrefix` ("Скилл" / "Skill"). - **Fix (ADR-125 follow-up: model wasn't progressing seeded scenario steps + web card surfacing "+N more hidden" after all rows completed).** Two live regressions surfaced during ADR-125 validation and were folded into one slice. (1) The model treated `(seeded by …)` rows as read-only narration — it walked the scenario steps in chat but never called `todo_write({action:"update", status:"in_progress"})` or `action:"complete"` on the seeded ids. Cause: `todo_write.modelUsageGuidance` had no SCENARIO_SEEDED LIFECYCLE clause, and the `<persai_chat_plan>` body had no in-block hint either, so the model effectively had no instruction telling it those rows are mutable and that it owns their lifecycle. Fix: added an explicit `SCENARIO_SEEDED LIFECYCLE:` section to `todo_write.modelUsageGuidance` that names the seeded rows as model-owned, mandates `update status:"in_progress"` before substantive work and `complete` before moving on, repeats the one-`in_progress`-per-parent rule, and points the model at the `— by id <id>` tail of each `<persai_chat_plan>` row as the canonical id source; and added a one-line `// Rows tagged (seeded by …)…` lead inside the `<persai_chat_plan>` body, emitted only when at least one `scenario_seeded` row is still non-completed (suppressed entirely when none are seeded or every seeded row is already done, so we don't pollute finished plans). (2) The web `GET …/plan` endpoint was reusing `selectChatPlanWindow` — the model-prompt window that caps completed rows at "last 2 by `completedAt`" so the cached `<persai_chat_plan>` block stays cheap — which meant the user-facing card was rendering "Plan 2/5 +3 more hidden" with three rows invisibly stashed once the model had completed all of them. Fix: new `readFullPlanForWeb({chatId})` that returns up to `WEB_PLAN_RESPONSE_MAX = 50` rows in raw `sortOrder` with the real `totalCount`, and flags `windowed: true` only when the cap is tripped; the web controller swapped to it, the internal runtime endpoint still uses `readWindow` so the model prompt window stays tight. Tests: `apps/api/test/assistant-chat-todos.service.test.ts` walks a 5-step plan to "all completed" and asserts the model window collapses to 2 rows while `readFullPlanForWeb` returns all 5, plus an overflow case that inserts 60 rows across two `add` calls and asserts `windowed: true` at the 50-row cap; `apps/runtime/test/turn-context-hydration.service.test.ts` covers the lifecycle hint appearing for an open `scenario_seeded` row and being suppressed both when no `scenario_seeded` row is present and when every `scenario_seeded` row is already completed; `apps/api/test/tool-catalog-data.test.ts` pins the `SCENARIO_SEEDED LIFECYCLE` section and the `by id <id>` reference inside `todo_write.modelUsageGuidance`. Files: `apps/api/prisma/tool-catalog-data.ts`, `apps/api/test/tool-catalog-data.test.ts`, `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/turn-context-hydration.service.ts`, `apps/runtime/test/turn-context-hydration.service.test.ts`, `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/assistant-chat-todos.service.ts`, `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/interface/http/assistant-chat-todos.controller.ts`, `apps/api/test/assistant-chat-todos.service.test.ts`. Gate: focused chat-todos + tool-catalog + runtime turn-context-hydration tests PASS; web focused suites (chat-plan-card, use-chat, assistant-api-client) 171/171 PASS; api/web/runtime typecheck PASS; full repo lint PASS; format:check PASS. Effective after the next dev api+web image pin (no Prisma changes).

- **Change (ADR-125 plan card redesign: sticky-top, collapsed-by-default, current-task preview).** Founder review of the live card landed three asks: pin to the top of the chat zone, lighter / more premium surface, and stop always rendering the full list — collapsed by default with the active task shown as a one-line preview, following Cursor / Linear practice. `<ChatPlanCard>` moved from above the composer to inside the chat scroll container as a `sticky top-2 z-20` overlay centred under the existing `max-w-3xl` column, so it stays visible while the user scrolls. Surface upgraded to `rounded-xl` + `border-border/40` + `bg-bg/85` with `backdrop-blur-xl backdrop-saturate-150` (and a `supports-[backdrop-filter]:bg-bg/70` fallback) plus a layered soft shadow. Header reordered: status icon (green check / spinner / muted circle depending on plan state) → "План" bold → pill `done / total` (tabular nums) → optional `+N more` → "·" → current-task preview (truncated). Current task = first `in_progress`, else first `pending`, else the new `planAllDone` indicator. Body now conditionally renders only when expanded — chevron rotates 180° on expand for the visual cue without DOM bloat. New i18n key `chat.planAllDone` ("Все задачи выполнены" / "All tasks completed"). Tests updated: legacy "defaults to expanded" replaced by three collapsed-by-default cases (in_progress preview, pending fallback, all-done indicator); body-content tests now `expand(container)` before asserting against `#chat-plan-body`; toggle test asserts the body element actually disappears on collapse. - **Fix (ADR-125 live regression: `<ChatPlanCard>` invisible after deploy).** Live `persai-dev` showed the model successfully calling `todo_write` and 7 rows landing in `assistant_chat_todos` for the active web chat, but the inline plan card never appeared and every `GET /api/v1/assistant/chats/web/:chatId/plan` returned `401` in ~1 ms with `userId: null` in the access log. Root cause: the two new web-facing routes (`GET` + `DELETE …/plan`) on `AssistantChatTodosController` were registered via `WorkspaceManagementModule` but were missing from the `ClerkAuthMiddleware.forRoutes(...)` allowlist in `IdentityAccessModule`, so requests reached the controller with `req.resolvedAppUser === undefined` and the handler rejected them — the BFF proxied that 401 back to the SPA, the silent `catch` in `useChat.refreshChatPlan` swallowed it, and `chat.chatPlan` stayed empty (the card returns `null` when empty). Same regression class as ADR-074 / ADR-076 / ADR-088 / ADR-115 / ADR-118 Slice 3 / ADR-076 avatar follow-up — the existing module test already pins those, so a matching assertion now pins ADR-125. Files: `apps/api/src/modules/identity-access/identity-access.module.ts`, `apps/api/test/identity-access.module.test.ts`. Gate: API focused module test PASS; `@persai/api` typecheck PASS; full repo lint PASS; format:check PASS. Effective after the next dev image pin.

- **ADR-125 implemented locally (in-chat TodoWrite + scenario-seeded plan):** new model-owned, zero-provider-cost native PersAI tool `todo_write` plus a Cursor-style inline plan card in the web chat. **(1) Backend foundation.** New Prisma model `AssistantChatTodo` + enums `AssistantChatTodoStatus` / `AssistantChatTodoOrigin` (additive migration `20260622130000_adr125_assistant_chat_todos`), hierarchical (`parentId`), three statuses (`pending` / `in_progress` / `completed`), two origins (`model_authored` / `scenario_seeded`), `seedScenarioKey` / `seedSkillId` / `seedSkillLabel` / `seedKey` columns + a reserved `completionCriteria JSONB NULL`; indexes on `(chatId, sortOrder)`, `(chatId, parentId, sortOrder)`, `parentId`, and a non-unique `(chatId, seedKey)` index for skill-engage idempotency lookups. New `AssistantChatTodosService` enforcing invariants: one `in_progress` per parent, valid transitions only (no resurrection of `completed`), parent cannot complete with open children, parentage cycle detection, content length cap + normalization, soft ~200 active / hard 500 cap. New runtime contract types `RuntimeTodoItem` / `RuntimeTodoWriteToolResult` and constants `PERSAI_RUNTIME_TODO_WRITE_ACTIONS|_STATUSES|_ORIGINS`, `RUNTIME_CHAT_PLAN_WINDOW_MAX = 12`. New native tool projection `createTodoWriteToolDefinition`; runtime dispatcher case + `RuntimeTodoWriteToolService` (inline execution, mirrors `runtime-memory-write-tool.service.ts`). New `<persai_chat_plan>` reinjection block in `turn-context-hydration.service.ts` (`cacheRole: volatile_context`, `volatileKind: chat_plan`) wrapped by every provider client. New internal-runtime + user-facing controllers (`POST /v1/internal/runtime/chat-todos/{apply,window,seed-skill-scenario}`, `GET`/`DELETE /v1/assistant/chats/web/:chatId/plan`). Catalog row + Starter Trial policy (`active:true`, both limits `null`); `runtime-tool-policy.ts` execution mode `inline`. **(2) Skill engage seeding (Path C).** After a successful `skill({action:"engage", scenarioKey})`, the runtime calls `seedSkillScenarioTodos` to materialize scenario steps as `origin: scenario_seeded` todos under the deepest current `in_progress` parent (top-level if none). Idempotent per `(chatId, seedKey)` — one batch shares one `seedKey`, existence check + inserts run in one Prisma transaction; failures are warn-logged and never fail engage. **(3) Web UI.** New `<ChatPlanCard>` rendered inline above the composer (Cursor-style collapsible card) with status icons (pending circle / in-progress spinner / completed strike-through), parent/child indenting, `from <skill>` pill for seeded items, `done / total` counts, optional `+N more` tail when windowed, inline clear-confirm row. `useChat` integration refetches the plan on chat load, on terminal turn completion/interruption/failure, on `todo_write` SSE tool events, and on soft-detach reconcile / focus-resume paths. New API client helpers `getAssistantWebChatPlan` / `clearAssistantWebChatPlan`. Lifecycle labels `todo_write_started/finished/failed` wired through `ACTIVITY_LABEL_KEYS`. New ru/en `chat.plan*` keys + `activityTodoWrite*` keys. **(4) Admin / catalog regression.** Backend canonical `PROMPT_CONSTRUCTOR_MODEL_TOOL_ORDER` and the web `/admin/presets` mirror both include `todo_write` between `memory_write` and `quota_status`. `/admin/plans` toggle appears via the existing plan-managed backfill; new `TOOL_CARD_DESCRIPTION.todo_write` blurb. New focused regression test `apps/api/test/tool-catalog-data.test.ts` locks the catalog row (`displayName: "Todo Write"`, `policyClass: "plan_managed"`, `toolClass: "utility"`, `capabilityGroup: "workspace_ops"`, non-empty `description` / `modelDescription` / `modelUsageGuidance`) plus the Starter Trial activation shape. **Intentionally out of scope (see ADR-125 § Scope fence):** cross-chat continuity, completion-criteria proof contracts (column reserved, unused in v1), runtime stream resilience, background-task ↔ todo unification, `cancelled` status, user-side todo editing in UI (clear-all only on v1), live two-way binding between scenario state and todos, `<tool_usage_policy>` template additions (the model already discovers `todo_write` via native projection, so the selection guide and the byte-golden fixture do not change). Gate: lint · format:check · `@persai/api`/`@persai/web`/`@persai/runtime`/`@persai/provider-gateway` typecheck · API/runtime/web focused tests (incl. all new and extended suites) PASS. **Effective after the next dev deploy.** The migration pauses on the `persai-dev-migrations` GitHub Environment per CI policy.

- **ADR-123 + ADR-124 closed by founder (doc-only slice).** Both orchestration programs moved to the closed-program archive in `AGENTS.md`; do not reopen for new scope. **ADR-123** (native sandbox runtime — isolation, lifecycle, network, secrets, in-sandbox document execution): live verified — sandbox Deployment runs the post-Slice-7 image (`sandbox:31607214…`); `command -v rg` → `/usr/bin/rg` and `command -v fd` → `/usr/local/bin/fd` inside the running pod (the Slice 7 deploy residual). gVisor isolation, secret-free execution unit, deny-all egress + allowlist proxy, per-`(assistantId,workspaceId)` warm exec pod, `sandbox-pool` min-nodes=1 + prepull DaemonSet, 15-min idle TTL, expanded doc/data/image baseline image, WeasyPrint PDF cutover, mode-B data documents (`xlsx`/`docx`), and `grep`/`glob`/`shell` are all operating against real assistant traffic; no transitional flags or compatibility shims remain in the active code path. **ADR-124** (provider-agnostic model routing, prompt-cache-retention capability, structured-output schema sanitation, fallback semantics, DeepSeek onboarding): live verified — DeepSeek main-reply turns complete; tool-loop turns no longer disconnect (`reasoning_content` echoed back; `parallel_tool_calls: false` keeps one tool call per assistant turn); runtime gateway-result validator accepts `deepseek` alongside `openai`/`anthropic`; image/PDF attachments on a DeepSeek main slot are described via the plan's `systemTool` vision slot; admin guard prevents picking a text-only provider for `systemTool`; Anthropic numeric-range schema 400s gone; `gpt-5.5` works when `promptCacheRetention = "24h"`; cross-provider fallback on satisfiable 4xx (balance/quota/capacity/auth) runs before the first token only.
