- **ADR-121 opened (two-dimensional execution routing — task `level` separated from `(model, thinking budget)`):** new open program ADR `docs/ADR/121-two-dimensional-execution-routing-model-and-thinking-budget.md` (Accepted — founder go). Post-119 audit found the router output `executionMode: normal|premium|reasoning` conflates "how heavy is the task" with "which model + how much thinking" — the root cause of two production hardcodes: `project-execution-profile.ts:72` forces `reasoning` for every project turn, and `turn-routing.service.ts` hard-caps `deepMode` ("smarter") at `premium` (seven `deepMode ? "premium" : "normal"` ternaries + `coerceExecutionMode`), so thinking budget is never set and "smarter" never reaches a reasoning model. Decision: the router emits a single semantic `level` (`light|medium|heavy|deep`); one pure resolver maps `level → ExecutionProfile { modelRole, thinkingBudget }` (medium and heavy share the premium slot, differ only by ~8k thinking — the reason a second axis is required); `executionMode` is retained as a derived model-slot token (downstream model resolution unchanged, minimal blast radius); new `thinkingBudget` field plumbed contract → provider-gateway (Anthropic `thinking.budget_tokens` / OpenAI `reasoning_effort`); both hardcodes removed (`project` → `heavy` signal, `deepMode` → +1-level nudge); signals enriched (length, attachments, active Skill, chatMode, keyword cues, KB availability); per-plan thinking budgets in admin. Five slices (contract+resolver+plan config → router rewrite → provider plumbing → admin UI → tests). No infra. Out of scope (separate ADRs): memory JIT redesign, scenario step progression, RAG unification (ADR-120, not yet authored), sandbox/shell model. Decided at acceptance: code/reasoning-term turns default to `heavy`, `deep` only with an explicit depth signal. Authored only; no routing code changed yet.

- **ADR-119 program closed (founder acceptance):** ADR-119 status updated to `Closed — 2026-06-19 (founder acceptance; program complete)`. § Founder acceptance closure documents live validation on `persai-dev`: cache/payload assembly **PASS**; scenario gate (c) **PARTIAL** (engage/release + volatile `<persai_active_scenario>` rails OK; step-by-step adherence and `activeStepNumber` deferred). Explicit non-reopen policy — scenario step progression and remaining live matrix gates (a)(b)(d)(e) belong in a **new founder ADR**, not ADR-119 slices. `AGENTS.md` updated: ADR-118 + ADR-119 in closed archive; no open orchestration program ADR. Local evidence: `tmp/adr-119-slice-1-validation/scenario-live-gate-report.md`.

- **ADR-119 polish — Anthropic sliding history cache marker (#2 of 2) fixed + "legacy" wording removed:** Anthropic sliding history cache marker (#2 of 2): fixed formula so the marker actually fires at 3k-token boundaries; previous version required 6k+ before firing and effectively disabled history caching in production. Tool-loop turns intentionally skip the marker — transient `tool_result` data is not cached. Also removed "legacy" wording from the single-block system-prompt path (Slice 2 multi-block rejected on review). Details:
  - **Formula (`applyAnthropicMovingHistoryBreakpoint` in `apps/provider-gateway/src/modules/providers/anthropic/anthropic-provider.client.ts`):** changed `maxCachedPrefixBytes = floor((total - minTail) / minTail) * minTail` (with `< minTail` gate) → `floor(total / minTail) * minTail` (with `<= 0` gate). The old "tail buffer" subtraction required ≈2× the chunk (~6k tokens) of stable history before the marker would fire at all, so ordinary PersAI dialogs never reached it and re-paid full `inputTokens` for the whole growing history every turn. The dynamic tail (`volatile_context` + current question) is already spliced in _after_ this marker by `buildAnthropicMessages`, so no extra buffer is needed; the marker now fires as soon as one full chunk of stable history exists, stays put while history grows inside a chunk (cache hot), and advances forward across each chunk boundary (Anthropic READs the cached older prefix instead of re-WRITEing it). Method JSDoc rewritten to document the window and why the tail buffer was wrong. Byte-based measurement (UTF-8 bytes, 3 bytes/token via `APPROX_ANTHROPIC_BYTES_PER_TOKEN`) folded in from the prior session so the threshold fires correctly for Cyrillic/mixed content. The `shouldApplyAnthropicMovingHistoryBreakpoint` gate (`main_turn` only) is unchanged — `tool_loop_followup` turns intentionally never place the marker because transient `tool_result` data will not survive into long-term history. Volatile blocks (`<persai_memory>`, active scenario, `<system-reminder>`) are physically extracted before the marker and spliced back after it, so the cached prefix is the stable history fact only.
  - **"legacy" cleanup + dead multi-block removal (Step 0):** Slice 2 multi-block system path (extra per-zone cache markers #3/#4 via `systemPromptBlocks`) is **rejected on review, not deferred** — the single-block system marker already caches `tools` + the whole `system` zone (Anthropic order `tools → system → messages`), and multi-block only helps under independent per-zone invalidation, which PersAI never does (zones change together on publish). The dormant field/branches were removed (no-dead-stubs): deleted `ProviderGatewayTextGenerateRequest.systemPromptBlocks` from `packages/runtime-contract`, the multi-block branch + `ANTHROPIC_MAX_SYSTEM_CACHE_MARKERS` from `buildAnthropicSystemBlocks`, the never-populated per-block branch from OpenAI `buildOpenAISystemDeveloperItems`, and the related provider-client test cases. Renamed all "legacy" comments/JSDoc in the active single-block system-prompt path and the `turn-execution.service.ts` `buildProviderRequest` comment. `rg "systemPromptBlocks" --type ts` returns only a single explanatory JSDoc reference in the Anthropic client.
  - **Tests:** `apps/provider-gateway/test/anthropic-provider.client.test.ts` — bucketed moving-history suite recomputed under the new formula (stable within a chunk; advances on chunk-boundary crossing; marker lands on the latest eligible assistant message); new "first firing at exactly one chunk" + "just below one chunk does not fire" edge cases; existing `toolHistoryBreakpointRequest`, `shortToolHistoryRequest`, and `tool_loop_followup` coverage preserved. OpenAI test swaps the removed `systemPromptBlocks` cases for single-`systemPrompt` developer-item coverage (`instructions` field stays absent).
  - **Gate green:** `corepack pnpm -r --if-present run lint` PASS · `corepack pnpm run format:check` PASS · `@persai/api` typecheck PASS · `@persai/web` typecheck PASS · `@persai/provider-gateway` test PASS (exit 0, full suite incl. Anthropic). `@persai/runtime` + `@persai/provider-gateway` typecheck also PASS.
  - **Cache prefix impact:** none on system-prefix bytes — change is per-turn marker placement inside `messages[]` plus dead-field removal. Anthropic target config is now **2/4 markers used** (system prefix + sliding history); markers #3/#4 (multi-block) intentionally unused.

## 2026-06-18

- **ADR-119 follow-up — Anthropic moving-history-breakpoint fix for tool-loop conversations:** Founder live-test observation: per-turn `inputTokens` kept climbing past the 3k `anthropicHistoryBreakpointMinTokens` threshold on tool-heavy chats — the moving history `cache_control` marker was never being placed. Root-cause audit of `apps/provider-gateway/src/modules/providers/anthropic/anthropic-provider.client.ts`: (1) `applyAnthropicMovingHistoryBreakpoint` only accepted assistant messages whose content was a **single text block** as breakpoint candidates (via the now-deleted `resolveAnthropicHistoryBreakpointText` returning `null` for any non-`text` block), so every assistant turn emitted from `toolHistory` (pure `tool_use` content) was silently skipped — i.e. in real production conversations where the model has called any tool, the breakpoint never fires; (2) the candidate's content was **destructively replaced** with a single text block, which would have corrupted multi-block messages; (3) `measureAnthropicTextTailChars` counted only `text` blocks, under-estimating the message's true byte length and skewing the chunked-cache math toward "not enough yet" on tool-loop turns; (4) `countAnthropicCacheBreakpoints` only counted `cache_control` markers in `system` and `tools`, so even when the breakpoint did fire there was no log visibility into it. **Fix:** `AnthropicBuiltMessageContent` type extended to allow `cache_control` on `image`, `document`, `tool_use`, and `tool_result` blocks in addition to `text`. `applyAnthropicMovingHistoryBreakpoint` rewritten — accepts **any** assistant message as a candidate, walks chunked-cache math using the new `measureAnthropicMessageContentChars`, and delegates marker placement to a new `attachCacheControlToLastBlock` helper that **non-destructively** clones the message and attaches `cache_control` to the last cache-control-capable block (text/image/document/tool_use/tool_result). `measureAnthropicMessageContentChars` (renamed from `measureAnthropicTextTailChars`) counts `text` text length, `tool_use` `JSON.stringify(input).length`, and `tool_result` string-content length — image/document base64 counted as zero (not part of the textual cache key). `countAnthropicCacheBreakpoints` extended to also walk `payload.messages` so log lines surface message-level markers. **Tests:** existing breakpoint suite passes unchanged; new `toolHistoryBreakpointRequest` case asserts (a) the pure-`tool_use` assistant message emitted from `toolHistory` is byte-preserved and (b) `cache_control` is correctly attached to the last `tool_use` block; new `shortToolHistoryRequest` case asserts chunked math still gates correctly (no marker on tiny histories). **Gate green:** provider-gateway lint PASS, full provider-gateway vitest suite PASS, format:check PASS, api/web/runtime/provider-gateway typecheck PASS. **Cache prefix:** no change to system-prefix bytes — fix purely affects per-turn breakpoint placement inside `messages[]`.

- **ADR-119 cleanup slice (template + tool descriptor normalization + legacy fallback canonicalization):** post-live-test cleanup of structural inconsistencies the founder flagged: (1) markdown headings (`# X`, `## X`) still surfaced inside XML-wrapped templates; (2) four templates were never wrapped (`router_classifier`, `skill_state_classifier`, `preview_bootstrap`, `welcome_bootstrap`); (3) only 8/20 catalog tools and 3/5 synthetic tools followed the WHEN/NOT/EXAMPLES/GOTCHAS ACI shape; (4) `compile-prompt-constructor.service.ts` legacy fallbacks still produced `# Identity` / `# User Context` / `# Character Preview` / `# First Conversation` markdown when a template was null; (5) `renderTraitsBlock` emitted `## Personality Traits` markdown heading inside the `<voice>` block.
  - **Templates (`apps/api/prisma/bootstrap-preset-data.ts`):** all 7 visible XML-wrapped templates (`soul`, `user`, `identity`, `memory_protocol`, `tools`, `heartbeat`, `presence`) had their markdown `# H1`/`## H2` headings replaced with nested canonical XML elements (`<core_persona>`, `<style>`, `<openings>`, `<emotion_response>`, `<silence>`, `<examples>`, `<sense_of_time>`, `<usage>`). Numbered priority list inside `<tool_usage_policy>` (1. 2. 3. …) lifted from Markdown `N.` to canonical XML `<rule order="N">…</rule>`. List labels normalized from `- **Name**: value` to `- Name: value` (bold inline emphasis stripped from list-item labels; bold-emphasis kept where it carries true emphasis like `**${assistantName}**`). 4 previously-unwrapped templates wrapped: `router_classifier` → `<router_classifier>` (with `<modes>`, `<retrieval_plan>`, `<tool_hints>`); `skill_state_classifier` → `<skill_state_classifier>` (with `<rules>`); `preview_bootstrap` → `<character_preview>` (with `<task>`, `<constraints>`); `welcome_bootstrap` → `<first_conversation_greeting>` (with `<task>`, `<opening_requirements>`, `<middle_section>`, `<closing_requirements>`, `<formatting_constraints>`). Provenance documentation added inside `<memory_protocol><read>` enumerating all four enum values (`user_explicit`, `system_inferred`, `auto_extracted`, `legacy`) and how the model should treat each.
  - **Tool descriptors (`apps/api/prisma/tool-catalog-data.ts` + `runtime-tool-policy.ts files-override` + `bootstrap-preset-data.ts hidden synthetics`):** every model-visible tool now carries the canonical 4-section ACI shape. Catalog: 10 new conversions — `video_generate`, `document`, `tts`, `browser`, `scheduled_action`, `background_task`, `persai_tool_quota_status`, `files` (also synced into the runtime override), `exec`, `shell`. Synthetics: 3 new conversions — `summarize_context`, `compact_context`, `quota_status`. Hidden-internal entries (`cron`, `persai_workspace_attach`) keep their one-liner shape deliberately (not model-visible).
  - **Legacy fallback canonicalization (`apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/compile-prompt-constructor.service.ts`):** the legacy markdown-heading fallback paths in `generateSoulPrompt`, `generateUserPrompt`, `generateIdentityPrompt`, `generatePreviewPrompt`, `generateWelcomePrompt` were rewritten to emit canonical XML (`<voice>` + `<character_notes>`, `<user>`, `<identity>`, `<character_preview>`, `<first_conversation_greeting>`) so any code path that runs with `template === null` no longer regresses to markdown headings. `renderTraitsBlock` rewritten from `## Personality Traits` heading + `- **trait**: N/100` bullets to canonical `<personality_traits>` XML with plain `- trait: N/100` bullets. `interpolateTemplate` callers now feed `- Name: value` line builders to `*_line` placeholders, matching the bold-free style of the new template defaults.
  - **Tests:** `bootstrap-preset-data.test.ts` — `SKIPPED_TEMPLATE_KEYS` emptied (all templates now pass XML-balance check); `EXPECTED_OUTER_TAGS` extended with `router_classifier`, `skill_state_classifier`, `preview_bootstrap`, `welcome_bootstrap`; new `runNoMarkdownHeadings` invariant test scans every template (with `stripCodeAndPlaceholders` applied) and asserts no `^#{1,6}\s` markdown headings remain inside any XML tag. `seed-tool-catalog.test.ts` — Slice 7 8-tool ACI check generalized to "every model-visible catalog entry must carry the 4-section ACI shape" (only `cron` and `persai_workspace_attach` excluded); ALLOW_LIST expanded with the new legitimate cross-references (`browser ↔ web_search/web_fetch`; `video_generate → image_generate/image_edit/tts`; `document → files`; `scheduled_action ↔ background_task`; `persai_tool_quota_status → knowledge_search/document`; `files → exec/shell/document`; `exec → shell/files/document`; `shell → files/exec/document`). `runtime-tool-policy.test.ts` `files` override assertions updated for the canonical 4-section shape. Golden snapshot `apps/api/test/fixtures/adr119-golden-prompt-snapshot.expected.txt` deleted and regenerated against the new prompt bytes (11346 bytes vs prior 11007).
  - **Migration:** templates ship as defaults but existing assistants carry their own snapshot copies in DB. Founder will `Reset to default` per template after deploy. Reset checklist provided in handoff: 11 visible+hidden templates (`system`, `soul`, `user`, `identity`, `memory_protocol`, `tools`, `heartbeat`, `presence`, `router_classifier`, `skill_state_classifier`, `preview_bootstrap`, `welcome_bootstrap`) plus seed of `tool-catalog-data.ts` (auto-applied on next API pod startup via existing `SeedToolCatalogService`). - **ADR-119 follow-up — Anthropic gateway terminal usage metadata + wired `dumpResponse` (live-test blocker fix):** Live-test runner subagent reported P0 blocker — `provider_payload_response_dump` events were never being emitted despite `PERSAI_DEBUG_PROVIDER_PAYLOAD=true` (Slice 0.5 defined `ProviderDebugPayloadLogger.dumpResponse()` but no call site ever invoked it in any provider client), so cache-hit/miss metrics (`cache_creation_input_tokens`, `cache_read_input_tokens`) could not be read from cluster logs. Fixed in `apps/provider-gateway/src/modules/providers/anthropic/anthropic-provider.client.ts`: (1) new always-on `[anthropic-non-stream-end]` and `[anthropic-stream-end]` info-level metadata lines emit per turn at the same single-line printf format as the existing `[*-start]` lines, surfacing `requestId`, `classification`, `iteration`, `model`, `stopReason`, `toolCalls`, `inputTokens`, `cacheCreationInputTokens`, `cacheReadInputTokens`, `outputTokens`, `totalTokens` (with `null` literal when a field is unset) — readable from `kubectl logs` without enabling the debug toggle; (2) `debugPayloadLogger.dumpResponse(...)` is now actually called from both transports (non-stream after `finalMessage()`, stream at `message_stop` for both `tool_calls` and `completed` paths) carrying the final `stop_reason` + `usage` snapshot + tool call count + text. No user content is ever logged on the always-on line. Tests (`apps/provider-gateway/test/anthropic-provider.client.test.ts`): generate-path asserts a `[anthropic-non-stream-end]` line with the full printf grammar; stream-path asserts a `[anthropic-stream-end]` line and the exact `cacheCreationInputTokens=4`, `cacheReadInputTokens=6`, `inputTokens=10`, `outputTokens=5`, `totalTokens=25` figures from the existing stream-cache fixture. ## 2026-06-17

- **ADR-119 Slice 4 landed (volatile active-scenario XML format + step field extensions):** `BuildActiveScenarioBlockService.renderActiveScenarioBlock` rewritten from Markdown (`## Active Scenario: …`, `Steps:`, `Recommended tool:`, `Guards:`) to canonical XML per ADR-119 D5: inner content starts with `Active: <scenarioDisplayName> (Skill: <skillDisplayName>)` summary line, then `<step number="N">` elements containing `<directive>`, optional `<recommended_tool_call>`, optional `<expected_user_response>`, optional `<next_step_trigger>`, optional `<recovery_guidance>`, optional `<may_be_skipped_if>`, optional `<negative_guards><guard>Do NOT …</guard></negative_guards>`, then `<exit_condition>` at the end. Sub-tags omitted when null/empty for byte stability. Provider wrapper inner tag renamed from `active_scenario` → `persai_active_scenario` in `anthropic-provider.client.ts` (OpenAI already used `persai_active_scenario` since ADR-118 Slice 4). Schema additive — three new optional fields added to `RuntimeBundleSkillScenarioStep` in `packages/runtime-contract`: `expectedUserResponse?`, `nextStepTrigger?`, `recoveryGuidance?` (all `string | null`). Mirrored in `SkillScenarioStepState` (API-side parse type) and `parseStep` (accepts + validates the new fields up to 400 chars each). `normalizeSkillScenarioSteps` in the materializer populates all three with `null` when absent — stable byte order, never `undefined`. `normalizeSkillScenarioSteps` exported for direct unit testing. Tests: `build-active-scenario-block.service.test.ts` fully updated and extended (18 cases — XML tag assertions, new field presence/absence, byte-stability); `anthropic-provider.client.test.ts` updated to assert `<persai_active_scenario>` (NOT `<active_scenario>`); `openai-provider.client.test.ts` negative assertion added; `materialize-assistant-published-version.service.test.ts` extended with 3 normalizer unit tests (field flow-through, missing-fields → null, explicit-null → null). Existing scenarios continue to work — new fields are optional and default to null; Admin UI to expose them deferred to Slice 10.

- **ADR-119 Slice 3 landed (Skills progressive disclosure + `first_step_preview`) — batched with Slices 1+2 in same persai-dev deploy:** Each enabled Skill in the cache prefix is now a compact XML card (`<skill id="..." key="...">`) instead of a Markdown block with full `body`/`guardrails`/`examples`. The long instruction payload (~1,200 chars `body` + guardrails + examples per Skill) is removed from the cache prefix and delivered by the runtime only when the model calls `skill({action:"engage"})` — field name `instruction: {body, guardrails, examples}` in the engage response (Part B). The new `<first_step_preview>` scenario field (≤200-char excerpt of `steps[0].directive`, stripped to a single line) is emitted inside each `<scenario key="...">` entry so the model sees step 1 guidance **before** calling `skill({engage})`, fixing [F3] parallel-tool-call pre-emption. XML card format per ADR-119 D4: `<display_name>`, `<summary>`, `<when_to_use>` (new optional InstructionCard field), `<category>`, `<tags>`, `<available_scenarios>` with per-scenario `<name>`, `<one_line>`, `<first_step_preview>` (omitted when no steps), `<recommended_tools>` (omitted when empty). Expected prefix shrink: ~60-80% per Skill (3 Skills × ~1,500 chars ≈ ~4,500 chars / ~1,100 tokens per request, back-of-envelope from ADR D4). **R8 invariant**: body/guardrails/examples are added to `AssistantRuntimeEnabledSkillSummary` in `packages/runtime-bundle` and materialized from the existing `EnabledSkillPromptCard` fields in the same commit — guaranteed to arrive in the engage tool result the moment they leave the prefix. Tests: `enabled-skills-prompt-materialization.test.ts` rewritten for XML assertions (skill tag, key attr, first_step_preview present/absent, R8 sentinel check, byte-stability); `runtime-skill-tool.service.test.ts` extended with instruction payload assertions (engage no-scenario, engage with-scenario, byte-match sentinel). Web admin presets `skill_cards_block` sample updated to new XML format.

- **ADR-119 Slice 2 landed (provider cache_control markers + parallel-tool-calls discipline):** `packages/runtime-contract` `ProviderGatewayTextGenerateRequest` extended with two optional fields — `skillsEnabled?: boolean` (triggers parallel-tool-calls discipline) and `systemPromptBlocks?: Array<{id, text}>` (per-zone cache marker placement, deferred population to follow-up slice). **OpenAI `developer` role migration (R4):** `payload.instructions` removed from both non-streaming and streaming Responses API paths; system prompt (or each named block) is now emitted as `{role:"developer", content:[{type:"input_text", text}]}` items prepended to `input[]` — makes the stable system prefix the OpenAI Responses API cache prefix. **Anthropic per-block cache markers (R6):** `buildAnthropicSystemBlocks` extended — when `systemPromptBlocks` is provided and validates (concatenation equals `systemPrompt`), emits one `TextBlockParam` with `cache_control:{type:"ephemeral"}` per block, capped at 3 system markers (4th breakpoint reserved for moving-history window); excess blocks emitted as plain text with `anthropic_cache_breakpoints_truncated` warn; concatenation mismatch falls back to single-block with `anthropic_system_blocks_mismatch` warn, no throw. **Parallel-tool-calls discipline (R5):** Anthropic `toAnthropicToolChoice` returns `{type:"auto", disable_parallel_tool_use:true}` when `skillsEnabled===true && tools present`; OpenAI sets `parallel_tool_calls: skillsEnabled===true ? false : true`. **Runtime wiring:** `buildProviderRequest` in `turn-execution.service.ts` passes `skillsEnabled: bundle.skills?.enabled.length > 0`; `systemPromptBlocks` deferred — providers fall back to single-block until a follow-up micro-slice exposes compiler block offsets. **Deviation from spec:** `cacheBreakpoints: number[]` (byte-offset array) replaced by `systemPromptBlocks: Array<{id,text}>` (named-block array) because byte-offsets are fragile under string handling. Tests: `anthropic-provider.client.test.ts` and `openai-provider.client.test.ts` each extended with Slice 2 coverage (disable_parallel_tool_use branches both ways, systemPromptBlocks 3-block / 4-block / mismatch cases, OpenAI `instructions`-absent assertion). **Deploy note:** BATCH Slice 1 + Slice 2 + Slice 3 in the same persai-dev deploy per ADR-119.

- **ADR-119 Slice 1 landed (XML compile output + persona deduplication) — one-time prompt-cache prefix invalidation on rollout:** all eight visible prompt templates in `bootstrap-preset-data.ts` are now wrapped with their canonical ADR-119 outer XML tags (`<voice>` + `<character_notes>` for `soul`; `<user>`, `<identity>`, `<enabled_skills>`, `<tool_usage_policy>`, `<memory_protocol>`, `<background_task_evaluation>`, `<persai_environment>`); the `system` template's "# Response UI Contract" section is wrapped in `<response_contract>`. The `soul` template splits into two adjacent blocks: `<voice>` holds archetype-driven content and `<character_notes>` holds `{{instructions_block}}` (`snapshotInstructions`) — this is the [F1] persona dedup fix; `snapshotInstructions` is now rendered exactly once across the materialized system prompt. `compile-prompt-constructor.service.ts` drops the duplicate `{{persona_instructions_block}}` path (resolves to `null` so legacy custom templates simply drop the line), adds `stripEmptyCharacterNotes` to collapse the empty shell on persona-less assistants, and emits `compileMode: "xml_canonical_v1"` on every new materialization. `packages/runtime-bundle/src/index.ts` gains the `AssistantRuntimePromptCompileMode` type and the optional `compileMode` field on `AssistantRuntimePromptConstructor.ordinary`; the legacy fallback synthesizer emits `"legacy_markdown"`. New tests: `apps/api/test/bootstrap-preset-data.test.ts` — XML balance validator (stack-based, strips fenced code + backticks + placeholders before parsing) + outer-tag presence + `<character_notes>`/`{{instructions_block}}` placement assertions; `apps/api/test/compile-prompt-constructor.service.test.ts` — three fixture snapshots (archetype-only, free-form-only, archetype+instructions) each asserting `compileMode`, `<voice>` count, `<character_notes>` count, single-occurrence of `snapshotInstructions`, and `<voice>`/`<character_notes>` adjacency. ADR-117 golden test updated for `<tool_usage_policy>` and `<memory_protocol>` outer tags (inner heading assertions preserved). **One-time prompt-cache prefix invalidation on rollout** — the XML tag bytes added to every cached template change the stable prefix; `configDirtyAt` cleared implicitly on next materialization.

- **ADR-119 Slice 0.5 landed (Anthropic gateway observability + symmetric debug payload dump):** `apps/provider-gateway` now emits always-on INFO metadata lines before both Anthropic text transports: `[anthropic-non-stream-start]` for caller-facing `generateText()` (even though it uses `messages.stream(...).finalMessage()` internally) and `[anthropic-stream-start]` for `streamText()`, with request id, classification, tool-loop iteration, model, system block count, cache breakpoint count, message count, tool count, and tool-history count derived from the assembled provider payload. A new shared `ProviderDebugPayloadLogger` adds env-flag-gated request body dumps for Anthropic and OpenAI on the dedicated `persai.debug.provider` logger; `PERSAI_DEBUG_PROVIDER_PAYLOAD` must be exactly `true`, `PERSAI_DEBUG_PROVIDER_PAYLOAD_RATE` defaults to `0.05` when enabled and sanitizes invalid/out-of-range values back to `0.05`, and all flags are OFF by default in production. Dumps include bounded system/message/tool previews, 500-char truncation, and base64 redaction markers such as `<redacted:image/png:base64:LENGTH=N>` instead of raw image/document bytes. OpenAI keeps its existing stream metadata and now gets the same gated dump on non-streaming and streaming Responses requests. Operator follow-up documented for Slice 0.5: configure Loki retention for `persai.debug.provider` at 3 days; no infra files changed in this slice.

- **ADR-119 Slice 0 landed (architecture inventory and reachability ledger):** read-only subagent produced `docs/ADR/119-prompt-inventory.md` — 1062-line ledger with 9 sections: 41 prompt-section writer rows (W1-W41 detailed), 15 template constants from `bootstrap-preset-data.ts`, 7 tool-descriptor surfaces, 5 volatile-context kinds traced end-to-end (memory + active_scenario exist today; retrieved_knowledge / environment / system-reminder do NOT exist as `volatileKind`), selection-guide single-seat verification, persona compiler duplication audit (`snapshotInstructions` rendered through both `personaInstructions` AND `instructionsBlock`), 12 future-slice hit lists (Slice 0.5 + Slice 1-11) with files-to-modify/create/delete plus tests, 10 risks R1-R10, and 8 reachability spot-checks with file:line citations. Risks folded back as actionable adjustments for executor subagents: **R1** (active_scenario `volatileKind` already exists since ADR-118 Slice 4 — Slice 4 rewrites format, doesn't introduce kind), **R2** (retrieved knowledge today is developer-tail Markdown via `buildRetrievedKnowledgeContextDeveloperSection` at `turn-execution.service.ts:2023-2027`, not on volatile rail — Slice 4/9 must migrate), **R3** (presence/environment compiled stable but rendered per-turn into developer tail, not via `volatileKind` — Slice 5 migrates, doesn't invent), **R4** (OpenAI today uses `payload.instructions = systemPrompt` at `openai-provider.client.ts:197-199,979-981` instead of `developer` role inside `input[]` — Slice 2 must include this request-shape migration), **R5** (OpenAI explicitly sets `parallel_tool_calls = true` whenever tools exist at `openai-provider.client.ts:203-206,985-988` — Slice 2 needs both enabled/disabled-Skills test cases), **R6** (Anthropic currently emits ONE `cache_control` marker on the whole `systemPrompt` at `anthropic-provider.client.ts:591-604` — Slice 2 needs compiled offset metadata to split into 3 BP boundaries safely), **R7** (`skill_state_classifier` prompt template still seeded at `bootstrap-preset-data.ts:226-240` and materialized into `promptDocuments.skillStateClassifier` despite ADR-118 deleting the caller path — orphan cleanup deferred to ADR-119 closure or separate slice), **R8** (Enabled Skills prefix still renders `card.body` + `guardrails` + `examples` at `enabled-skills-prompt-materialization.ts:128-140` — Slice 3 progressive disclosure must move all three into `skill({engage})` tool response in the same deploy), **R10** (`buildOpenAIInputItems` batches all volatile messages with same wrapper at `openai-provider.client.ts:1390-1393` — provider clients must group/sort volatile messages by `volatileKind` before adding `retrieved_knowledge` / `environment` / `system-reminder` kinds). Orchestrator audit: 8/8 spot-checks verified. Gate: format:check PASS, lint PASS. No code touched; only one new docs file created.

- **HOTFIX — Anthropic provider gateway: non-streaming refused for high `max_tokens` + `maxItems` rejected in structured-output schema:** production fire reported by the founder via Telegram bot — every "Собери pdf" request returned `Запрос принят. Готовлю документ…` then never delivered; subsequent retries returned `Ассистент временно недоступен. Попробуйте ещё раз.`. Cluster log dive on `persai-dev` surfaced TWO independent SDK errors hammering `provider-gateway` every few minutes: (1) `Streaming is required for operations that may take longer than 10 minutes. See https://github.com/anthropics/anthropic-sdk-typescript#long-requests for more details` — thrown synchronously by `@anthropic-ai/sdk@0.87.0` in `Anthropic.calculateNonstreamingTimeout` (client.js:425) when `Messages.create({...max_tokens, stream:false})` projects wall-time > 10 min based on `max_tokens`; (2) `400 invalid_request_error: output_config.format.schema: For 'array' type, property 'maxItems' is not supported` — Anthropic structured-output `output_config.format.schema` does not accept `maxItems` (or `minItems`) on `array` types. Bug 1 killed PDF content generation (`runtime-document-provider-adapter.service.ts` passes up to `DEFENSIVE_OUTPUT_TOKEN_CAP = 64_000` tokens) AND the LLM document failure-framing fallback (so the user got the generic "Ассистент временно недоступен" instead of a real reason). Bug 2 killed `AutoExtractToMemoryService` background memory extraction and `SessionCompactionService` shared compaction continuously (`AUTO_EXTRACT_OUTPUT_SCHEMA.items.maxItems` + `REUSABLE_SHARED_COMPACTION_OUTPUT_SCHEMA.properties[*].maxItems`); also would have killed `generate-skill-authoring-draft.service.ts` if routed to Anthropic. **Fix A (Bug 1):** in `apps/provider-gateway/src/modules/providers/anthropic/anthropic-provider.client.ts`, `generateText()` switched from `this.client.messages.create(payload, { signal })` to `this.client.messages.stream(payload, { signal })` + `await stream.finalMessage()` — same `Message` result shape (`content`/`stop_reason`/`usage`), but the underlying connection is streaming so the SDK skips the 10-min nonstream pre-check. Caller-facing API of `generateText` is unchanged; `streamText` untouched. **Fix B (Bug 2):** added private `sanitizeAnthropicStructuredOutputSchema(value)` that recursively walks the schema and strips `maxItems` and `minItems` keys without mutating the caller's input; `toAnthropicOutputConfig` now sanitizes before sending. Tool definitions (`tools[].input_schema`) untouched — Anthropic accepts `maxItems` there. Caller-side validators in `auto-extract-to-memory.service.ts` and `shared-compaction-state.ts` still enforce caps after the model returns. **Tests:** `apps/provider-gateway/test/anthropic-provider.client.test.ts` restubbed for the new `messages.stream(...).finalMessage()` path + new cases: high `maxOutputTokens=32_000` succeeds (was throwing before); structured schema with `maxItems: 5, minItems: 1` round-trips with both fields stripped and the input schema **not mutated** (asserted); deeply-nested `maxItems` stripped at every level; empty-completion warn (`anthropic_empty_completion`) still triggers under the new code path. `apps/provider-gateway/test/anthropic-empty-completion.test.ts` extended fake client to expose both `stream` and `create` so legacy stream-path tests still pass. Gate green: recursive lint PASS (14 packages) · format:check PASS · provider-gateway typecheck PASS · provider-gateway tests PASS (exit 0; both `anthropic_empty_completion` warns triggered as expected) · api typecheck PASS · web typecheck PASS. **Cache prefix invalidation:** none — provider-gateway internal change only, system-prefix bytes unchanged. **Out-of-scope follow-up (founder owns):** `SANDBOX_RUNNING_JOB_GRACE_MS = 15000` is too aggressive for legitimate workspace-hydrate-heavy `files` jobs (founder said they'll bump in `infra/helm/values-dev.yaml`); secondary sandbox-stale-job warnings observed during the same incident at 23:08:25 and 23:09:25 against `tool=files`.

## 2026-06-16

- **ADR-118 post-deploy hotfix (skill state write-race — tool engage was silently reverted by post-turn turnRouting echo):** model successfully called `skill({action:"engage", skillId, scenarioKey:"instagram_carousel"})` and got back the engaged payload, but on the NEXT turn no `<persai_active_scenario>` developer block appeared because `assistant_chats.skill_decision_state` was back to `{status:"inactive"}`. Root cause: `TurnRoutingService` (post-Slice-6) always echoes back `request.skillStateContext.decision` as `routeDecision.skillState` (no longer derives a new decision — by design), and `AutoSkillRoutingStateService.persistFromTurnRouting` then wrote that stale echo over the **active** state that `RuntimeSkillToolService` had just persisted via `POST /api/v1/internal/runtime/skill/state` inside the same turn. Two writers, last-write-wins, the post-turn write always lost the tool's update. Fix: split the write surface into two methods with explicit roles — (1) `persistFromTurnRouting` is now strictly read-only and returns `readChatSkillState(chatId)` (the freshest DB value, which the tool may have just written); (2) new `persistDecisionState({chatId, nextState})` is the single authoritative writer, performs the row write + retrieval-cache mismatch clear in one logical step. `InternalRuntimeSkillStateService` (the `/internal/runtime/skill/state` handler) switched from `persistFromTurnRouting({turnRouting:{skillState:next}})` to `persistDecisionState({chatId, nextState:next})` for both engage and release. `auto-skill-routing-state.service.test.ts` rewritten: asserts `persistFromTurnRouting` performs zero writes even when `turnRouting.skillState` disagrees with the DB; asserts `persistDecisionState` writes + calls `clearForChatWhenSkillMismatches` with the correct `activeSkillId`; asserts a post-engage `persistFromTurnRouting` echoes back the just-written DB state (not the stale runtime echo). `internal-runtime-skill-state.controller.test.ts` unchanged (stubs the service). Gate green: lint PASS · format:check PASS · api typecheck PASS · web typecheck PASS · `auto-skill-routing-state.service.test.ts` PASS · `internal-runtime-skill-state.controller.test.ts` PASS · `send-web-chat-turn.service.test.ts` PASS (11/11) · `stream-web-chat-turn.service.test.ts` PASS (14/14). Also: 3 marketer SkillScenario rows were seeded directly into `persai-dev` DB (`instagram_carousel`, `content_plan_monthly`, `landing_audit`) for the Маркетолог Skill (`131c1531-5566-4ad2-9422-3b9b76f6d666`) with `configDirtyAt = NOW()` bumped on 2 assigned assistants so the next turn rematerializes the bundle. No new ADR — fix is a direct ADR-118 D1 invariant repair (model owns activation; runtime turn-routing snapshot is not authoritative).

- **ADR-118 post-Slice-7 production hotfix (Skill ID rendering + selection-guide expansion + `routingExamples` Slice-6 residual cleanup + Clerk middleware admin scenarios registration):** Production caught the model passing `skillId: "Диетолог"` (display name) and `skillId: "1"` (random) to `skill({action:"engage", ...})` and getting `skill_not_enabled`. Root cause: `renderSkillCard` in `enabled-skills-prompt-materialization.ts` never rendered `card.id` — the tool description told the model "Must be one of the Skill ids listed in the Enabled Skills block" but the block contained no IDs. **Fix A**: each Skill card now starts with `- Skill ID: ${card.id}` followed by `- Display name: ${card.name}` (renamed from `- Skill: ...` for clarity); the `# Enabled Skills` block intro explicitly says the `Skill ID` field is the EXACT opaque identifier to pass as `skillId`; new regression test asserts `- Skill ID: accounting` etc. **Fix B**: `## Skills` section in `bootstrap-preset-data.ts` selection guide expanded from one prose paragraph to a bullet-list with concrete trigger logic — points the model at the `# Enabled Skills` block as source of truth, forbids substituting display name / category, gives concrete `scenarioKey: "instagram_carousel"` example, and references both engage/release call signatures. The sample preview string in `apps/web/app/admin/presets/page.tsx` (`skill_cards_block`) updated to match the new card format (`- Skill ID: skl_accounting_demo`, `- Display name: Accountant`). ADR-117 golden test (`apps/runtime/test/native-tool-projection.test.ts`) updated: 4 old single-line `**Skills.**` assertions replaced with 7 new assertions verifying `## Skills` heading occurrence (exactly 1), `# Enabled Skills` cross-reference, `Skill ID — exact opaque identifier` phrase, NEVER-substitute clause, engage/release signatures, and concrete scenarioKey example. **Fix C (Slice 6 ledger-gap follow-up)**: `routingExamples?: string[]` field removed from `AssistantRuntimeEnabledSkillSummary` (runtime-bundle) — it was a derived field (`card.examples.slice(0, 2)`) populated in `materialize-assistant-published-version.service.ts` and parsed into the local `EnabledSkillSummary` type in `turn-routing.service.ts`, but never read post-Slice-6 (its only consumer was the deleted `hasSkillLexicalMatch`). Removed from the type, the materialization, the parse in `resolveEnabledSkillSummaries`, and 3 test fixture files (`turn-routing.service.test.ts` 5 occurrences, `turn-execution.service.test.ts` 2 occurrences). Cache prefix bytes change once (deliberate). Grep audit: 0 active-code matches for `routingExamples`. **Fix D (production-blocking, Slice 3 follow-up)**: the 5 new scenario routes added in Slice 3 were never registered with `ClerkAuthMiddleware` in `IdentityAccessModule.configure`, so the API received the request, no middleware populated `req.resolvedAppUser`, and `AdminSkillsController.resolveRequestUserId` threw 401 "Authenticated user context is missing.". Production caught it on the admin Skill detail page → Scenarios section. Added all 5 paths (`GET/POST /api/v1/admin/skills/:skillId/scenarios`, `GET/PATCH/DELETE /api/v1/admin/skills/:skillId/scenarios/:scenarioKey`) to `ClerkAuthMiddleware.forRoutes(...)`. `identity-access.module.test.ts` extended with 5 new `hasRoute` assertions so any future scenario route addition surfaces the guardrail. Gate green: lint PASS; format:check PASS; all 5 typechecks PASS; api test PASS (incl. new Skill ID regression); runtime test PASS (ADR-117 golden test passes with expanded assertions); web test PASS (777/777); provider-gateway test PASS.

- **ADR-118 Slice 6 landed — full dead-code sweep (classifier / cadence / HTTP route / lexical-gate stack):** Two-phase sweep; Slice 0 ledger missed the second batch because the methods were named differently — orchestrator audit caught them and they were deleted in the same slice.

The `selectRecentRoutingRows` private helper deleted. - **ADR-118 Slice 5 landed (admin UI for SkillScenario authoring):** `apps/web/app/admin/skills/page.tsx` extended with an inline "Scenarios" section co-located below the existing Skill editor. When a Skill is selected, the section fetches all scenarios via `getAdminSkillScenarios` (orval-generated client from `packages/contracts`), displays them ordered by `displayOrder` with status badges (draft / active / archived), and provides a toggle to show/hide archived ones. "Создать сценарий" opens an inline collapsible editor with all ADR-118 D3 fields: `key` (slug-validated `^[a-z][a-z0-9_]{1,63}$`, readonly after create), `displayName.ru/en`, `description.ru/en`, `iconEmoji`, `displayOrder`, `status`, `intentExamples` (repeatable list, cap 10), `recommendedTools` (checkboxes for 9 native tool keys hardcoded as `NATIVE_SCENARIO_TOOL_KEYS` — no extractable constant exists in the codebase), `exitCondition`, and a structured `steps` array editor with auto-numbered steps, per-step `directive` (required), `recommendedToolCall` dropdown, `mayBeSkippedIf`, `negativeGuards` (repeatable), up/down reorder buttons, and add/delete step buttons. Inline validation: `key` regex, at least one step, non-empty `directive`, soft yellow warning if last step's directive omits `skill({` or `release`. Per-scenario actions: Edit, Activate (draft→active), Archive (active→archived), Reactivate (archived→active). Two live preview panes updating at 300 ms debounce: Pane A "Catalog rendering" mirrors `enabled-skills-prompt-materialization.ts` format with `ru`/`en` locale toggle; Pane B "Active Scenario developer block" mirrors `BuildActiveScenarioBlockService` output format (formatting duplicated in `renderActiveScenarioBlockPreview` with a comment pointing to the source file). All API calls pass `Authorization: Bearer <token>` directly through the orval client `options`; optimistic state + refetch on success, error display on failure. New pure-helper exports: `SCENARIO_KEY_REGEX`, `NATIVE_SCENARIO_TOOL_KEYS`, `validateScenarioDraft`, `scenarioDraftToCreatePayload`, `scenarioDraftToUpdatePayload`, `scenarioToDraft`, `renderScenarioCatalogLine`, `renderActiveScenarioBlockPreview`. `apps/web/app/admin/skills/page.test.tsx` extended with 10 new test cases covering round-trip `scenarioToDraft`, `scenarioDraftToCreatePayload` payload shape, `validateScenarioDraft` regex rejection, `validateScenarioDraft` empty-steps rejection, `scenarioDraftToUpdatePayload` key omission, `scenarioDraftToUpdatePayload` archived status, `renderActiveScenarioBlockPreview` directive reflection, `renderScenarioCatalogLine` format exactness, soft warning for last step without `skill({`/`release`, and `NATIVE_SCENARIO_TOOL_KEYS` membership. Gate green: lint PASS; format:check PASS; web typecheck PASS; api typecheck PASS; runtime typecheck PASS; api test PASS (exit 0); runtime test PASS (exit 0); web test PASS (772/772 including all 10 new scenario cases). No backend changes. Not committed, not deployed.

- **ADR-118 Slice 4 landed (scenario catalog materialization + active-scenario volatile developer block):** Scenarios for each enabled Skill are now materialized into the runtime bundle and rendered in the cached system-prompt prefix (`Available scenarios:` section per Skill, up to `SCENARIO_CATALOG_RENDER_LIMIT = 8`, with `... +N more` footer for overflow). New types `RuntimeBundleSkillScenarioStep` + `RuntimeBundleSkillScenario` added to `packages/runtime-contract/src/index.ts`; `AssistantRuntimeEnabledSkillSummary` extended with `scenarios?: RuntimeBundleSkillScenario[]` in `packages/runtime-bundle/src/index.ts`. `materialize-assistant-published-version.service.ts` fetches active scenarios from Prisma, converts via locale resolution, attaches to both the prompt cards (cached prefix catalog) and the bundle `skills.enabled[i].scenarios`. ## 2026-06-15

- **HOTFIX — `image_edit` deferred jobs failed 100% on `persai-dev` (ADR-117 cleanup regression from `4a0baa39`):** every deferred `image_edit` (worker path) failed with `invalid_arguments: Unexpected arguments: referenceImageAlias`, then burned ~7.5 min of exponential-backoff retry (30/60/120/240/480s) before surfacing failure to model/user — observed live as 3 consecutive failed turns (2× with 2 input images + 1× with 1 input image) inside one Marketer-themed chat. Root cause: commit `4a0baa39` removed legacy singular `referenceImageAlias` from the parser whitelist (input) but left it as a derived field on the parsed `RuntimeImageEditRequest` (output) and in the contract — the deferred worker rehydrates the persisted parsed request through the same parser, which now rejects its own previous output. End-to-end single-path cleanup landed: removed `referenceImageAlias` / `referenceFilename` / `referenceImage` (singular) from parser output (`apps/runtime/.../runtime-image-edit-tool.service.ts` — `ResolvedImageEditSelection`, parser output, worker selection shape, all 13 tool-result composition sites, plus the rehydrate fallback `(request.referenceImageAlias === null ? [] : [request.referenceImageAlias])` that bridged legacy single → plural), from `RuntimeImageEditRequest` / `RuntimeImageEditToolResult` / `ProviderGatewayImageEditRequest` (`packages/runtime-contract/src/index.ts` — now plural-only `string[] | null` required), from the OpenAI image-edit client + the image-generation service normalize path (`apps/provider-gateway/.../openai-provider.client.ts`, `provider-image-generation.service.ts` — both used the singular as a fallback for the plural array). Adjacent hardening: `invalid_arguments` for image jobs now non-retryable (new `NON_RETRYABLE_IMAGE_REASONS` set in `runtime-media-job-run.service.ts` mirroring the existing video pattern, plus six other model-correctable image reasons) — surfaces as terminal `BadRequestException` in seconds, no more 7.5-min retry theatre for any deterministic image failure. Regression guards added: `runtime-media-request-parsing.test.ts` now has a `persisted RuntimeImageEditRequest passes worker rehydrate parse` round-trip test (parse model args → simulate enqueue → re-parse rehydrated shape) that would have caught this in CI; `runtime-media-job-run.service.test.ts` has a `treats invalid_arguments image jobs as non-retryable bad requests` test asserting `BadRequestException` with the reason + message preserved; `turn-execution.service.test.ts` now contains explicit absent-key assertions (`referenceImageAlias === undefined`, `referenceFilename === undefined`) so a future reintroduction can't slip past. All affected tests updated to the plural-only shape (8 test files total). Gate green: format + lint + 4-package typecheck + runtime/provider-gateway/api affected test suites all pass. **Out of scope (separate fixes):** `messageToUser` honesty gap (`"Accepted... being prepared"` emitted at enqueue, before the worker actually accepts the job — model can't tell from the tool result alone that a downstream worker failure happened); separate Prisma `runtimeSession.upsert ... value too long for the column's type` regression visible in the same log window.

- **ADR-118 opened (Skill scenarios + model-owned activation):** new open program ADR `docs/ADR/118-skill-scenarios-and-model-owned-activation.md` running in parallel to ADR-117 (does not block, does not supersede). Replaces the hidden Skill activation stack (`SkillStateRoutingService` background classifier + `matchesSkillLexically` foreground substring-gate + cadence intervals `initialCheck=3` / `recheck=5`) with **model-owned activation via a single `skill({ engage | release })` tool**, and adds a **new first-class product concept** — admin-authored `SkillScenario` — so Skills can carry reusable structured workflows like "Instagram-карусель: 8 slides via image_generate series". Three-level engagement (Enabled → Active → Running scenario), single discriminated-union tool, scenario steps injected via existing `cacheRole: "volatile_context"` pattern (cached system prefix stays byte-stable across engage/release), and quiet UX indicator as inline annotation **in the `:::working` block header row, to the right of the `Выполнено ▾` toggle** (Skill name + optional `· Scenario`; nothing when no active Skill; not a line inside the block body). - **HOTFIX — `@persai/runtime-contract` startup crash (ADR-117 Slice 3 regression):** the prior push (`260837c2`) crash-looped the new `api`/`runtime` rollout pods with `ERR_MODULE_NOT_FOUND` resolving `./media-prompt-fragments` imported from `runtime-contract/src/index.ts`. Root cause: the contract package is consumed as **un-built TypeScript source** (`main` → `src/index.ts`, no build step), and Slice 3's `export … from "./media-prompt-fragments"` was the first relative import — Node 22's type-stripping ESM loader cannot resolve an extensionless relative specifier, `.ts` extension fails the emit typecheck (TS5097), and no `.js` sibling exists. Fix: inlined the provider-conditioning fragments (`ANTI_COLLAGE_RULE`, `STANDALONE_*`, `referenceGuidanceRule`, `seriesItemHeaderLine`) directly into `packages/runtime-contract/src/index.ts` and deleted the sibling file, restoring the single self-contained module. No consumer imports changed (all import from `@persai/runtime-contract`); the ADR-117 golden single-source test now anchors on `index.ts`; `API-BOUNDARY.md` / `ARCHITECTURE.md` / `TEST-PLAN.md` / ADR-117 closure updated. Provider output and model-facing text unchanged. Gate green: runtime-contract typecheck + **api emit build** + runtime/gateway typecheck + lint + golden single-source/projection tests.

Single-reference prompt wording preserved verbatim for backward compatibility.
- **Web stream silent-cut fix (cadence watchdog):** once any native tool starts in a stream span, the `slow_avg` cadence signal is now disabled for the rest of that span (`apps/api/.../cadence-watchdog.ts`). Root cause from `persai-dev` logs (`alex@agse.ru`, turn `c8c44383`): on media turns the model streams a short post-tool wrap-up answer slower than the 200 ms/token threshold, `slow_avg` fired and aborted the runtime fetch with **no error**; because tool side-effects make the turn unsafe to retry, the reply was left truncated and the user had to re-ask. Mirrors the silent-timer philosophy already documented for `recordToolFinished` (slow post-tool answers are the job of provider/runtime stream timeouts). Pure-text-turn `slow_avg` behavior is unchanged.
- **Media `prompt` optional in series mode (image_edit + image_generate):** when `outputMode="series"` carries non-empty `seriesItems`, a missing top-level `prompt` is no longer rejected as `invalid_arguments` (which silently skipped the whole media request and produced no job). The parser now synthesizes an overall prompt; non-series calls still require `prompt`. Same `persai-dev` incident: the carousel `image_edit` call shipped 4 `seriesItems` and no `prompt`, so the job was never enqueued. Added `requestId`-tagged `skipped` warn logs to the previously silent `invalid_arguments` / selection branches for future diagnosis.

## 2026-06-14

- **Current-message attachment ordinals:** multi-attach composer shows ephemeral 1/2/3 watermarks on pending thumbnails; runtime labels direct-input image/PDF blocks as `Current message attachment N of M` (separate from Working Files `image #N` aliases).

- **ADR-116 Slice 116.1 (read hardening):** `files.read` on PDF/DOCX now surfaces `charCount`, `extractionQuality`, `readNote`, `extractionCached`; sanitizer sets `truncated` + `charCount` when clipping to 16k; internal extract API returns `cached: true` on metadata cache hits.
- **Doc hygiene — program closure:** retired stale “active program” references to ADR-078 / ADR-102 across `AGENTS.md`, `ARCHITECTURE.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `DATA-MODEL.md`, `SESSION-HANDOFF.md`, and cursor rules. All orchestration programs through ADR-115 are closed archive; new work requires explicit user priority + new ADR.
- **Media job completion framing:** plan-level `mediaCompletionVisionEnabled` toggles vision review on the existing `/media-jobs/complete` LLM call for `image_generate` / `image_edit` (up to 10 hydrated images, required non-empty reply). Cheap plans stay text-only but prompts now require a real delivery reply instead of optional silence + hardcoded «Медиафайл отправлен.» / `Media sent.`
- **Media completion follow-up:** vision input limited to job output images only; completion max output tokens raised to 1000; `seriesItems` must be unique per frame in image tool projection.
