## 2026-06-13

- CI test fix + final UI polish follow-up: investigated the failed post-push GitHub Actions `CI` run and traced it to two brittle `ImageLightbox` native-inline expectations that depended on jsdom image/canvas behavior rather than the intended product contract. The lightbox tests now explicitly simulate a loaded image + canvas extraction path before asserting inline native transfer, which restores deterministic full-suite CI coverage without changing runtime behavior. The same commit also includes the remaining founder-requested web polish still pending in the tree: tighter responsive integrations cards and calmer shared pill-button shadows.
- Legacy `mediaClasses` cleanup: removed the dead plan-entitlement `mediaClasses` dimension from the active API/domain/persistence path and dropped `plan_catalog_entitlements.media_classes` via Prisma migration. Effective capability/routing/enforcement truth now derives from `toolClasses`, `channelsAndSurfaces`, tool activations, and quota state instead of a stale parallel media-class layer. Admin plan parsing/state, plan catalog persistence, and model-visible assistant knowledge no longer round-trip or expose `mediaClasses`, which removes the false "image/audio/video/file disabled" signal the model previously saw even when media tools were active.

## 2026-06-12

- Mobile bridge binding fix + APK refresh: `ImageLightbox` native save/share now invokes `window.PersaiNative` methods with the native bridge object as the call context instead of detaching the function first, which keeps Android `addJavascriptInterface` calls on the real native object and stops the WebView from falling through to the dead `blob:` browser path. Added focused regression coverage for the binding contract, rebuilt/exported the Android APK again, and re-ran the full AGENTS verification gate plus full monorepo tests before push.
- Media auth path + APK refresh: the same-origin `assistant-file` BFF now accepts a fresh `X-PersAI-Session-Token` like the other protected web BFF routes, chat inline image previews now use the authenticated blob loader instead of a raw protected `<img>` URL, lightbox transfer fetches/native payloads now carry the same fresh session token, Android/iOS native media transfer forwards that header alongside cookies, and the Android APK artifact was rebuilt/exported again. This closes the auth seam that reproduced in Chrome/Capacitor but not in Cursor browser and also stabilizes native save/share against `/api/assistant-file/...`.
- HeyGen voice curation follow-up: the Admin Tools `Model` checkbox now implies `approved + enabled` instead of silently saving a contradictory state that disappears after refresh, and the private-imported HeyGen catalog path now enriches missing preview URLs from the legacy `/v2/voices` response when `/v3/voices?type=private` omits them.
- Post-interruption UI/API fixpack: Admin HeyGen `Edit voices` curation routes now pass through Clerk auth middleware and surface load failures honestly, legacy raw HeyGen voice cache rows can still populate the curation table, home recent chats show smart/project icons plus a soft active-work dot and preview text while the redundant Telegram quick action is gone, the expanded sidebar account footer has safer top spacing, assistant-file downloads prefer canonical file MIME over storage `octet-stream`, chat history falls through to canonical `assistant_files.metadata.mediaDerivatives` when attachment metadata is stale so thumbnails/posters do not unnecessarily fall back to full-size media, and the Android APK artifact was rebuilt from the fixed `persai-mobile` shell.
- Full repo founder verification fixpack: the current wide working tree was brought back to a green AGENTS gate before commit/push. Web chat soft-detach/reattach continuity now carries a distinct `terminal_status` path so the new stream reconciliation stays type-safe, and stale API HeyGen test doubles were updated to the approved-catalog contract (`getApprovedVoiceCatalogEntries`) so the full monorepo test suite passes again on the combined founder web/API/mobile tree.
- Admin HeyGen voice approval landed for talking-avatar voices: Admin Tools now has an `Edit voices` table beside `Refresh voices` where operators can search/filter all cached public/private HeyGen voices, preview audio, approve/enable voices, correct `RU` / `EN` / `Other` / `Multi` language and gender, and separately mark approved voices as model-selectable. Manual curation is stored in `platform_heygen_voice_curation` and is not overwritten by provider refresh; user-facing Characters catalogs now expose only approved + enabled voices, while model-facing talking-avatar shortlists additionally require the model checkbox.
- Fixpack: completed chat working notes now keep their `:::working` structure across final/history/status/reattach reconciliation, remove duplicated working text from the final answer, and render as a quiet collapsed `Done` / `Выполнено` disclosure after completion while streaming notes use a single left-rail style. Admin Tools now reads HeyGen voice catalog metadata from the active `heygen-voices-avatar-v` cache key, and the HeyGen refresh path now includes imported `type=private` voices, classifies them as ElevenLabs-quality entries, and projects unknown-language private imports into RU/EN via multilingual handling so imported voices can appear in the Characters picker/model shortlist.
- Chat media derivatives landed as additive file/runtime truth: canonical chat media now stays on full/master `fileRef`, while image `thumbnail` and video `poster` refs can be generated asynchronously as hidden non-billable `assistant_files` system variants tracked in canonical file metadata and mirrored into attachment payloads. Web chat bubbles now prefer those lightweight refs when present but keep automatic legacy fallback to `fileRef`, and ordinary multimodal runtime image inputs now use an explicit transient resize path (about `2048px` max edge only when needed) while `image_edit` and media-tool reference images still use full/master bytes.
- Chat media gallery polish: image attachments that arrive as a small same-message set now open as one lightbox gallery. Mobile can swipe horizontally between images while keeping vertical swipe-to-close, and desktop gets quiet previous/next controls plus keyboard arrows. Video lightbox behavior is unchanged.
- HeyGen voice catalog quality hardening: the platform HeyGen voice cache now enriches each voice with derived source (`elevenlabs` / `heygen` / `gemini`), quality tags (`professional` / `natural` / `lifelike`), preview availability, locale/pause support, and a server-side quality rank. The model-facing 24-voice shortlist now prefers RU/EN ElevenLabs-backed voices, then high-quality HeyGen voices, then safe fallbacks instead of alphabetical filler. The Characters voice picker keeps the same RU/EN/OTHER/MY + gender filters, but sorts each bucket by quality, labels ElevenLabs/Pro/Natural/Lifelike voices inline, and does not offer broken static Gemini previews as playable.
- Chat working-text stream cleanup: assistant live "working" notes no longer rely on text regex heuristics to split progress markers from the final reply. Web chat now wraps already-streamed pre-tool prefixes into persisted `:::working` markdown blocks when the turn enters another tool/retrieval/project pass, renders those blocks as quieter working notes above the live/final answer, keeps the inline status beside the cursor alive even after the first visible answer text arrives, and removes the old progress-line normalization hack. Runtime project guidance was updated accordingly so visible working notes stay short/natural instead of newline/bullet-formatted for UI parsing.
- Founder setup polish tail: the recreate/setup flow is quieter and more human. The upload-avatar card no longer shows an extra bottom banner, the temporary recreate/recover explanation banner was removed from the user path, the `Shape the personality` / `Настрой характер` surfaces now use the same calmer card/input language as assistant settings in both themes, and recreate-confirmation copy now describes the reset in plain language instead of exposing programmer terms like `runtime bundles/specs` or `media artifacts`.
- Characters / HeyGen persona identity follow-up: workspace video personas now persist a fixed `videoFormat` (`16:9` / `9:16` / `1:1`) as part of avatar identity instead of treating talking-avatar aspect ratio as request-only truth. Persona creation now center-crops/normalizes the uploaded portrait to that stored format before HeyGen avatar creation, the Characters create modal exposes `Auto / 9:16 / 1:1 / 16:9` with auto-detect from source image dimensions, edit keeps avatar immutable and shows the stored format read-only, public/internal persona APIs now carry `videoFormat`, and runtime talking-avatar generation now resolves aspect ratio in the order `explicit request -> stored persona videoFormat -> provider/admin default`.

## 2026-06-11

- Founder UI polish tail follow-up: several last-mile web settings surfaces were normalized after live review. `Payment settings` and `Clone voice` now sit on the same compact pill baseline as the rest of the CTA system; the shared pill-button shadow was reduced to a calmer half-strength treatment; Files rows became truly one-line and compact by dropping the redundant origin/type subline for ordinary files while keeping only meaningful document-output chips (`Current`, `vN`); the Characters voice language selector now matches the Gender segmented control height/style; and the Memory drawer was tightened so tabs, search/add controls, row spacing, expand actions, and right-edge delete affordances read as one dense premium list instead of mixed ad hoc controls.
- Founder UI polish final follow-up: payment settings in assistant limits now stays quiet by default but escalates to a primary CTA only when billing truth indicates real attention/action (`grace/past_due`, auto-renew restore/off, scheduled change, recurring migration trouble, provider-managed recovery, or an explicit warning). The Knowledge base list no longer keeps reloading on incidental rerenders, gets a separate round manual status-refresh button beside `Upload documents`, and swaps the per-row reindex affordance away from the generic refresh glyph so indexing checks are less confusing. Locked `Characters` plans no longer show the demo avatar card at all; instead they show only the pricing gate copy (`Available on Plan Pro and above` / `Доступно на тарифе Pro и выше`) plus the clarified avatar-video explanation. The compact token progress bar inside the expanded sidebar account menu also had its track/background restored so it matches the fuller quota style again.
- CTA polish follow-up: shared primary/secondary pill buttons are now shorter and more unified across the user-facing web surfaces. The base pill height was reduced by about 18%, secondary pills were lightened a tone in both dark and light themes, and the local duplicate CTA styles in assistant settings and the home dashboard were collapsed back onto the shared button helper so pairs like `Сохранить / Настроить` read as one calmer system.
- Chat UI polish follow-up: normal and project chats no longer render separate activity banners inside the timeline. Live tool/project progress now appears only as one quieter inline status beside the streaming cursor in the active assistant bubble, with a brief left-to-right fade on appearance, and the terminal `Response ready` / `Ответ готов` banner path was removed so completion leaves no extra status pill after the answer.
- Web UI polish follow-up: the assistant-settings/sidebar cleanup now uses shared soft-outlined inputs and pill buttons across the touched user surfaces, keeps knowledge/files/support rows flatter and quieter, and localizes Telegram group-refresh feedback beside the `Refresh` control instead of rendering it as a page-level status block.
- Billing UI follow-up: recurring paid copy no longer says `Next`. Shared billing-summary resolution now renders ordinary active recurring states as `Charge {date}` / `Списание {date}`, while an already scheduled plan downgrade renders the future plan and switch date instead (`BASIC c 26 июн.` style) across the sidebar/account surfaces and payment/settings UI. The web bootstrap/app-data seam now includes billing-subscription management state so scheduled downgrade truth can be shown consistently outside the payment modal without guessing from plan visibility alone.
- Billing/quota truth correction: `grace_period` after an already-effective scheduled downgrade now keeps the downgraded current plan and its limits, but preserves the last paid subscription window as the quota period until `payment_recovered` / `renewal_succeeded`. `TrackWorkspaceQuotaUsageService` no longer rewrites grace reads back to the previous paid plan; it now uses the stored current plan for limits while still recovering the previous paid period boundaries from `previousPaidPlanCode` / matching lifecycle history so usage counters do not reset or open a new period early. `expired_fallback` still starts a new fallback period.
- UI follow-up: workspaces in `grace_period` / `past_due` now show a calm payment-issue badge in the three intended visible surfaces instead of leaking the token-budget light-mode badge there: the collapsed sidebar mini-profile, the expanded sidebar account card, and the settings payment/plan surfaces (current-plan summary plus payment-settings modal status area). The badge copy is localized as `Payment issue` / `Сбой оплаты`.
- ADR-114 is now closed for its decided scope after live operator validation. Reserve OpenAI-compatible transport for `image_generate` / `image_edit` is confirmed working end-to-end with the intended primary-then-reserve behavior; OpenAI video fallback remains explicitly out of scope and deferred pending separate compatibility proof and a future decision.
- Billing lifecycle fix: overdue provider-managed paid subscriptions no longer depend solely on a timely CloudPayments renewal webhook to leave stale `active` state. When PersAI reads an `active`/`past_due` paid row whose `currentPeriodEndsAt` is already in the past and the row still has `providerSubscriptionRef`, it now first reconciles against CloudPayments `subscriptions/get`: an `Active` provider subscription with an advanced `NextTransactionDateIso` self-heals through `recoverPayment()` (missed success webhook), while a `Cancelled` provider subscription self-heals through the normal canceled-period-end fallback. If provider reconciliation cannot prove the renewed period, the existing grace-start safety path remains the fallback so stale recurring rows do not keep infinite paid access.
- Billing lifecycle fix: effective subscription resolution now self-heals expired paid grace periods the same way it already self-heals expired trials. If a workspace subscription is still `grace_period` after `graceEndsAt`, the read path now attempts `expireGrace()`, reloads the row, and returns `expired_fallback`; if fallback application is misconfigured, it logs `expired_grace_fallback_skipped` and returns the stale row instead of breaking admin/runtime reads with a user-facing error.

## 2026-06-09

- ADR-114 forced-fallback hotfix: intentionally breaking the primary OpenAI image key with an `Incorrect API key` / `invalid_api_key` response now triggers reserve OpenAI-compatible image fallback instead of failing before ProxyAPI is tried. Live dev confirmed the failed job had reached provider-gateway and stopped on primary OpenAI `401`; provider-gateway classification now treats that account-access failure as reserve-eligible, with focused coverage for both `image_generate` and `image_edit`.
- ADR-114 live hotfix: enabling the reserve OpenAI-compatible media key no longer breaks the primary OpenAI image path during materialization. The internal runtime secret resolver now recognizes `tool/image_generate/reserve/api-key`, and a regression test locks that mapping so direct OpenAI image generation can continue before any reserve fallback is needed.
- ADR-114 Slice 1 implemented for OpenAI image generation/edit fallback only. `Admin > Tools` now carries reserve OpenAI-compatible media transport settings (enable, API key, base URL), materialization forwards the config to runtime/provider-gateway image refs, provider-gateway retries once on strict primary OpenAI transport/account availability failures, and successful reserve fallback logs plus emits the existing admin notification path. OpenAI video fallback remains deferred; billing/quota semantics stay on the existing OpenAI image path with no transport-only billing-facts metadata.
- ADR-114 replaced the withdrawn realtime live voice artifact and superseded fal draft with the active reserve OpenAI-compatible media transport program. Direct OpenAI media behavior, model selection, Admin Runtime, and Admin Plans stay unchanged; the only intended product surface is an `Admin > Tools` Media reserve block with enable boolean, reserve API key, and reserve base URL (default `https://api.proxyapi.ru/openai/v1`). Slice 1 is image generation/edit fallback only; OpenAI video fallback is deferred pending separate route compatibility proof. The ADR defines strict retry criteria, keeps reserve attribution in logs plus one existing-platform admin notification per successful fallback, avoids new billing-facts metadata solely for attribution, and keeps the orchestrator-run GPT-5.4 subagent execution model.
- Android/Capacitor video preview follow-up: real-device smoke on `com.persai.app` showed inline WebView video elements can paint Android's grey native play fallback even while the same file opens correctly in the video viewer. Chat video cards are now about 30% smaller and extract a real decoded frame into a canvas-backed thumbnail image; Android/native shells keep the inline `<video>` surface hidden while showing that true thumbnail and preserving click-to-play behavior.
- Chat media polish: web video attachment cards now use stable portrait/square/landscape preview presets, reveal the real inline video frame after frame data loads, and keep the same same-origin `/api/assistant-file/...` path used by desktop and Capacitor playback. Working Files prompt text also now separates PDF-only document anchors from the general chat-file list and exposes a general `LAST_DELIVERED_FILE` anchor.
- ADR-112 formally closed after the live video-tool follow-up: the ADR status now reflects Slices 1-10 complete, the stale "Slices 7-8 pending" wording is removed, and the handoff points the separate HeyGen VC catalog/settle residual to future API/accounting work rather than ADR-112.
- ADR-112 live video-tool follow-up: `video_generate` guidance now draws a hard boundary between ordinary/cinematic video and `talking_avatar`. Silent/no-speech/gesture/image-animation requests route to `mode="cinematic"`; `talking_avatar` is reserved for explicit spoken-avatar narration with non-empty `speechText`. Runtime validation errors for empty `speechText` now tell the model to use cinematic or ask for a real script, model-correctable async video failures (`invalid_arguments`, bad reference/portrait aliases, missing voice/persona/config) are non-retryable so jobs stop immediately instead of burning the retry window. Media/document worker attachment payloads now use Working Files sticky aliases as the single source of truth; the old separate recent-image/recent-document-source attachment resolvers (`last 6` / `last 4`) were removed from the runtime path instead of being kept as hidden fallback namespaces.
- ADR-112 Slice 8 completed in the working tree: background model-call prompt hygiene now has clearer names and classifications. Runtime bundles expose `promptDocuments.backgroundTaskEvaluation` while keeping legacy `heartbeat` as a compatibility alias; skill-state classifier calls now include `checkReason` in the prompt and use the `skill_state_classifier` provider classification; quota advisory evaluation is split from real background-task evaluation via `quota_advisory_evaluation`; and compaction-exhausted follow-ups no longer invoke the two-phase background-task evaluator, instead creating a bounded static notification intent from durable compaction facts after the existing suppression checks.
- ADR-112 Slice 7 completed in the working tree: background job visibility now splits runtime prompt truth into real in-progress jobs vs post-completion delivery updates. API/web continuity remains unchanged (`activeMediaJobs` and web document chips still keep `completion_pending` / `ready_for_delivery`), but runtime-facing `openMediaJobs` / `openDocumentJobs` now exclude those states and instead receive a compact internal `jobDeliveryUpdates[]` seam on `RuntimeTurnRequest`. Runtime renders one `## Job Delivery Updates` developer section that says generation/rendering is already finished, distinguishes `finalizing_delivery` from `delivered_recently`, prevents stale "still generating" replies during the delivery race, and explicitly closes the async audio lane: voice replies use synchronous `tts`, not background `audio_generate`.
- ADR-112 prompt-context follow-up: internal memory hydration now returns each memory row's existing `chatId`, and runtime renders slim source markers (`this chat` / `past chat`) in durable-memory labels only when the current chat can be compared. Past-chat memory blocks add one short instruction telling the model to use chat/context search for missing details rather than assuming the fact happened in the current conversation. Unresolved `open_loop` short memories no longer duplicate into the recent short-memory prompt block because the operational surface is `Open Loop Refs`. Telegram channel context is now the same centralized developer section for private and group Telegram turns, with a concise voice/audio hint when the inbound Telegram message includes audio and group-only privacy cautions kept only for groups. `Working Files` was slimmed by removing the format legend, compressing file-tool guidance, and suppressing historical audio/voice attachments from the default prompt surface. No database migration was needed.

## 2026-06-08

- ADR-112 Slice 9 completed in the stacked working tree: runtime model-facing tool descriptors/instructions were cleaned without changing execution architecture. `document` guidance now consistently uses `docId` and states it is UUID-only, `memory_write` no longer exposes ADR-id implementation cruft, `scheduled_action` projection is sanitized to user-visible reminders and no stale `assistant_check` hidden-follow-up copy, `background_task` no longer advertises a ghost `update` action, pending-delivery honesty copy is shared across image/video/document tools, video persona guidance consistently says `Settings -> Characters`, and `tts` now has one concise rule to call the tool for spoken replies/voice notes and not claim audio exists unless the same turn returns `action='generated'`. Focused projection/scheduled-action/TTS tests plus runtime lint/typecheck passed.
- ADR-112 Slice 5/6 independent audit follow-up: four read-only auditors reviewed runtime Working Files, media/document/file consumers, descriptors/docs, and test coverage. The real production residual was closed: image/video tool attachments now reuse Working Files sticky aliases instead of a second ephemeral `image #N`/`file #N` renumbering path; media tool result/log aliases prefer sticky labels; files-tool model-visible alias arrays keep sticky aliases first and drop legacy ordinal aliases; non-UUID `docId` values are nulled/logged instead of forwarding alias-like strings; `docId` tool projection is camelCase + UUID-only; and stale `RuntimeTurnResult.discoveredFileRefIds` / ADR-081 alias docs were corrected to the sticky Working Files truth.
- ADR-112 Slice 6 residual developer-block cleanup completed in the same stacked flow: the Working Files title/tool vocabulary alignment had already landed with Slice 5, and the remaining unused `showCurrentTurnImageOrdinals` / direct-attachment counter plumbing was removed from runtime hydration. Source audit confirms no active runtime turn assembly still emits `## File history` or carries the dead current-turn image ordinal path.
- ADR-112 Slice 5 completed in the working tree: runtime Working Files now uses stable sticky `file #N` / `image #N` handles instead of recomputed current/previous/found/listed/read aliases. The developer section is titled `## Working Files`, separates sticky labels from recency/role markers, keeps PDF-specific document anchors (`DOC_CURRENT_SOURCE` / `DOC_LAST_DELIVERED_PDF`) visible, and preserves same-name files with short-hash disambiguation. Hydration, tool-loop discovery merging, `files`, `document`, `image_edit`, `image_generate`, and native tool projection guidance now resolve/teach the sticky scheme; focused runtime tests plus runtime lint/typecheck passed.
- ADR-112 follow-up tightening on the Slice 10 auto-extractor: runtime `AutoExtractToMemoryService` now asks for at most `3` high-confidence items (or zero), rewrites the extraction prompt toward concise neutral evidence-backed notes, restricts `open_loop` to concrete unresolved follow-ups instead of vague ongoing interests/product direction, defaults ordinary open loops to `short`, and adds a small parser guard that skips obvious test-voice/demo/ephemeral summaries plus vague `open_loop` outputs, downgrades non-explicitly-durable `long` open loops to `short`, and skips numeric-confidence `long` fact/preference candidates below `0.85`. Focused runtime tests lock the prompt rules and parser behavior; no runtime/API contract shape changed.
- ADR-112 Slice 10 is now complete in the working tree: the model-facing `memory_write` contract uses a simple `layer` choice (`long` | `short`) instead of `durability` / `stability`, with deterministic routing `long -> core + identity/stable` and `short -> contextual + episodic/time_bound` on the API side; the raw `web_chat` post-turn memory writer is removed from the active path; contextual hydration is a bounded recent short-memory window instead of lexical pre-turn search; and runtime planning drops retrieved-knowledge memory items that would duplicate that already-rendered short-memory block. Anthropic now projects that volatile recent-memory block as app-provided `<persai_runtime_context><recent_short_memory>...` immediately before the real user request, while OpenAI keeps the provider-native `developer` item. The remaining follow-up also landed: `runtime_sessions` now carries an explicit `memoryExtractionWatermark`, compaction auto-extract advances that same watermark while processing only the unwatermarked compacted prefix, and a new API idle-session scheduler reuses the existing background-compaction queue to run one compact-model idle extraction pass only after `20` idle minutes and `>=10` new hydratable messages after the watermark. Idle/provider failures leave the watermark unchanged and are retry-bounded by the existing job scheduler; successful/no-item evaluations advance the watermark so the same message delta cannot be processed twice. Background queue dedupe now separates `compaction` and `idle_extract` lanes so an idle job cannot suppress a real compaction job.
- ADR-113 opened and Slice 1 (expressive delivery core) implemented: chat voice replies are now structured and controllable instead of flat tone steering. The `tts` worker tool drops the single `toneTag` argument and accepts structured expressive intent (`delivery`, `emotion`, `pace`, `intensity`, `pause`, `nonVerbal`); the runtime derives the legacy tone for Yandex/OpenAI baselines and forwards the structured intent to provider-gateway. A new safe, deterministic compiler turns that intent into a small conservative set of ElevenLabs `eleven_v3` audio tags (`[whispers]`, `[dramatic]`, `[excited]`, `[sad]`, `[curious]`, `[laughs]`/`[chuckles]`/`[sighs]`/`[clears throat]`, `[short pause]`/`[long pause]`) with conflict avoidance (whisper suppresses loud emotion/intensity), a hard 3-tag budget, and model-authored-tag stripping so the model can never inject raw tags through `text`. The ElevenLabs provider client now defaults the chat quality path to `model_id: "eleven_v3"` (honoring an explicit catalog `modelKey` override per ADR-110), prepends compiled tags, and sends conservative discrete-stability v3 voice settings; non-`eleven_v3` ElevenLabs models and non-ElevenLabs providers ignore v3 tags and keep prior tone-based behavior. The saved ElevenLabs `voiceId` and the existing media/job delivery flow are unchanged. Voice catalog v2 backend/cache and the premium picker UI are designed in ADR-113 as Slices 2-3.
- ADR-113 Slice 2 (voice catalog v2 backend/cache) implemented: ElevenLabs voices for the assistant voice settings are now served from a platform-wide read-through cache (`platform_elevenlabs_voice_catalog_cache`, new additive migration) via `ElevenLabsVoiceCatalogService` instead of a live per-request fetch. The cache refreshes lazily on a 24h TTL, upserts on a successful fetch, and serves the last known (stale) list with a warning if a refresh fails, so the settings UI stays responsive and rate-limit-safe. Entries are normalized with `gender`, `category`, `language` + a derived `languageBucket` (`ru`/`en`/`other`), and `previewUrl`. `GET assistant/voice/settings` keeps its existing fields and additively exposes per-entry `language`/`languageBucket`; `unavailable` is now only reported when the cache is empty and a live refresh fails. The premium picker UI remains Slice 3.
- ADR-113 Slice 3a (premium voice picker UI) implemented: the three plain voice dropdowns in assistant settings are replaced by a shared `VoicePicker` card component unified across ElevenLabs, Yandex, and OpenAI. It adds voice search, gender/language/category filter chips (each shown only when it discriminates), selectable cards, and ElevenLabs stock-preview playback (play/stop). ElevenLabs cards are sourced from the Slice 2 cached catalog (with `language`/`languageBucket`/`category`/`previewUrl`); Yandex/OpenAI cards come from their fixed enums. Honest loading/`not_configured`/`unavailable` states are surfaced inline, the saved per-provider voice still writes into `persai.assistantVoiceProfile.v1`, and the existing assistant-gender constraint on the selectable set is preserved. The `eleven_v3` test-phrase generation is split out as Slice 3b (needs metered backend synthesis).
- ADR-113 closed: Slice 3b (`eleven_v3` test-phrase synthesis) was dropped as unnecessary complexity. A paid on-the-fly preview synthesis (with its billing/quota and anti-abuse plumbing) is not justified for voice selection — the Slice 3a stock card preview covers "how does this voice sound", and real intonation is verified live by the assistant's actual voice notes in chat. TTS 2.0 ships on Slices 1 + 2 + 3a.
- ADR-113 voice picker follow-up: the ElevenLabs catalog refresh now uses the shared voice library (`/v1/shared-voices`) and stores a versioned cache key for a bounded picker set per `RU|EN|OTHER` bucket and assistant gender, mixed 50/50 from `featured` voices and locally popularity-ranked candidates (`cloned_by_count + liked_by_count`). The web picker was simplified to the intended premium list: ElevenLabs shows only `RU | EN | OTHER` plus voice name + preview play, while Yandex/OpenAI keep the same compact name + play surface without marketplace chips.
- ADR-113 admin voice curation follow-up: ElevenLabs now separates an expanded admin candidate catalog from the public picker list. Admin users can browse the larger cached candidate set, select a voice for their own assistant, mark voices as public/hidden, and flag broken demos; regular users only receive the admin-approved public voices (capped at 24 per language bucket + gender). The selected voice row now has an explicit check marker and ElevenLabs `voiceId` is no longer silently cleared by the settings filter before save/publish.
- ADR-113 fallback hotfix: Yandex SpeechKit v3 TTS now handles multi-JSON/NDJSON audio chunk responses instead of assuming a single JSON document, and OpenAI TTS rejects foreign provider model keys such as `eleven_multilingual_v2`, falling back to `gpt-4o-mini-tts` so fallback speech does not call OpenAI with an ElevenLabs model id.

## 2026-06-07

- ADR-111 closed as completed after live HeyGen voice-clone smoke and post-smoke repair. The completed program now records workspace-scoped cloned voices, VC-on-success debit, preset/cloned voice persona selection, runtime voice precedence, Characters/My voices UI, upload/record clone creation, mobile video preview/lightbox polish, Clerk route auth coverage, browser recording WAV conversion, and HeyGen `audio/x-wav` projection. Custom audio lip-sync, HeyGen Studio API, broad passthrough tuning, and chat TTS remain out of ADR-111 scope.
- ADR-112 Slice 4 completed in the working tree (held from push for the memory-block audit): safe assistant-scoped memory backfill now follows the established dangerous-admin two-phase pattern. API added `POST /api/v1/admin/memory-backfill/preview` (read-authorized dry-run) and `POST /api/v1/admin/memory-backfill/apply` (step-up required via new dangerous action `admin.memory_backfill.apply`). The backfill scans up to `1000` active rows for one assistant and reports/applies two exact cleanup rules only: legacy episodic `core` rows (`memoryClass = core` but not `identity + stable`) are reclassified to `contextual`, and trivial `web_chat` rows whose stored summary fails the durable-summary guardrail are soft-pruned with `forgottenAt` via `markForgottenById`. If a row matches both rules, prune wins. Repository support (`listActiveForBackfill`, guarded `reclassifyMemoryClassById`) and focused API tests landed, and OpenAPI was hand-edited minimally for the new endpoints/action without regenerating contracts.
- ADR-112 Slice 3 completed (two sub-slices, local commits only, held from push): durable-memory normalization + consolidation + lifecycle. 3a (`56613bff`) added nullable `superseded_at` / `superseded_by_memory_id` columns, a `markSupersededById` repository method, and `supersededAt: null` exclusion on every active memory read/hydration/search path so a superseded fact stops resurfacing while its audit row is retained. 3b (`8433dd6d`) added lazy memory embeddings (`embedding_vector` JSONB + `embedding_model_key` + `embedding_generated_at`, model key reused from the knowledge embedding policy) and a best-effort `ConsolidateAssistantMemoryService` that runs after each successful background compaction (reusing the existing scheduler lease/cadence, never failing the compaction job): it lazily embeds new memories, merges same-kind near-duplicates (cosine >= 0.92 -> supersede loser, survivor priority core > confidence > recency), and decay-prunes time_bound contextual rows idle for > 45 days. Unresolved open loops are never merged/pruned; identity/stable/core rows are never decay-pruned; with no embedding model available it skips merge and still runs decay. Mechanical cosine merge, not a positive classifier.
- ADR-112 Slice 2 completed: durable-memory retrieval/render quality. Runtime-facing hydration now drops trivially-non-durable contextual hits (reusing the Slice 1 negative guardrail, so legacy greeting/ack rows that pass the lexical exact-token floor no longer hydrate into the prompt) and de-duplicates contextual memories against core by normalized text (not just id), while preserving search relevance order. The per-turn contextual block is rendered as one volatile block under the existing header, deterministically grouped by kind (`Preferences -> Facts -> Open loops -> Other`), still flagged `cacheRole: "volatile_context"` and placed last in the prefix. A provider-gateway regression test now locks the ADR-110 invariant that a `volatile_context` block is re-projected as a non-cacheable `user` block before the current question and never carries `cache_control`; the core stable cache token is asserted invariant under contextual rotation. The earlier per-turn `cache_creation` worry was investigated directly against live `persai-dev` receipts (session `78ae7b44`) and confirmed resolved: post-deploy short Anthropic turns keep history cache reads growing with only tiny new-tail writes, versus pre-deploy turns that re-wrote a 3k-10.5k segment every turn.
- ADR-112 Slice 1 completed: `memory_write` and compaction auto-extract now require model-emitted `durability` (`identity|episodic`) and `stability` (`stable|time_bound`) with optional `confidence`; API persistence added nullable memory durability/stability/confidence columns plus semantic routing (`identity+stable -> core`, otherwise contextual, negative guardrails -> soft `not_durable` skip); trivial web-chat greeting/ack turns are no longer stored; and runtime `memory_write` guidance/schema/tests now reflect the tightened durable-memory contract.
- ADR-112 opened as an orchestrator-run quality program for context, memory, and the tool surface. Grounded in five read-only GPT-5.4 audits (durable memory, prompt/developer assembly, file aliases, background jobs/turns, tool descriptors), it defines seven workstreams (A memory formation, B prompt/block formation, C developer block + file/media, D sticky file aliases, E background jobs visibility, F background model-call prompt hygiene, G tool descriptor/instruction hygiene) and a 10-slice subagent-coded backlog. Memory formation is decided by model judgment with embedding dedup, periodic consolidation, and lifecycle/supersession - heuristics only as a guardrail, never the deciding layer. The parent agent orchestrates and audits; GPT-5.4 subagents implement.
- ADR-111 post-smoke UX/video cleanup: mobile chat video previews now use a deterministic premium play card with metadata-driven aspect geometry instead of a forced `16:9` frame, the video lightbox chrome can be recovered by tapping the playing video, the locked demo character prefers a female localized voice, talking-avatar generation no longer lets a generic hard landscape `16:9` default win when no explicit aspect is requested and defers that case to provider `auto`, and cloned-voice cards/modal copy are quieter.
- Prompt-cache discipline (PROD): the per-turn `durable_memory_contextual` block is now repositioned out of the cached prompt prefix in both providers via a typed contract flag instead of fragile header string-matching. `ProviderGatewayTextMessage` gained `cacheRole?: "volatile_context"`, which the runtime sets when it hydrates relevance-retrieved contextual memory. Live `persai-dev` Anthropic receipts showed that contextual memory is intentionally query-dependent and was sitting before conversation history, so every Anthropic history breakpoint included a changing prefix and rewrote roughly `10.5k` cache-creation tokens on short turns. Both provider clients now detect the flagged block, drop it from the cacheable prefix, and re-project it as a `user` block immediately before the current user question (symmetric Anthropic/OpenAI schema) so the question keeps the highest recency while the stable system/tools cache and Anthropic moving-history breakpoint stay hot. OpenAI per-turn developer instructions remain a provider-native trailing `developer` suffix.
- ADR-111 post-audit cleanup completed: cloned-voice recording now ignores stale microphone permission resolutions and duplicate starts, clone/persona preview blob URLs are revoked on replace/close, failed cloned-voice rows count toward the UI limit gate to match API active-row truth, and archiving a cloned voice best-effort marks workspace assistants config-dirty so materialized persona guidance refreshes.
- ADR-111 Slice 5 implementation completed: Settings -> Characters now includes a compact `My voices` subsection, cloned-voice upload/record modal with visible quality and rights guidance, ready-only cloned-voice persona selection, inline clone-and-attach flow, cloned-voice API client helpers, and runtime persona guidance that surfaces only safe cloned-voice labels from materialized catalog truth. Cross-docs now record the cloned-voice API/data/test boundaries. Local focused checks and full verification passed; authenticated live dev smoke remains outstanding because no signed-in dev session/local app was available.
- ADR-111 Slice 4b completed: personas can now link a workspace cloned voice through `clonedVoiceId` while retaining preset HeyGen fallback fields. API create/update validates linked cloned voices as same-workspace, active, ready, and provider-backed; internal runtime reads expose usable clone metadata; materialized persona catalogs keep provider ids out of user/model-facing labels; and talking-avatar voice resolution now follows explicit `voiceKey` -> linked cloned voice -> preset persona voice.
- ADR-111 Slice 4a completed: provider-gateway now submits/polls HeyGen voice clones with exact `complete` success semantics and stable clone-limit/plan-upgrade/auth/rate-limit error mapping. API now exposes workspace-scoped cloned voice create/list/archive/set-default endpoints, validates multipart audio uploads, enforces clone limits and duplicate names, marks failed clone attempts without debit, and debits VC once through `voice_clone_creation` only after a clone is marked ready.
- ADR-111 Slice 4 was split after the first GPT-5.4 implementation pass identified missing persona linked-clone substrate for the runtime precedence rule. Execution now proceeds as 4a provider-gateway/API cloned-voice CRUD + successful-completion VC debit, then 4b persona linked-clone substrate + runtime resolve.
- ADR-111 Slice 3 completed: API substrate now includes workspace-scoped `workspace_video_cloned_voices` persistence with Prisma migration, repository port/adapter, platform settings for cloned voice workspace limit and VC creation cost (`5` / `50` defaults, hard cap `10` for limit), and the typed VC ledger discriminator `voice_clone_creation`. No HeyGen HTTP call, REST endpoint, runtime resolve change, wallet debit, or web UI was added.
- ADR-111 Slice 2 completed: Characters now use a compact premium responsive grid with shared card geometry for unlocked personas, locked saved personas, and the locked demo record. The create action is a compact grid slot that disables for plan/limit gating without opening the modal, locked cards expose no edit/delete/portrait actions, and voice labels now use `Voice - ...` / `Голос - ...` copy.
- ADR-111 Slice 1 completed: inline chat video previews now render a deterministic compact play placeholder instead of depending on Android WebView decoding the first frame, while preserving metadata duration and click-to-lightbox behavior. The video lightbox hero play overlay now disappears once playback starts instead of staying mounted when chrome is visible, video chrome auto-hides after playback and returns on tap, and the same-origin assistant-file BFF is regression-covered for Capacitor-relevant `Range`/validator passthrough plus upstream `206`, `Content-Range`, `Accept-Ranges`, `Content-Length`, and `Content-Type: video/mp4` preservation. No API or `persai-mobile` change was needed.

## 2026-06-06

- History compaction: `docs/CHANGELOG.md` now keeps only current entries and concise recent summaries. Detailed 2026-06-05-and-earlier entries moved to `docs/CHANGELOG.archive-2026-06-05-details-and-earlier.md`; older pre-existing archive remains unchanged.
- ADR-103/104/106/107 closure sweep: old non-active tails are now explicitly closed. ADR-103 keeps the stubbed interactive landing demo as completed scope and cancels/defer-indefinitely the public unauthenticated LLM demo endpoint; ADR-104 keeps D1/D2 as completed deploy-resilience scope and cancels/defer-indefinitely the auto-mutating drift-repair cron while leaving prod atomicity as a future design note; ADR-106 is marked completed; ADR-107 is marked closed as a partial program with its existing Program closure as source of truth.
- ADR-110 closed as completed after operator verification. The active execution order is finished: embedding truth moved to `Admin > Knowledge`, runtime text failover and retrieval-helper fallback execute on the native path, TTS model truth no longer depends on the old OpenAI hardcode, and Anthropic prompt-cache/accounting landed with the later stream-accounting hotfix. Deferred STT/web-search provider-model work stays out of ADR-110 and should return only as a separate future ADR/slice if product priority requires it.
- ADR-110 Anthropic stream-accounting hotfix: provider-gateway no longer double-counts Anthropic streaming usage by summing `message_start` and `message_delta` token snapshots as if they were additive deltas. Later stream usage payloads now replace earlier fields instead of accumulating them, which brings PersAI's Anthropic ledger/session token counts back in line with Anthropic's own logs and prevents false context-pressure / compaction signals on short chats.
- ADR-109 closed as completed after operator verification. The HeyGen talking-avatar foundation is accepted as done; remaining voice cloning, Characters UI v2, and video-player polish work is explicitly owned by ADR-111 and must not reopen ADR-109.
- ADR-111 opened as the orchestrator-run program for HeyGen voice cloning and Characters UX v2. It keeps ADR-109 closed, supersedes only ADR-109's deferred voice-cloning non-goal, excludes custom audio lip-sync / broad HeyGen passthrough tuning, and defines a 5-slice GPT-5.4 subagent execution plan covering video-player polish, premium Characters UI cleanup, cloned-voice substrate, HeyGen voice-clone backend/runtime wiring, voice-clone UI, docs, and live smoke.
- ADR-110 Anthropic prompt-cache fix: runtime now passes prompt-cache intent to Anthropic text calls instead of limiting prompt caching to OpenAI-only requests. Anthropic provider-gateway already projects that intent as `cache_control: { type: "ephemeral" }` on the stable system block, so live Claude calls can now produce `cacheCreationInputTokens` / `cachedInputTokens` in usage instead of always recording zero cache usage.
- ADR-110 live hotfix: Admin Runtime settings now tolerate persisted token-metered catalog rows created before `cacheCreationInputPer1M` existed by defaulting the missing cache-write price to `0` during normalization. The dev cluster's persisted runtime catalog was patched in place so existing OpenAI/Anthropic/image/video rows no longer break Admin Runtime reads or materialization rollouts.
- Billing lifecycle fix: CloudPayments recurrent `check` webhooks can now resolve an existing PersAI subscription by `SubscriptionId`/`AccountId` even when there is no local renewal payment intent, so provider retries are not rejected as an unknown payment intent. Manually/admin-activated paid subscriptions with no provider subscription reference now enter the same `active -> grace_period -> expired_fallback` lifecycle when their paid period expires, preserving the standard grace notifications, materialization rollout, and fallback behavior.
- ADR-110 Slice 4: Anthropic prompt cache is now provider-specific and economically honest. The Anthropic provider client keeps the stable `systemPrompt` cacheable via `cache_control: { type: "ephemeral" }` only when prompt caching is enabled, leaves volatile `developerInstructions` as an uncached suffix system block, and never emits a literal `developer` role to Anthropic. Usage/accounting now has a separate `cacheCreationInputTokens` bucket in addition to normal `inputTokens`, cache-read `cachedInputTokens`, and `outputTokens`; token pricing metadata adds `cacheCreationInputPer1M`, with Anthropic cache writes priced separately from ordinary input and cache reads in both quota weighting and the cost ledger.
- ADR-110 Slice 3: TTS keeps its existing runtime provider-chain fallback, but OpenAI TTS model truth is no longer hardcoded on the execution path. The API now materializes the OpenAI `text_to_speech` catalog entry onto the TTS credential ref, runtime/provider-gateway forward that `modelKey`, and OpenAI speech billing facts now reflect the actual successful model from the catalog-driven path. Yandex `speechkit-v3` remains intentional code-owned API-version truth in the active TTS path.
- ADR-110 scope correction: STT and web-search provider/model truth are deferred out of the active ADR-110 execution order because they are not current production blockers and need a later full vertical contract/runtime/provider-gateway/UI/test slice. The next active ADR-110 slice is now TTS model/default truth cleanup.
- ADR-110 Slice 2: runtime text failover now executes on the active runtime path for eligible text-model failures instead of stopping at the primary provider/model. `apps/runtime` now performs one-shot fallback for ordinary turn text calls plus router/background system-tool calls when the primary text request fails with timeout/5xx-style provider execution errors, and logs primary failure plus fallback success/failure explicitly. The API knowledge rerank helper keeps `retrievalModelKey = null` as graceful-off, but when configured it now retries once onto the runtime fallback provider/model for the same retryable helper failures. Embedding fallback, generated media, STT, TTS, and web-search behavior were left unchanged in this slice.
- ADR-110 Slice 1: embedding model truth moved out of Plans and into `Admin > Knowledge`. Plan payloads/contracts/UI no longer write `embeddingModelKey`; assistant-owned knowledge now resolves embedding/index/search model choice from `adminKnowledgeRetrievalPolicy`, preserving lexical graceful-off when admin embedding is unset or same-model embedding generation fails. Admin Knowledge policy updates now expose embedding-change impact (`affectedSourceCount`, chunks, bytes, by-source breakdown), require dangerous-action step-up confirmation when the embedding model changes, and enqueue backfill across all Admin Knowledge-governed sources: global uploaded Product KB, Product KB text entries, Skill documents, Skill knowledge cards, and assistant-uploaded knowledge. OpenAPI/generated contracts, admin-web tests, and focused API tests were updated to match the new source of truth.
- ADR-109 live delivery hotfix: three recent talking-avatar jobs in `persai-dev` were proven complete on HeyGen, but chat delivery still hung because HeyGen sometimes serves the finished `.mp4` with `Content-Type: binary/octet-stream`. The provider-gateway now normalizes empty / octet-stream HeyGen video downloads back to a real video MIME based on the download URL suffix (defaulting `.mp4` to `video/mp4`), so runtime no longer rejects completed HeyGen renders as “unsupported MIME type”.
- ADR-109 Characters edit flow: saved persona cards now open the same shared modal in `Edit` mode, but avatar replacement is intentionally forbidden there. Operators can update only the persona name and voice, preview the existing portrait in a larger view, and see a quiet hint that changing the face requires creating a new character. The API now exposes a bounded `PATCH /api/v1/workspaces/:workspaceId/video-personas/:personaId` path that updates only `displayName + heygenVoiceId`, preserving the existing `heygenAvatarId` and portrait identity instead of mutating HeyGen avatar state in place.
- ADR-109 live voice-catalog hotfix: HeyGen `GET /v3/voices` uses the opaque `next_token` response field, but the follow-up request must send it back as query parameter `token` per the official docs. The previous refresh path incorrectly sent `next_token=...`, and live dev verification from the `api` pod proved HeyGen kept returning the same first 20 EN voices with an unchanged cursor. The cache refresh now uses `token=...`, requests up to `100` rows per page, and stops early if HeyGen repeats the same cursor to avoid looping on a broken upstream page stream.
- ADR-109 live hotfix: fixed the Admin HeyGen voice refresh route so it goes through Clerk auth like the other admin tool-credentials endpoints; the live dev cluster root cause was a real `401 userId=null` on `POST /api/v1/admin/runtime/tool-credentials/heygen-voice-catalog/refresh`, which meant the spinner ran but the cache never refreshed.
- ADR-109 Admin Tools voice refresh feedback now shows `Last refresh ... · N voices` and a concrete post-refresh status like `Updated: 300 voices.` instead of a spinner-only transition with no visible outcome.
- ADR-109 HeyGen voice catalog truth-hardening: the shared HeyGen cache now follows provider pagination and stores the full deduped catalog, while runtime still materializes a short prompt-safe talking-avatar shortlist (`10 EN + 10 RU` target, balanced by gender as available) for model-facing instructions.
- ADR-109 Admin Tools now exposes a manual HeyGen voice refresh action with a visible last-refresh timestamp, so operators can force a catalog sync without waiting for the 24h cache TTL.
- ADR-109 Characters voice picker now reads the full HeyGen catalog instead of the model shortlist, and the `OTHER` bucket adds inline language search so non-EN/RU voices are browseable/listenable without bloating the runtime prompt.
- ADR-109 Characters UI polish: locked plans now show a single premium demo character with the provided demo portrait, a real voice preview, and a direct `https://persai.dev/app/pricing` upsell link; unlocked plans hide the demo card, move `Create character` below the saved list, add a quiet usage hint, and open saved portraits in a lightbox on click.
- ADR-109 voice-picker cleanup: fixed the RU/EN regression by normalizing human-readable HeyGen language labels like `English` / `Russian` into the same `en` / `ru` buckets used by the filter, and removed the nested-button markup in the create-persona voice list so the voice preview control no longer emits invalid HTML hydration warnings in tests.
- ADR-109 root-cause fix (saved-persona render): persona create/archive now best-effort mark workspace assistants `configDirtyAt` so the materialized spec re-builds and the model actually sees saved characters with their real `personaId` (previously the model saw an empty `videoPersonaCatalog`, told users "no saved characters", and improvised `personaId="alexey"` from the display name); and the persona repository `findById`/`archive` now guard against non-UUID ids and resolve to `null` (honest `persona_not_found`) instead of letting Prisma throw a raw "Error creating UUID" — that raw DB error was the cause of the "UUID error" the model paraphrased on saved-persona renders.
- ADR-109 fix (10-minute banner on a permanent error): the async media-job worker `assertVideoToolResultAccepted` threw `503 ServiceUnavailable` (retryable) for every `isError` video reason except `requested_mode_unsupported`, so permanent talking-avatar config/input failures (`persona_not_found`, `talking_avatar_persona_unavailable`, `talking_avatar_provider_unavailable`, `talking_avatar_plan_disabled`, `voice_not_found`, `voice_required`) were retried through the exponential-backoff budget (30s→60s→120s→240s→480s) for ~10–15 min before the banner cleared. These reasons are now classified non-retryable `400` and fail fast; genuinely transient reasons keep their `503`/retry budget.

## 2026-06-05

- ADR-109 follow-up fixpack: made saved persona portraits actually load through a same-origin authenticated proxy path, improved the HeyGen voice shortlist so `ru` and `en` both survive shortlist materialization, added a `RU | EN` filter in the Characters create-persona form, clarified that cinematic `voice_control` shortlist entries are not for talking-avatar voice selection, and changed large HeyGen video delivery so files over the `100MB` inline ceiling fall back to a direct download link instead of failing the job.
- ADR-109 follow-up fixpack: fixed workspace voice catalog auth to resolve membership canonically, accepted HeyGen fractional-duration responses in runtime, whitelisted HeyGen in scheduler recovery, and added `talkingAvatarAspectRatio` as a talking-avatar-only user/model intent field that overrides aspect only when the HeyGen admin row is set to `auto`.
